 namaḥ buddhāya parokṣa artha pratipatteḥ anumāna āśraya tvāt tad vyutpādana artham saṃkṣepata idam ārabhyate pakṣa dharmas tad aṃśena vyāptaḥ hetuḥ tridhā eva saḥ avinā abhau niyamāt hetvābhāsāḥ tatas apare pakṣaḥ dharmī avayave samudāya aupacārāt prayojanaa bhāvāt anupacāra iti ced na sarva dharmi dharma pratiṣedha artha tvāt upacārasya evam hi cākṣuṣatva ādi parihṛtam bhavati dharma vacanena api dharmasya para āśraya tvāt dharmya āśraya siddhau dharmi grahaṇāt pratyāsatteḥ sādhya dharmi siddhiḥ iti ced na dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇaḥ api pratyāsatteḥ tad aṃśa vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattva siddheḥ dharmi vacanāt sādhya dharmi parigrahaḥ siddhe api punarvacanam niyama artham āśaṅkyeta sajātīya eva sattvam iti siddhe api tad abhāve vyatireke sādhyaa bhāve asattva vacanavat tad aṃśa vyāpti vacanāt siddhe api dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi sattve dharmi vacanam tatra eva bhāva niyama artham āśaṅkyeta tasmāt sāmarthyāt artha gatau api upacāra mātrāt samāna nirdeśāt pratipatti gauravam ca parihṛtam bhavati pakṣasya dharma tve tad viśeṣaṇa apekṣasya anyatra ananuvṛtteḥ asādhāraṇa tā iti ced na ayoga vyavacchedena viśeṣaṇāt yathā caitraḥ dhanurdhara iti na anya yoga vyavacchedena yathā pārthaḥ dhanurdhara iti tad aṃśas tad dharmaḥ vyāptiḥ vyāpakasya tatra bhāva eva vyāpyasya vā tatra eva bhāvaḥ etena anvayaḥ vyatirekaḥ vā pakṣa dharmaḥ ca yathāsvam pramāṇena niścita uktaḥ sarvatra hetau sādhya dharmaa bhāve vyāptya siddheḥ vyāpaka nivṛttau vā vyatirekaa bhāvāt anvaya vyatirekābhyām niścitābhyām tad aṃśa vyāptiḥ niścitā tatra pakṣa dharmasya sādhya dharmiṇi pratyakṣataḥ anumānataḥ vā prasiddhiḥ niścayaḥ yathā pradeśe dhūmasya śabde vā kṛtaka tvasya sa dhūmam hi pradeśam artha antara vivikta rūpam asādhāraṇa ātmanā dṛṣṭavataḥ pratyakṣeṇa yathā dṛṣṭa bheda viṣayam smārtam liṅga vijñānam utpadyate tatra yad ādyam asādhāraṇa viṣayam darśanam tad eva pramāṇam tasmin tathābhūte dṛṣṭe sati sa yena yena asādhāraṇas tad asādhāraṇa tām tatas bhedam abhilapanti atad vyāvṛtti viṣayā smṛtiḥ utpannā pratyakṣa balena yathā dṛṣṭa ākāra grahaṇān na pramāṇam prāk asādhāraṇam dṛṣṭvā asādhāraṇa iti abhilapataḥ apūrva artha adhigamaa bhāvāt artha kriyā sādhanasya darśanāt adṛṣṭasya punar tad sādhana svabhāvasya vikalpena apratipatteḥ ca anumānavat artha kriyā arthī hi sarvaḥ pramāṇam apramāṇam vā anveṣate prekṣāvān na ca sāmānyam kāṃcid arthakriyām upakalpayati sva lakṣaṇa pratipatteḥ ūrdhvam tad sāmarthya autpanna vikalpa vijñāna grāhyam yathā nīlam dṛṣṭvā nīlam iti jñāne tad eva hi nīla sva lakṣaṇam tathāvidha sādhya artha kriyā kāri tad ca tena ātmanā dṛṣṭam eva pratyakṣeṇa na ca tad sva lakṣaṇa grahaṇa auttara kāla bhāvi nīla vikalpasya viṣayeṇa nīla artha sādhya artha kriyā kriyate tasmāt anadhigata artha viṣayam pramāṇam iti api anadhigate sva lakṣaṇa iti viśeṣanīyam adhigate tu sva lakṣaṇe tad sāmarthya janmā vikalpaḥ tad anukārī kāryatas tad viṣaya tvāt smṛtiḥ eva na pramāṇam anadhigata vastu rūpaa nadhi gateḥ vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ artha kriyā yogya viṣaya tvāt tad arthinām pravṛtteḥ artha kriyā yogya lakṣaṇam hi vastu tatas api vikalpāt vastuni eva tad adhyavasāyena pravṛtteḥ pravṛttau vikalpasya pratyakṣeṇa abhinna yogakṣema tvāt pūrva pratyakṣa kṣaṇena upayogaa bhedāt uttareṣu kasyacid aprāmāṇya prasaṅga iti ced na kṣaṇa viśeṣa sādhya artha vāñchāyām nānā yogakṣema tvāt sādhāraṇe hi kārye na teṣām sāmarthya bhedaḥ apara apara dhūma pramita saṃnikṛṣṭa agniṣu iva agni mātra sādhye arthe etena dharma dharmi liṅga ādi vikalpasya pramāṇa pṛṣṭha bhāvinaḥ prāmāṇyam pratyuktam anvaya niścayaḥ api svabhāva hetau sādhya dharmasya vastu tas tad bhāva tayā sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anubandha siddhiḥ sā sādhya viparyaye hetoḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttiḥ yathā yad sat tad kṣaṇikam eva akṣaṇika tve artha kriyā virodhāt tad lakṣaṇam vastu tvam hīyate kārya hetau kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhiḥ yathā idam asya upalambha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam prāk anupalabdham upalabhyate satsu api anyeṣu hetuṣu asya abhāve na bhavati iti yaḥ tad bhāve bhāvaḥ tad abhāve abhāvaḥ ca pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhanaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tasya siddhiḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva eva hi artha antarasya evam syāt yatra dhūmas tatra avaśyam agniḥ agneḥ bhāva eva hi bhāvaḥ dhūmasya tad kārya tvam anupalabdhau api anvaya niścayaḥ asat vyavahārasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhi mātre vṛtti sādhanam nimittaantaraa bhāva aupadarśanāt vyatireka niścayaḥ api kārya svabhāva hetoḥ kārya kāraṇa vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau dṛśya viṣayābhyām kāraṇa vyāpaka anupalabdhibhyām sādhyaa bhāve hetu abhāva siddhiḥ uddiṣṭa viṣayasya abhāvasya upadarśane anyathā anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya kvacid abhāvaa siddheḥ anuddiṣṭa viṣayam sādhyaa bhāve abhāva khyāpanam apratibandha mātra siddhau sidhyati iti na tatra vyatireka sādhane anupalabdhyoḥ dṛśya viṣaya tā apekṣyate vyatireka niścayaḥ anupalabdhau upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāt sataḥ anupalambha abhāva darśanam etad lakṣaṇa s tridhā eva saḥ hetuḥ tri prakāra eva svabhāvaḥ kāryam anupalabdhiḥ ca iti yathā anitye kasmiṃścid sādhye sattvam agnimati pradeśe dhūmaḥ abhāve ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ iti atra eva trividhe avinā abhau niyamāt pakṣa dharmasya yathā uktā vyāptiḥ avinābhāvaḥ sa trividhāt hetoḥ anyatra na asti iti atra eva niyata ucyate tatra sādhana dharma bhāva mātra anvayini sādhya dharme svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ apara apara vyāvṛtti bhedena dharma bhede api vastu tas liṅgi svabhāva eva hetu svabhāve anvaya vyabhicāraa bhāvāl lakṣaṇe tanmātra anvayena viśeṣaṇam parama taapekṣam pare hi artha antara nimittam atadbhāva mātra anvayinam api dharmam svabhāvam icchanti viśeṣaṇena tathāvidhasya atat svabhāvatām tasmin sādhye hetoḥ vyabhicāram ca āha yathā hetumati vināśe kṛtaka tvasya tasya dvidhā prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca yathā yad sat tad sarvam kṣaṇikam yathā ghaṭa ādayaḥ saṃś ca śabda iti tathā kṣaṇika tvaa bhāve sattvaa bhāvaḥ saṃś ca śabda iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām sarva aupasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti pradarśana lakṣaṇau sādharmya vaidharmya prayogau atra sāmarthyāt eva pratijñā arthasya pratīteḥ na pratijñāyāḥ prayogaḥ apradarśite prameye arthe katham tad pratītiḥ iti ced svayam pratipattau prameyasya ka upadarśayitā pradeśa stham dhūmam upalabdhavata s tasya agninā vyāpteḥ smaraṇe tad sāmarthyāt eva agniḥ atra iti pratītiḥ bhavati na ca tatra kaścid agniḥ atra iti asmai nivedayati na api prāk eva pratipadyate kiṃcid pramāṇam antareṇa evam pratīteḥ nimittaa bhāvāt pratītau liṅgasya vaiyarthyam svayam eva akasmāt agniḥ atra iti prameyam vyavasthāpya paścāt tad pratipattaye liṅgam anusarati iti kaḥ ayam pratipatteḥ kramaḥ pareṇa api tad ucyamānam plavata eva upayogaa bhāvāt viṣaya aupadarśanam upayoga iti ced tena eva tāvat darśitena kaḥ arthaḥ yadi pratītiḥ anyathā na syāt sarvam śobheta tasmāt eṣaḥ svayam pratītau vinā api kenacid viṣaya aupasthāpakena pratiyan asmān kāryiṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā parva brāhmaṇa iva vyaktam mūlyam mṛgayate asmad vacanāt api svayam siddham eva liṅgam anusṛtya pratyeti iti kaḥ anayoḥ avasthayoḥ viśeṣaḥ dṛṣṭā ca pakṣa dharma sambandha vacana mātrād pratijñā vacanam antareṇa api pratītiḥ iti kas tasya upayogaḥ sva niścayavat anyeṣām api niścaya autpādanāya ca sādhanam ucyate tatra svayam ayam prameyasya upadarśanam antareṇa api pratipadya param pratipādayan apūrvam artha kramam āśrayata iti kim atra kāraṇam tasmāt na prameya vacanena kiṃcid prayojanam anyathā api pratipatteḥ utpatteḥ etena upanaya nigamana ādikam api pratyuktam etāvatā eva sādhya pratīteḥ bhāvāt ḍiṇḍika rāgam parityajya akṣiṇī nimīlya cintaya tāvat kim iyatā pratītiḥ syāt na vā bhāve kim prapañca mālayā iti iyān eva sādhana vākye prayogaḥ jyāyān atra pakṣa dharma sambandha vacanayoḥ krama niyamaḥ api na kaścid sarvathā gamaka tvāt sambandha vacane api kevalaḥ prayogaḥ bhinnaḥ ubhayathā api dharma bhede tathā api tad bhāvasya eva khyāpanāt na hi atad svabhāvasya bhāva ekāntena anya bhāvaḥ kṛtaka tvasya bhāve prayatna ānantarīyaka tvavat na api atad svabhāvasya nivṛttau akāryasya tasya nivṛttiḥ yathā anayoḥ eva dharmayoḥ nivṛttiḥ tasmāt anvaya vyatirekayoḥ yathālakṣaṇam ekaḥ api prayuktaḥ dvitīyam ākṣipati iti na ekatra sādhana vākye dvayoḥ prayoga iṣyate vaiyarthyāt tad svabhāvatayā anvaya siddhau tad abhāve abhāva siddheḥ tad abhāve abhāva siddhau ca anvayasya api siddheḥ tad abhāva eva abhāva khyātiḥ yathā syāt na anyatra viruddhe vā iti niyama khyāpana arthaḥ api vyatireka prayogaḥ na yuktaḥ anya viruddhayoḥ api vipakṣa tvāt katham idam avagamyate sat avaśyam naśvara svabhāvam iti yena anvaya vyatireka sambhava iti ced vināśa hetu ayogāt svabhāvata eva naśvarā bhāvāḥ na eṣām niṣpannānām anyatas vināśa autpattiḥ tasya asāmarthyāt na hi vināśa hetuḥ bhāva svabhāvam eva karoti tasya nivṛtteḥ na api bhāvaantaram eva bhāvaantara karaṇe bhāve tad avasthe na kiṃcid karoti iti tathā aupalabdhy ādi prasaṅgaḥ na api bhāvaantaram asya āvaraṇam tad avasthe tasmin āvaraṇasya api ayogāt na api vināśa hetunā bhāvaa bhāvaḥ kriyate abhāvasya vidhinā upagame vyatirekaa vyatireka vikalpa anatikramāt bhāva pratiṣedha eka rūpa tve bhāvam na karoti iti syāt evam ca akartuḥ ahetutvam iti na vināśa hetuḥ kaścid vaiyarthya āc ca yadi svabhāvataḥ naśvaraḥ sva ātmani anavasthāyī bhāvaḥ tasya na kiṃcid nāśa kāraṇaiḥ tad svabhāvatayā eva svayam nāśāt yaḥ hi yad svabhāvaḥ sa sva hetoḥ eva utpadyamānas tādṛśaḥ bhavati na punar tad bhāve hetu antaram apekṣate prakāśa drava auṣṇa kaṭhina ādi dravyavat na hi prakāśa ādayaḥ tad ātmāna utpannā punar prakāśa ādi bhāve hetu antaram apekṣante tad ātmanaḥ tādātmyaa bhāve nairātmya prāsaṅgāt tadvat asthiti dharmā ced svabhāvataḥ niṣpannaḥ na punar tad ātma tāyām hetu antaram apekṣate bīja ādivat anekānta iti ced syāt etad bīja ādīnām aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvānām api salila ādi hetu antaraapekṣaṇāt kevalā na janayanti tadvat bhāvaḥ api vināśe syāt iti na tad svabhāvasya jananāt ajanakasya ca atad svabhāva tvāt ata eva tayoḥ avasthayoḥ vastu bhedaḥ niśceyaḥ bhāvānām svabhāva anyathātvaa bhāvāt tad svabhāvasya paścāt iva prāk api janana prasaṅgāt tasmāt yaḥ antyaḥ avasthā viśeṣaḥ sa eva aṅkura ādi janana svabhāvaḥ pūrva bhāvinaḥ tu avasthā viśeṣāḥ kāraṇasya kāraṇāni iti na anekāntaḥ kṣaṇikeṣu bhāveṣu apara aparautpatteḥ aikyaa bhāvāt te antyāḥ samarthāḥ kim na janayanti iti janayanti eva na atra anyathā bhāvaḥ svabhāvasya avaiparītyāt teṣu sarveṣu sahakāriṣu samartha svabhāveṣu kaḥ aparasya upayoga iti ced na vai bhāvānām kācid prekṣā pūrva kāri tā yatas ayam ekaḥ api samarthaḥ kim asmābhiḥ iti apare nivarteran nirabhiprāya vyāpārā hi sva hetu pariṇāma aupanidhi dharma as tad prakṛteḥ tathā abhavantaḥ na upālambham arhanti samarthāḥ kim na apara aparam janayanti iti ced na tatra eva sāmarthyāt tasya eva ekasya janane samarthā na anyasya iti na apara apara jananam bhinna svabhāvebhyaḥ cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ sahakāribhya eka kāryautpattau na kāraṇa bhedāt kārya bhedaḥ syāt iti ced na yathāsvam svabhāva bhedena tad viśeṣa aupayogatas tad upayoga kārya svabhāva viśeṣaa saṅkarāt yathā mṛd piṇḍa kulāla sūtra ādibhyaḥ bhavataḥ ghaṭasya mṛd piṇḍāt amṛd svabhāvebhyaḥ vṛkṣa ādibhyaḥ bhinnaḥ svabhāvaḥ kulālāt tasya eva mṛdā ātmanaḥ sataḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātma tayā tad anyebhyaḥ bhinnaḥ sūtrāt tasya eva mṛd saṃsthāna viśeṣa ātmanaḥ cakra ādeḥ vibhaktaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhavati tad evam na kulālān mṛd svabhāva tā na mṛdaḥ saṃsthāna viśeṣaḥ na ca tayoḥ śakti viśeṣa viṣaya bhedaḥ api tad janita viśeṣa bhedasya kāryasya svabhāva bhedaḥ mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ aparaspara ātma tayā saṃsthāna mṛdrūpābhyām tayoḥ apratibhāsana prasaṅgāt anyat eva saṃsthānam guṇa u mṛd dravyāt tena bhinna svabhāvaḥ kulāla mṛd piṇḍayoḥ upayoga viṣaya iti ced uktam atra api ca yadi saṃsthānam bhinnam mṛdaḥ kulālaḥ kim na pṛthak karoti guṇasya dravya paratantra tvam iti na pṛthak karoti tad saṃsthāna ādhāra ātmakam yadi svabhāvena tad dravyam tad saṃsthānam vā tad ādheya ātmakam kim kulāla apekṣayā iti ced na tatas paraspara sambandha yogya tā pratilambhāt anyathā vastuna eva yogya tā dharmatā iti prāk api mṛd piṇḍasya saṃsthāna viśeṣa sambandha yogya tve sati saṃsthāna viśeṣeṇa sambandha prasaṅgaḥ evam tarhi sā yogya tā mṛd dravyasya kulālāt bhavati iti na anayoḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ bhede hi prāgvat prasajyeta asti tāvat eka svabhāva tve api kasyacid aneka pratyaya aupadheya viśeṣa tā iti na mṛd saṃsthānayoḥ eka svabhāvatva sādhanāya nirbandhaḥ tena sahakāriṇaḥ pratyayā na ekaupayoga viṣayāḥ kārya svabhāvasya ekatve api vastuta iti yathā iha kāraṇa bhedaḥ bhinna viśeṣa aupayogān na eka kārya s tathā cakṣuḥ ādibhyaḥ vijñāna autpattau unneyaḥ tathā hi samanantara pratyayāt vijñāna āt cakṣuḥ vijñānasya upalambha ātma tā tasya eva upalambha ātmanaḥ sataś cakṣuḥ indriyāt rūpa grahaṇa yogya tā pratiniyamaḥ viṣayāt tad tulya rūpa tā iti abhinna tve api vastutas kāryasya kāraṇānām bhinnebhyaḥ svabhāvebhyaḥ bhinnā eva viśeṣā bhavanti iti na kāraṇa bhede api abhedas tad kārya viśeṣasya ta eva ete kāraṇa śakti bhedā yathāsvam prativiśiṣṭa kārya janane avyavadheya śakti tayā pratyupasthitāḥ kṣaṇika tvāt sāmagrī kāryasya svabhāva sthiti āśraya iti ucyante tathā hi tad tebhyaḥ samastebhya upalambha ātmakam rūpa grahaṇa pratiniyatam viṣaya rūpam ca iti prativiśiṣṭa svabhāvam ekam jātam apratirodha śaktikeṣu anantara kāryeṣu anādheya viśeṣeṣu kṣaṇikeṣu pratyayeṣu parasparam kaḥ sahakāra artha iti ced na vai sarvatra atiśaya autpādanam sahakriyā kim tarhi bahūnām yad eka artha karaṇam api yathā antyasya kāraṇa kalāpasya tad eva mukhyam sahakāri tvam saha kārīṇām tasya eva antyasya kāraṇa tvāt tatra ca kṣaṇa ekasya svabhāvasya avivekāt viśeṣasya kartum aśakya tvāt svabhāvaantara autpatti lakṣaṇa tvāt viśeṣa utpatteḥ bhāvaantara autpattau antyam na syāt tatas ca na sākṣāt kāraṇam syāt tasmāt na kāraṇasya saha kāribhyaḥ viśeṣa utpattiḥ te samarthāḥ svabhāvataḥ antyāḥ pratyayāḥ saha jāyante kṣaṇikā yeṣām prāc paścāt pṛthak bhāvaḥ na asti yebhyaś ca anantaram kāryam utpadyate tatra ekaartha kriyā eva sahakāri tvam samarthaḥ kutaḥ jāyata iti ced sva kāraṇebhyaḥ tāni enam apara pratyaya saṃnidhāna kim janayanti kadācid anyathā api syuḥ tatas ca ekaḥ api kvacid janayet iti ced apara apara pratyaya yogena pratikṣaṇam bhinna śaktayaḥ saṃskārāḥ santanvantaḥ yadi api kutaścid sāmyāt sarūpāḥ pratīyante tathā api bhinna eva eṣām svabhāvaḥ tena kiṃcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam tatra yaḥ avyavadhāna ādi deśaḥ rūpa aindriya ādi kalāpaḥ sa vijñāna janane samarthaḥ hetuḥ yaḥ teṣām paraspara aupasarpaṇa ādya āśrayaḥ pratyaya viśeṣaḥ sa tadhetu janane samarthaḥ teṣām ca na pūrvam na paścān na pṛthak bhāva iti samarthān api pūrvaa para pṛthak bhāva bhāvinaḥ doṣā na upalīyante tena yaḥ teṣām paraspara aupasarpaṇa ādi hetuḥ sa samarthasya hetuḥ iti tatra na kadācid anyathā bhāvaḥ anena nyāyena sarvatra hetu phala bhāva pratiniyamaḥ boddhavyaḥ pratikṣaṇam anya anya svabhāva bheda anvayinīṣu bhāva śaktiṣu na tu sthira eka svabhāveṣu bhāveṣu svabhāvasya anyathātvaa sambhavāt samarthaa samartha svabhāvānām kriyāa kriyā aanupapatteḥ anya sahitaḥ karoti na kevala iti ced kim kevalasya kārya janane samarthaḥ svabhāvaḥ asamarthaḥ vā samartha iti ced kim na karoti akurvan katham samarthaḥ kuvinda ādayaḥ paṭa ādi kriyāyām samarthā api na sarvadā kurvanti iti ced krīḍana śīlaḥ devānāṃpriyaḥ mūrkhaḥ sukha edhitaḥ kṛtam api punar punar kārayati tathā hi etad bīja ādi upanyāse nirloṭhitam tasmāt svabhāvasya anyathātvaa sambhavāt tad dharmaṇa s tathā abhāvaḥ antya avasthāvat anivāryaḥ antyaavasthāyām prāk asamarthasya sāmarthya autpattau sāmarthyasya tad svabhāva tve apūrva autpattiḥ eva sā atad svabhāva tve saḥ akāraka eva sāmarthya ākhyād bhāvāt kāryautpatteḥ api ca sa eva tāvat sakala sahakāri sahitaḥ kāryam kasmāt karoti kurvan dṛṣṭaḥ tena karoti iti brūmaḥ ahaḥ mahā sāmarthyam mahā prabhāvasya darśanam atatsvabhāvān api bhāvān svabhāva mātreṇa nānā vyāpāreṣu niyuñjanam yadi nāma kadācid kiṃcid kathaṃcid atrabhavantaḥ darśana patham atikrāmet hantaa prasava dharmakam apeta santānam syāt iti iyam cintā cittam dunoti na vai vayam atatsvabhāvānām asmad darśana vaśāt kārya kriyām brūmaḥ kim tarhi svabhāvena eva te tad karaṇa dharmāḥ tān paśyantaḥ kevalam jānīmahe ta ete kārakā iti satyam idam api asti svabhāvaḥ teṣām kārya kriyā dharmā tena samasta pratyayavatām akṛtvā na upekṣā āpattiḥ iti saḥ akṣepa kriyā dharmā svabhāvaḥ kim teṣām tadā eva antya avasthāyām utpanna āhosvit prāk api āsīt āsīt apracyuta autpanna sthira eka svabhāvānām kadācana kasyacid svabhāvasya abhāva virodhāt tad kim idānīm mātā ca vandhyā ca kaḥ vā asya bhāṣitasya arthaḥ akṣepa kriyā dharmā ca svabhāvaḥ na ca karoti iti sahita s tad svabhāvaḥ na kevala iti ced anyas tarhi kevalaḥ anyaḥ ca sahita s svabhāva bhedaḥ hi bhāva bhedasya lakṣaṇam na hi sa sāhitye api para rūpeṇa kartā svarūpam ca asya prāk api tad eva iti katham kadācid kriyā virāmaḥ yasya api bhāvaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ tasya api kasmāt kevalaḥ na karoti yadi bhavet kuryāt eva katham na bhavati kṣaṇika tvāt uktam yādṛśasya kriyā sa katham eka kṣaṇa bhāvi anyathā bhavet yaḥ ca bhavati sa eva na bhavati iti na ayam prasaṅgaḥ kārakaa kārakayoḥ svabhāvatad hetoḥ virodhāt yaḥ api manyate akṣepa kriyā dharmā eva sa tasya svabhāvaḥ na sa sāhityam apekṣate kāryam tu pratyaya antara apekṣam iti sahitebhya eva jāyate na kevalebhyaḥ iti tasya api katham sa kevalaḥ api karoti eva kāryam ca tasmāt na utpadyate iti tad avasthaḥ virodhaḥ na kevalaḥ karoti eva iti ced katham idānīm akṣepa kriyā svabhāvaḥ nanu etad eva paridīpitam bhavati karoti eva iti kāryam ca ayam kevalaḥ api samarthaḥ san param apekṣamānam katham upekṣeta param anādṛtya etad prasahya kuryāt evam hi anena ātmanaḥ sāmarthyam darśitam bhavati kāryam param apekṣata iti tatas kevalāt anutpattiḥ uktā bhavati sa kevalaḥ api samartha svabhāva iti tatas utpattim brūṣe ete ca ekatra katham syātām tad ayam īrśyā śalyavitudyamāna marmā viklavam vikrośati iti upekṣām arhati tasmāt idam eka artha kriyā lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam kṣaṇikānām eva bhāvānām na tu akṣaṇikānām pṛthak bhāva sambhavānām pṛthakkriyā sambhavena sahakāritva niyamaa yogāt yatra tu santāna aupakāreṇa bhāvā hetu tām pratipadyante yathā taṇḍula bīja ādibhya odana aṅkura ādi janmani dahana audaka pṛthivī ādayaḥ tatra santāna āśrayeṇa viśeṣa autpādanam pratyayānām sahakriyā ucyate na dravya āśrayeṇa kṣaṇike dravye viśeṣa anutpatteḥ na hi taṇḍula ādīnām dahana ādau krameṇa svabhāva atiśayaa nutpattau odana ādi siddhiḥ prabhāsvarād vā apavaraka praviṣṭa aindriyasya svaupakāribhyaḥ santāna viśeṣaa nutpattau artha pratipatti janma akṣepa kāriṣu tu indriya ādiṣu na viśeṣa autpattiḥ parasparataḥ tatra yathāsvam pratyayaiḥ paraspara aupasarpaṇa ādi āśrayaiḥ ye yogya deśa ādi avasthā jātāḥ te saha svabhāva niṣpattyā jñāna hetu tām pratipadyanta iti tatra ekaartha kriyā eva sahakāri tvam yatra viśeṣa autpādanena sahakāriṇaḥ pratyayās tatra hetu santānaḥ pratyayān apekṣata iti tatas svabhāvaantara pratilambha ucyate tatra svarasataḥ hetu pratyayānām pūrvakṣaṇa nivṛttau tebhya eva viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa autpādāt krameṇa yāvat atiśayavataḥ antya kāraṇa kalāpāt kāryasya utpattiḥ sahakāriṇaḥ samutpanna viśeṣāt kāraṇāt kāryautpattau viśeṣasya eva utpattiḥ na yuktā aviśiṣṭāt viśeṣa autpattau kāryasya api syāt paraspara viśeṣa autpādān apekṣiṇaḥ api sahakāriṇaḥ kāryam kurvīran tena akṣaṇikānām api sahakāryanapekṣāṇām kāraṇa tā syāt apekṣaṇīyebhyaḥ svabhāva atiśaya autpattiḥ ca na syāt atha sahakāriṇā kṛta viśeṣa eva viśeṣa autpādau api upatiṣṭheta evam anavasthā syāt na ca sahakāriṇaḥ paraspara kārya autpāda anuguṇa viśeṣa autpādane nityam yogi aavasthā yena eṣām paraspara kṛta viśeṣaḥ nitya anuṣaktaḥ syāt tad upāya apāyayoḥ kārya vyakti viraha darśanāt tena ādyaḥ viśeṣaḥ saha kāribhyaḥ nirupakārasya na utpadyata iti ced na asmākam punar punar vacane kaścid udvegaḥ bhavati yadi evam api lokasya nyāya pratītiḥ bhavati hanta tarhi ucyatām na viśeṣa autpādanāt eva sahakāriṇām sahakāri tvām yatas tad abhāvāt viśeṣa janane sahakāriṇaḥ na syuḥ kim tarhi ekaartha kriyāyāḥ api sa api bhavet parasparataḥ viśeṣa rahitānām atha bhavet pṛthak api bhavet tathā ca tad viśeṣa bhāvi kāryam api kevalāt bhavet iti ced pratikṣaṇam apara aparaiḥ pratyayaiḥ yathā bhāva santāne viśeṣa autpattiḥ yogya deśa tāa ādi avasthā viśeṣāṇām ca kārya karaṇam teṣām ca yata utpattiḥ pratyekam ca sāmarthye api yathā kevalānām akriyā kartṛ viśeṣasya pṛthak bhāvaa bhāvāt kārya dvaividhyam ca sahakāri sañjanita viśeṣa paraṃparautpatti dharmakam anya t ca aṅkura ādivat akṣepa kāri indriya vijñāna vac ca kārya kāraṇayoḥ svabhāva bhedāt iti sarvam uktam tatra saha kāribhyaḥ santāna aupakāra apekṣa kārya kāraṇa janmani sahakāriṇām ādyaḥ viśeṣaḥ sahakāri kṛta viśeṣa janmā na bhavati anantara kāryavat tad prabhṛti ye viśeṣa aḥ te tad janmānaḥ tasya teṣām ca tad prakṛti tvāt iti na anavasthā tathā yadi akṣaṇikaḥ api bhāva ādya viśeṣa kāraṇavat ajanitaatiśayaḥ kāryam kuryāt karotu nāma saḥ asya svabhāvaḥ yadi akṣepa kartṛ dharmā pṛthak bhāvasya sambhavāt kevalaḥ api tathā syāt iti uktam atad svabhāvaḥ tu tadā api akāraka eva tasmāt akṣaṇikānām kāraṇānām na eka artha kriyayā kaścid sahakāritva niyamaḥ na api santāna aupakāreṇa iti na tasya kaścid sahakārī tasmāt kevalaḥ api kuryāt prāyas tu saṃghāta sthāyī bhāva santānaḥ sahakāri pratyayaiḥ upajanita viśeṣaḥ sva kāryam kurvan dṛṣṭaḥ bīja ādivat sthira hetuvādinaḥ pratyaya apekṣāyām kārakasya svabhāvaantarasya utpattiḥ iti vyaktam kāryasya apekṣā iti ucyate kārakasya svabhāvasya prāk api bhāvaḥ akriyā na yujyate tasmāt yaḥ yad ātmā sa sattā mātreṇa tādṛśaḥ bhavati na bhūtvā tad bhāve paraabhisaṃskāram apekṣate svabhāvataḥ asthiti dharmaṇaḥ bhāvasya na kiṃcid nāśa kāraṇaiḥ sthiti dharmaṇaḥ api bhāvasya nāśa kāraṇaiḥ kim svabhāvasya kenacid anyathā kartum aśakya tvāt anyathātva pratipattau vā tad svabhāva eva na syāt iti pūrva eva vikalpaḥ tatra ca uktam yaḥ ca parasmāt anyathā bhāvaḥ saḥ aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ yaḥ ca aparaḥ sa katham tasya svabhāva bheda lakṣaṇa tvāt bhāva bhedasya tathā ca pūrva kaḥ bhāvaḥ acyuti dharme sthita iti na tasya anyathā bhāvaḥ etena kaṭhina ādīnām tāmra ādīnām agni ādibhyaḥ drava ādi svabhāvaantara autpattiḥ pratyuktā tatra api pūrvakasya svarasa nirodhi tvāt vināśe agni ādeḥ upādānāc ca apara eva drava ādi svabhāva utpannaḥ sa svayam sthiti dharmā eva vināśa hetu asambhave avasthānāt tasya parasmāt vināśaḥ na ca vināśaḥ nāma aparaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāva cyutiḥ eva vināśa iti ced na idam uttaram vikalpa dvayam atikrāmati kim nityaḥ bhāvaḥ svabhāvena āhosvit anityaḥ iti vikalpe prāṅ nityaḥ bhūtvā paścāt anityaḥ bhavati iti bruvāṇaḥ prāktanasya nityaabhimatasya sarvadā nityaa nitya svabhāva bhedam bhāva dvayam ca svayam ca nāśam anāśam ca prāha iti pūrvasmin vināśa hetuḥ asamarthaḥ na prāṅ nityaḥ bhūtvā paścāt anityaḥ bhavati kim tarhi paścāt api nityaḥ eva eka svabhāva tvāt sa tarhi bhāvaḥ svabhāvena nāśam anāviśan katham naṣṭaḥ nāma tad svabhāva vināśayoḥ aparaspara rūpa tvāt tasmāt sati asya vināśe vināśa svabhāvena anena bhavitavyam tathā api vyarthaḥ vināśa hetuḥ iti uktam tena svabhāvataḥ naśvare anaśvare vā bhāve na vināśa hetoḥ upayogaḥ tasmāt vināśe anapekṣaḥ bhāvaḥ tad bhāva niyata iti yaḥ san sa vināśī na aśvara tāyāḥ nivṛttau ca sattva nivṛttiḥ iti anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ svabhāvataḥ naśvara tve api kaścid atad svabhāvaḥ api syāt na hi sarvaḥ sarvasya svabhāva iti na anvaya vyatireka siddhiḥ iti ced na akṣaṇika tve avastutva prasaṅgāt śaktiḥ hi bhāva lakṣaṇam sarva śakti virahaḥ abhāva lakṣaṇam na ca akṣaṇya kvacid kācid śaktiḥ krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virahāt tasmāt yad sat tad kṣaṇikam eva iti vyāpti siddhiḥ artha antare gamye kārye kāryam hetuḥ avyabhicārāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvena yadi liṅgasya gamaka tvam sarvathā gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ sarvathā janya janaka bhāvāt iti ced na tad abhāve bhavataḥ tad upatti niyamaa bhāvāt tasmāt kāryam svabhāvaiḥ yāvadbhiḥ avinā bhāvi kāraṇe teṣām hetuḥ tad kāryatva niyamāt taiḥ eva ca dharmaiḥ ye taiḥ vinā na bhavanti aṃśena janya janakatva prasaṅga iti ced na tad janya viśeṣa grahaṇe abhimata tvāl liṅga viśeṣa aupādhīnām ca sāmānyānām aviśiṣṭa sāmānya vivakṣāyām vyabhicārān na iṣyate kasyacid kadācid kutaścid bhāve api sarva s tādṛśas tathāvidha janmā iti kutaḥ avasitam tathā ca na anvaya vyatirekau iti ced na atad bhāvinaḥ tasya sakṛt api tatas abhāvāt paraspara apekṣayā janya janaka svabhāva lakṣaṇe kārya kāraṇe tatra yadi dhūmaḥ agni ādi sāmagryā anyatas api bhavet tasya tad janyaḥ svabhāvaḥ na bhavati iti sakṛt api tatas na bhavet artha antaravat na api sāmagrī tam janayet atajjanana svabhāva tvāt sāmagryantaravat na ca dhūmasya tad atat janya svabhāvaḥ yuktaḥ eka svabhāva tvāt dhūmaa dhūma janana svabhāvāt bhavataḥ dhūma adhūma svabhāvaḥ syāt kārya svabhāvānām kāraṇa svabhāva kṛta tvāt akāraṇaapekṣaṇe ca ahetutva prasaṅgāt tasmāt yaḥ dhūma jananaḥ saḥ agni ādi sāmagrī viśeṣaḥ yaḥ agni ādi sāmagrī viśeṣa janitaḥ saḥ dhūma iti kārya kāraṇayoḥ evam svabhāva niyamāt tad vijātīyāt utpattiḥ na bhavati tad kāryam kāraṇam na vyabhicarati tena siddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve kāryasya kāraṇena vyāptiḥ siddhā bhavati nanu vijātīyāt api kiṃcid bhavat dṛṣṭam tad yathā gomaya ādeḥ śālūka ādiḥ na vijātīyāt utpattiḥ tathāvidham eva hi tādṛśām ādi nimittam iti na kāraṇa bhedaḥ prabandhena vṛttau tu śarād bhavati asti ca gomaya etara janman svabhāva bhedaḥ rūpasya abhede api na hi ākāra tulya tā eva bhāvānām tattve nimittam abhinna ākārāṇām api keṣāṃcid anyatas viśeṣa at jāti bheda darśanāt anyathā hi vilakṣaṇāyāḥ api sāmagryā avilakṣaṇa kārya autpattau ca kāraṇa bhedaa bhedābhyām kārya bheda abhedau iti ahetukau viśvasya bhedaa bhedau syātām tathā hi na bhedāt bheda iti abhedāt api na abhedaḥ tad vyatiriktaḥ ca na kaścid bhāva svabhāva iti ahetuka tvāt bhāvānām nityam sattvam asattvam vā syāt apekṣyasya abhāvāt apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācid kā bhavanti vyavasthāvānś ca sādhyeṣu sādhana niyogaḥ na syāt kāraṇa śakti pratiniyame hi kiṃcid eva kasyacid sādhanāya upādīyeta na aparam tasya eva tatra śakteḥ anyasya ca aśakteḥ tayoḥ tad janana etara svabhāva tvena bhedāt tad janana svabhāva vilakṣaṇāt api tasya utpattau na tad janana śakti niyame iti yati atas kutaścit syāt tad janana śakti sāmye tu tad eva iti na kāryam dṛṣṭam kāraṇam vyabhicarati upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ abhāva hetuḥ abhāva vyavahāra hetuḥ vā atra upalabdheḥ upalabhamāna dharma tve tad jñānam upalabdhiḥ tasmāt anya aupalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ vivakṣita aupalabdheḥ anya tvāt abhakṣyaa sparśanīyavat paryudāsa vṛttyā upalabhyamāna dharma tve sva viṣaya vijñāna janana yogya tā la kṣaṇaḥ viṣaya svabhāva upalabdhiḥ yogyatāyā bhāva rūpa tvāt tasmāt anya aupalabdhi yogya tā eva anupalabdhiḥ pūrvavat yatra yasmin upalabhyamāne niyamena yasya upalabdhiḥ bhavati yogyatāyā aviśeṣāt sa tad saṃsṛṣṭaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargāt tayoḥ satoḥ na eka rūpa niyatā pratipattiḥ asambhavāt tasmāt aviśiṣṭa yogya tārūpayoḥ eka jñāna saṃsargiṇoḥ paraspara apekṣam eva anya tvam iha abhipretam pratyāsatteḥ āśrayaṇāt sa kevalaḥ tad apekṣayā tad anya iti tad jñānam tad svabhāvaḥ vā jñātṛ jñeya dharma lakṣaṇa anupalabdhiḥ sā abhāvam pratiyoginaḥ abhāva vyavahāram vā sādhayati katham anya bhāva s tad abhāvaḥ yena abhāva rūpa anupalabdhiḥ abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet iti ced uktam atra yathā paryudāsa vṛttyā apekṣātaḥ abhāvaḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca anupalabdhiḥ na pratiṣedha mātram tasya sādhanaa siddheḥ abhāva vyavahāraa siddhi prasaṅgāt tasya asaṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya bhāva siddhiḥ eva aparasya abhāva siddhiḥ iti anya bhāvaḥ api tad abhāva iti vyapadeśyate anya bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ bhāvaḥ svayam pramāṇa siddha s tad abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet tad siddhi siddhaḥ vā tad abhāva iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ yena anupalabdhyā abhāva vyavahāra siddheḥ virodhaḥ syāt sa eva anya bhāva s tad viṣayā ca upalabdhiḥ tad abhāvasya kim na sādhanam kim punar anya bhāvasya siddhiḥ eva tad abhāva siddhiḥ iti ced apṛthak siddhiḥ sambandhaa bhāvāt ca anya bhāva s tāvan na sādhanam yad siddhau yasya na siddhiḥ tad tasya liṅgam bhavati dhūma agnivat anya bhāva siddhyā eva tad abhāvaḥ prasidhyati tasya tad anyaa saṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya tattva vyavasthāpakena pramāṇena eva anya vyavaccheda siddheḥ sambandhaa bhāvāt ca tad ca tasya liṅgam yadi syāt tasya tena kaścid sambandhaḥ bhavet yathā kṛtaka tvaa nitya tvayoḥ ekaartha samavāyaḥ dhūmasya liṅginaḥ ca eka artha samavāyaḥ vā ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ vā janya janaka bhāvaḥ vā na evam kaścid bhāvaa bhāvayoḥ sambandhaḥ yena asya sādhanam syāt asti viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ śabda artha sambandhavat iti ced śabda arthayoḥ tad pratipādanaabhiprāye sati tad prayogāt tena saha kārya kāraṇa lakṣaṇaḥ avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ vā sambandhaḥ syāt ayam ca atra na sambhavati iti katham viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ syāt siddhe hi tayoḥ sādhya sādhana bhāve tad mukhena viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ syāt sa eva asati sambandhe na sidhyati tad asiddhau viṣaya viṣayi bhāvaḥ api na anyathā itaretara āśrayam idam syāt anya bhāvāc ca abhāva siddhau asamudāyaś ca sādhyaḥ syāt tathā ca ghaṭaa bhāvaḥ tad anya bhāvāt iti ghaṭasya sarvatra sarvadā ca abhāvaḥ syāt na pradeśa ādi dharmya bhāva sādhanāt iti ced pradeśa ādi dharmi viśeṣaṇa bhūtaḥ abhāvaḥ sādhyate na tu kevalaḥ tatas na asamudāyasya sādhya tā na ca liṅga liṅginoḥ asambandhaḥ anya bhāvasya pradeśa ādinā dharmiṇā sambandhāt iti manyate na pradeśa ādeḥ eva anya bhāva tvāt yatra eva hi pradeśe yad na asti iti ucyate sa eva tena asaṃsṛṣṭaḥ anya bhāvaḥ tad darśanāt eva asya ghaṭaḥ na asti iti vikalpa iti katham tasya eva liṅga liṅgi bhāvaḥ na ca atra sāmānya viśeṣa bhāva kalpanā sambhavati yena sāmānyam hetuḥ bhavet viśeṣaḥ dharmī iti tad viśeṣa pratipatteḥ eva tad abhāvasya pratīteḥ tasya ca anyatra anyaa bhāvāt pratijñā artha eka deśa tvāt ca na hetu tvam na ca yatra pradeśa mātram tatra ghaṭaa bhāvaḥ tādṛśe kevale pradeśe abhāva eva iti ced nanu tasya eva kevala iti ghaṭa viraha iti sa ca liṅga bhūta pradeśa pratipattau eva siddhaḥ kasya idānīm tal liṅgam anvayasya anugamanam ca nirarthakam tasmāt anya bhāvaḥ na sādhanam abhāvasya asti virodhaḥ sambandhaḥ tatas anya bhāvāt abhāvasya siddhiḥ iti ced kena kasya virodhaḥ anya bhāvena pratiyoginaḥ kim nu vai pratiyogī pramātum iṣṭaḥ yena liṅga liṅginoḥ virodhaḥ sambandhaḥ syāt abhāvaḥ tu pratiyoginaḥ ghaṭasya anya bhāvena aviruddhaḥ sahaavasthānāt tasmin prameye liṅga liṅginoḥ katham virodhaḥ tasmāt sambandhaa bhāvaḥ atra api asamudāya sādhya tvam tad avastham nanu anya bhāva tad bhāvayoḥ asati sambandhe anya bhāva gatyā api tad abhāva gatiḥ na syāt iti ced na vai kutaścid sambandhāt anya bhāva s tad abhāva gamaka iṣṭaḥ kim tu anya bhāva eva tad abhāvaḥ yathā uktam prāk tasya anyaa saṃsṛṣṭa rūpasya kevalasya eka ātma vyavasthitasya tad ātmanā paricchedasya eva anya vyavaccheda tvāt tasya kaivalyam aparasya vaikalyam iti tad anya bhāva eva tad abhāvaḥ tad anya pratipattiḥ eva ca tad apratipattiḥ iti anyathā tasya paricchedena tatas anyasya avyavacchede tad pariccheda eva na syāt tad atad rūpayoḥ avivekāt ya eṣa vyavahāraḥ kasyacid darśanāt kvacid prāpti parihāra arthaḥ sa na syāt na hi ayam analam paśyan api kevalam analam eva paśyati yena salilaarthī na pravarteta anupalambhena salilaa bhāvaḥ pratīyata iti ced kaḥ ayam anupalambhaḥ nāma yadi salila aupalambhaa bhāva iti katham saḥ abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ pratipatti hetuḥ vā tasya api katham pratipattiḥ tasya tatas vā anyasya kasyacid api apratipattau api abhāva pratipattau satyām svāpa mada mūrchā vyavadhāna pṛṣṭhībhava ādi avasthāsu api abhāvaḥ kim na pratīyate bhūyaḥ api vicāritam pramāṇa viniścaye tasmāt ayam analam paśyan api analaḥ ayam na salilam iti anadhyavasyan na tiṣṭhet na api pratiṣṭheta iti dustaram vyasanam pratipannaḥ syāt tatas eva ekasya darśanāt anyaa bhāva gatiḥ bhavati iti ced katham ekam dṛṣṭam anyan na asti iti pratyāyayati kevalasya darśanāt iti ced idam eva asmābhiḥ abhihitam kasmāt tava atra paruṣam iva ābhāti tasmāt tīraa darśinā eva śakuninā paryaṭā api pratyāgantavyam iti alam avidyamāna pratiṣṭhā anayā diśaḥ pratipattyā yadi eka paricchedāt eva anya vyavacchedaḥ sidhyati sarvasya anyasya aviśeṣeṇa tatra abhāva siddhiḥ bhavet na tulya yogyaavasthasya eva upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ abhāva sādhanī iti viśeṣaṇam ca na vaktavyam anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām api tatra vyavacchedāt eka ātma paricchedāt tad anyātma vyavacchedaḥ tad ātma niyata pratibhāsa jñānāt na hi tad ātmā tad anyasya ātmā bhavati anya ātmanaḥ avyavacchede pravṛtti nivṛttyoḥ abhāva iti pūrvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ tam ca deśa kāla svabhāva avasthā niyatam tad ātmanā upalambhamānā buddhi s tathātva pracyutim asya vyavacchinatti evam hi sa tayā paricchinnaḥ yadi anyathā abhāvaḥ vyavacchinnaḥ bhavati tathā tvam ca tasya eva bhavati na anyasya iti anyathā bhūtād vyavacchindati eva tad paricchinatti evam ekasya pramāṇasya vṛttiḥ sarva bhāvān dvairāśye vyavasthāpayati tasya anvaya vyatirekabuddhi hetu tvena eva sāphalyāt tad vyatiriktasya aśeṣasya vyavacchedena vyāpti sādhanāt eva prakāraantaraa bhāvaḥ sidhyati tasya tad anyatayā vyāpti abhāve tena tad arthaa vyavacchedāt punar bhāvasya apariccheda prasaṅgāt tasmāt kvacid pramāṇam pravṛttam tad paricchinatti tad anyat vyavacchinatti tṛtīya prakāra antaraa bhāvam ca sūcayati iti eka pramāṇa vyāpāra eṣaḥ tathā hi kvacid pramāṇam pravṛttam tad eva tad anyasmāt vyavacchinatti tasya eva paricchedāt tad anyat eva ca tasmāt vyavacchinatti tatra aparicchedāt atas tad eva pramāṇam prakāraantaraa bhāvam sādhayati tasmin dṛśyamāne adṛṣṭasya tad anyatvena sarvasya vyavasthāpanāt atad anyasya eva ca tattvena vyavasthāpanāt etena kramaa kramāt ayaḥ api anyonya vyavaccheda rūpā vyākhyātāḥ tad evam ekasya upalambhāt tasya tad anya ātmanaḥ vyavacchedaḥ na tad deśa kālayoḥ sarvasya anyasya bhāvasya vyavacchedaḥ tasmāt atadātmā ca syāt tad deśa kālaḥ ca rasa rūpa ādivat tasmāt yathā uktāt eva anupalambhāt kvacid kadācid kasyacid abhāva siddhiḥ anya bhāva viṣaya aupalabdhiḥ api tad abhāvasya sādhikā iṣṭā eva na tu liṅga tvena tatra api abhāvasya pṛthak sādhya tve sambandhaa bhāvasya tulya tvāt liṅga āvirbhāva kāla eva tad abhāva siddheḥ na hi anya bhāvam pratipadya tad pratipatteḥ anvaya vyatirekau prasādhya tad abhāvam pratipadyate kim tarhi tad anyam pratipadyamāna eva tad abhāvam pratipadyate darśana anantaram vyavadhānena vinā idam asti idam tu na asti iti vyavasthāpanāt dṛṣṭāntaa siddheḥ tad ca tasya liṅgam yad yasya anvayi vyatireki ca na hi evam śakyam darśayitum yatra anya bhāva aupalabdhiḥ tatra tad abhāva iti tad eka aupalabdheḥ kvacid api abhāvāt sāmānyena pradarśane dṛṣṭānte api pramāṇa antaraa bhāvāt sā eva tad anya bhāva aupalabdhiḥ sādhya dharmasya sādhikā iti dṛṣṭāntaa nava sthi tvād apratipattiḥ tasmāt na kutaścil liṅgāt abhāva siddhiḥ saḥ anya bhāvaḥ pratyakṣa lakṣaṇena anupalambhena siddhaḥ mūḍha pratipattau abhāva vyavahāram sādhayet iti alam prasaṅgena sā iyam tridhā anupalabdhiḥ siddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve bhāvasya kāraṇasya anupalabdhiḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva siddhau siddhaa bhāvasya vyāpakasya anupalabdhiḥ svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ ca tatra kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ api svabhāvasya asat vyavahāra siddhiḥ anya bhāva siddheḥ eva sa tatra asiddhaḥ kārya vyāpyayoḥ abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram vā sādhayati svabhauvaanupalabdhau tu anupalabdhyā liṅga bhūtayā abhāva vyavahāra eva sādhyate yadi kāraṇa vyāpakau tad anya bhāva siddhi rūpayā anupalabdhyā siddha sat vyavahārau anyasya abhāvam abhāva vyavahāram ca sādhayataḥ sā ca anupalabdhiḥ tayoḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptau eva asat vyavahārasya sādhikā katham tayoḥ parokṣe arthe prayogaḥ na eva prayogaḥ pramāṇa tayā liṅgasya aniścayāt kevalam kāraṇa vyāpakayoḥ siddha sambandhayoḥ yadi abhāvaḥ parasya avaśyam abhāva niścaya iti darśana artham ete prayujyete iti eṣa pakṣa dharmaḥ anvaya vyatirekavān iti tad aṃśena vyāptas tri lakṣaṇa s trirūpa eva hetuḥ gamakaḥ sva sādhya dharma avyabhicārāt ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti apare trīṇi ca etāni abādhita viṣaya tvam vivakṣita eka saṃkhya tvam jñāta tvam ca iti tatra abādhita viṣaya tvam tāvat pṛthak lakṣaṇam na bhavati bādhaa vinā bhāvayoḥ virodhāt avinā abhāvaḥ hi sati eva sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ hetoḥ sa hetuḥ tad lakṣaṇaḥ dharmiṇi syāt atra ca sādhya dharmaḥ katham na bhavet pratyakṣaanumāne hi sādhya dharmaḥ bādhamāne tam dharmiṇaḥ niṣkāsayataḥ tasmin sati eva hetuḥ bhavan tam tatra eva dharmiṇy avasthāpayati iti param bata bhāvānām asvāsthyam anyatra sādhya dharmeṇa avinā bhāvī hetuḥ na dharmiṇy eva iti ced tad kim ayam tapasvī ṣaṇḍham udvāhya putram mṛgyate yasya dharmiṇy asati api sādhya dharme bhāvaḥ tam upadarśya katham sa dharmī sādhya dharmavān iti ucyate ata eva bādhā bhāva uktaḥ syāt etad yata eva hetuḥ anyathā api bhavet ata eva pramāṇābhyām abādhita dharmā dharmī iti ucyate iti tad kim idānīm hetoḥ sāmarthyam abādhayā eva sādhya siddheḥ yadi sādhyaa bhāvaḥ bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau niyataḥ abādhāyām sādhya siddhiḥ iti vyarthaḥ hetuḥ bādhāyām api sādhana sāmarthya abhāvāt aniyame na ca bādhakam pramāṇam syāt sādhyaa bhāvasya ca sambhava iti na sāmarthyam abādhāyāḥ na bādhāyāḥ abhāvaḥ abādhā kim tarhi bādhāyāḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā ca puruṣasya kvacid bādhaa sambhave api syāt iti sa hetu prayogasya viṣayaḥ kim nu vai hetuḥ bādha aupalabdheḥ api bibheti na punar bādhāyāḥ yena bādhām anādṛtya api anupalabdhau prayoktavya iṣṭaḥ sa tarhi hetuḥ parama arthena bādhā kim asti na asti iti anapekṣya bādhā aanupalabdhau prayoktavyaḥ kim artham prayujyate sādhya siddhi artham sa kim kvacid satyām api bādhāyām sādhyam sādhayet yena asyāḥ abhāva niścayam prati yatnaḥ na kriyate hetuḥ ca prayujyate tathā ca abādhita viṣaya tvam hetu lakṣaṇam na bhavati bādhāyām api satyām asya sāmarthyāt tathā ca anabhyupagamye saṃśayitasya pravṛtti ayogāt yathā anupalabdhau bādha asadbhāva sambhave api abhyupagamya prayujyate tathā bādhā aupalabdhau api prayujyatām abhyupagame viśeṣaa bhāvāt na bādhāyām satyām sāmarthyam iti ced yadi evam prayuktasya api asāmarthya prāptiḥ iti anirṇīta bādhā sambhavaḥ prayogam na arhati bādhā anupalambhe sāmarthyam iti ced kim upalambhaḥ bādhām vyāpnoti yata evam hetoḥ bādhā sambhava kṛtam asāmarthyam na sambhavet atha tad nivṛttau bādhā nivartate tathā api bādhā anupalambhāt eva sādhya siddheḥ vyarthaḥ hetuḥ anupalambhe bādhāyāḥ asambhavāt upalambhasya nivṛttau api bādhāyāḥ anivṛttau tad avastham hetoḥ asāmarthyam iti aprayogaḥ tasmāt sva sādhya bhāvaa bhāvābhyām anyathā api bhavan hetuḥ dharmiṇi kiṃcid na bhāvayati na vibhāvayati iti upakṣepaḥ na samarthaḥ tad na bādhāa vinābhāvau saha avasthitau tena abādhā rūpa antaram na bhavati tad nāma tasmāt viśeṣaṇa antaram lakṣaṇa antara aupādāna artham vā bhavet yasya bhāve api yasya anyasya abhāvaḥ tad yathā pakṣa dharma tvam sa pakṣe ca bhāva iti na ca etad bādhāyāḥ avinā abhāve sati sambhavati iti na sādhya viparyayaa vibhāvinoḥ hetu viruddhayoḥ viṣaye bādhā sambhavati iti na tad abhāvaḥ pṛthak anayoḥ lakṣaṇa antara tvena vācyaḥ tasmāt hetoḥ prayoge pratijñāyā doṣāṇām sambhavaḥ na asti na api kevalā pratijñā prayujyata iti na pratijñā doṣā vācyāḥ etena eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā api pratyuktā katham ekaḥ hi sva sādhya bhāva eva bhāvāt tad avyabhicārī tatra eva tasmāt anyas tad bādhakasya eva bhāvāt tad viruddha iti atra bādhayā samānam api ca kim vastu tas asambhavat pratihetuḥ sa samyak jñāna viparyaya hetuḥ āhosvit apradarśita pratihetuḥ kim ca atas yadi asambhavat pratihetuḥ aśakya niścaya tvāt alakṣaṇam etad hetu abhāvaḥ vā na hi aniścita ātmanaḥ pratipādaka dharmasya tad lakṣaṇa tvam bhavati yathā sandigdha pakṣa dharma tvasya na api sandigdha lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ bhavati iti na kaścid hetuḥ bhavet tulya lakṣaṇe hi dṛṣṭaḥ pratiyogi sambhavaḥ adṛṣṭa pratiyogiṣu api śaṅkām utpādayati viśeṣaa bhāvāt sati vā viśeṣe hetoḥ lakṣaṇam tatas hi hetuḥ ekāntena nirasta pratipakṣaḥ sva sādhyam niścāyayati iti atad lakṣaṇaḥ na hetuḥ syāt tathā ca vyartha eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā atas viruddha avi abhicāriṇaḥ lakṣaṇam hīyeta sva lakṣaṇa yuktayoḥ hetvoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi virodhena upanipāte viruddha avyabhicārī iti na ca tasya viśeṣasya svarūpam nirdiśyate yad pratītya pratiyoginaḥ sambhavaa sambhavau utpaśyāmaḥ tasmāt na asti eva viśeṣa iti sarvatra śaṅkayā bhavitavyam dṛṣṭa pratihetor api hetoḥ prāk itareṇa na kaścid viśeṣaḥ lakṣyate na ca sambhavat pratihetūnām api sarvadā tasya upalabdhiḥ atiśayavatī tu prajñā utprekṣiṇī dṛṣṭā tena aniścayaḥ sambhavaa sambhavayoḥ iti lakṣaṇasya aniścita tvāt na kaścid hetuḥ syāt atha apradarśita pratihetuḥ yathā āha yadā tarhi śabda tvam nityam abhyupagacchati tadā ayam hetuḥ eva syāt yadi atra anityatva hetum kṛtakatva ādi kaścid na darśayet iti idam aprakāśyam api asaṃvaraṇīyam api iti kaṣṭhataram vyasanam āyātam katham nirvoḍhum śakyeta sa tāvat ayam hetuḥ vastūni sva sādhya tattva prakṛtīni kṛtvā tad pramāṇakān puruṣān abhyudaya niḥśreyasābhyām saṃyojayitvā punar pratibhāvatā puruṣeṇa hetu antara nidarśanena utkīlita sādhana sāmarthya s tāni vastūni tānś ca puruṣān tad bhāva sampadaḥ pracyāvya bhraṣṭa rājya iva rājā tapaḥ vanam gacchati iti kim atra brūmaḥ puruṣa pratibhākṛtam ca sādhana tvam tad kim vastutas sādhanam asādhanam vā sa ca hetuḥ svabhāvatas tad dharma bhāvī yadi katham anyathā kriyeta vastūnām svabhāvaanyathā bhāvasya ubhayoḥ ca viruddha svabhāvayoḥ abhāvāt atad dharma bhāvī ca katham anyadā api sādhanam kasyacid tasmāt svabhāvataḥ sva sādhyaa vinābhāvinoḥ ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ kārya svabhāvayoḥ tad lakṣaṇasya pratihetoḥ asambhavāt alakṣaṇam eka saṃkhyā vivakṣā vyavacchedyaa bhāvāt jñānam punar aliṅga dharma tve katham liṅga lakṣaṇam bhaviṣyati kiṃrūpāl liṅgāt arthaḥ jñātavya iti cintāyām pratipattuḥ avisaṃvādakasya rūpam abhidhīyate yasya darśanāt ayam sādhanaa sādhane pravibhajya tasya iṣṭa artha saṃnidhāna pratyayāt pravṛttim avalambate tathā yad asya ātma rūpam tal lakṣaṇam na tu para rūpam pratipatti janmani upayoga mātrāt tad lakṣaṇa tve atiprasaṅgaḥ evam prameya puruṣa ādīnām api tad lakṣaṇa tvam bhavet na hi teṣu asatsu liṅgini jñānam bhavati niścita grahaṇam tarhi na kartavyam na na kartavyam tasya anyaartha tvāt sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ darśanaa darśanābhyām gamakam hetum icchatām na eva samarthaḥ hetuḥ bhavati satoḥ api darśanaa darśanayoḥ agamakatva darśanāt tena bhāvaa bhāvābhyām gamaka iti jñāpana artham niścita grahaṇam tena para rūpam lakṣaṇam na bhavati tena liṅgasya rūpa viśeṣaa nabhidhānāt tau hi bhāvaa bhāvau tad bhāva sādhaka vṛttyā boddhavyau upāyaantara abhāvāt tena yadi api bhāvaa bhāva vacana mātreṇa tad sādhana pramāṇam ākṣipyate tayoḥ pratipādanāya niścita śabdaḥ prayuktaḥ lakṣaṇe anyathā jñāna sattā nibandhana tvāt jñeya sattā vyavasthāya as tayoḥ eva sattā prasiddheḥ iti sarvatra sattā vyavasthā eva tad sādhanam pramāṇam ākarṣati parārtha tvāt ca śāstra praṇayanasya trirūpam liṅgam saṃvādakam arthasya iti tad rūpam ye na vidanti na teṣām tatas pravṛttiḥ iti para aupa lakṣaṇa tvāt yadi api jñānam siddham tathā api tau eva bhāvaa bhāvau kecid darśanaa darśana mātreṇa vyavasthāpayanti iti tad niṣedha arthaḥ niścita śabda uktaḥ satoḥ api bhāvaa bhāvayoḥ anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sattāyām saṃśayāt tasmāt yatas sattā prasādhaka pramāṇāt anayoḥ niścaya s tad adhīnā iti jñāpana artham asmābhiḥ grahaṇam kṛtam yatas api bhāvaa bhāva vacana mātreṇa tad sādhana pramāṇa ākṣepa siddhiḥ pṛthak atas jñānam lakṣaṇam na bhavati tena eva arthasya avagata tvāt upanaya arthavat pakṣa dharma tvāt anvaya vyatirekayoḥ api tarhi na pṛthaktvam ekasya prayogāt ubhaya gateḥ iti ced na hetoḥ sa pakṣaa sa pakṣayoḥ bhāvaa bhāvayoḥ aparaspara ākṣepāt ekam vākyam ubhayam gamayati iti ucyate na ekaḥ arthaḥ dvitīyasya nanu tatra eva bhāvaḥ tad abhāve ca abhāva iti vākye paraspara ākṣepa iti ced vacanam etad ekasya api niyama khyāpakasya dvitīya ākṣepana antarīyaka tvāt sāmarthyāt ubhayam ākṣipati na punar kevalau bhāvaa bhāvau ākṣipataḥ niyamavantau ca na kevalau niyamasya ubhaya rūpa tvāt tasmāt tatra eva bhāva iti na bhāva eva ucyate itareṇa api na abhāva eva yena bhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vā dvitīyam ākṣipet na evam jñānam para aupalakṣaṇāt trailakṣaṇyād vyatirekitam iti na lakṣaṇa antaram tasmāt na hetuḥ ṣaṣ lakṣaṇaḥ hetu binduḥ ācārya dharma kīrti kṛtaḥ samāptaḥ
 samyak jñāna pūrvikā sarva puruṣa artha siddhiḥ iti tad vyutpādyate dvividham samyak jñānam pratyakṣam anumānam ca iti tatra pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham abhrāntam abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsā pratītiḥ kalpanā tayā rahitam timira āśu bhra maṇa nauyāna saṃkṣobha ādi anāhita vibhramam jñānam pratyakṣam tad caturvidham indriya jñānam sva viṣaya anantara viṣaya sahakāriṇā indriya jñānena samanantara pratyayena janitam tad manaḥ vijñānam sarva citta caittānām ātma saṃvedanam bhūta artha bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta jam yogi jñānam ca iti tasya viṣayaḥ sva lakṣaṇam yasya arthasya saṃnidhānaa saṃnidhānābhyām jñāna pratibhāsa bhedas tad sva lakṣaṇam tad eva paramārtha sat artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt vastunaḥ anyat sāmānya lakṣaṇam saḥ anumānasya viṣayaḥ tad eva ca pratyakṣam jñānam pramāṇa phalam artha pratīti rūpa tvāt artha sārūpyam asya pramāṇam tad vaśāt artha pratīti siddheḥ iti anumānam dvividhā sva artham para artham ca tatra sva artham trirūpāl liṅgāt yad anumeye jñānam tad anumānam pramāṇa phala vyavasthā atra api pratyakṣavat trairūpyam punar liṅgasya anumeye sattvam eva sa pakṣa eva sattvam asapakṣe ca asattvam eva niścitam anumeyaḥ atra jijñāṣita viśeṣaḥ dharmī sādhya dharma sāmānyena samānaḥ arthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ na sa pakṣaḥ asapakṣaḥ tatas anyas tad viruddha s tad abhāvaḥ ca iti trirūpāṇi ca trīṇi eva liṅgāni anupalabdhiḥ svabhāvaḥ kāryam ca iti tatra anupalabdhiḥ yathā na pradeśa viśeṣe kvacid ghaṭaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdheḥ iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ upalambha pratyaya antara sākalyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca yaḥ svabhāvaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu san pratyakṣa eva bhavati sa svabhāva viśeṣaḥ svabhāvaḥ sva sattā mātra bhāvini sādhya dharme hetuḥ yathā vṛkṣaḥ ayam śiṃśapā tvāt iti kāryam yathā vahniḥ atra dhūmāt iti atra dvau vastu sādhanau ekaḥ pratiṣedha hetuḥ svabhāva pratibandhe hi sati arthaḥ artham gamayet tad apratibaddhasya tad avyabhicāra niyamaa bhāvāt sa ca pratibandhaḥ sādhye arthe liṅgasya vastu tas tādātmyāt tad utpatteḥ ca atad svabhāvasya atad utpatteḥ ca tatra apratibaddha svabhāva tvāt te ca tādātmya tad upattī svabhāva kāryayoḥ eva iti tābhyām eva vastu siddhiḥ pratiṣedha siddhiḥ api yathā uktāyāḥ eva anupalabdheḥ sati vastuni tasyāḥ asambhavāt anyathā ca anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭeṣu artheṣu ātma pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ abhāva niścayaa bhāvāt amūḍha smṛti saṃskārasya atītasya vartamānasya ca pratipattṛ pratyakṣasya nivṛttiḥ abhāva vyavahāra pravartanī tasyāḥ eva abhāva niścayāt sā ca prayoga bhedāt ekadaśa prakārā svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūma upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhiḥ iti kārya anupalabdhiḥ yathā na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni dhūma kāraṇāni santi dhūmaa bhāvāt iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣaa bhāvāt iti svabhāva viruddha aupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ vahneḥ iti viruddha kārya aupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra śīta sparśaḥ dhūmāt iti viruddha vyāpta aupalabdhiḥ yathā na dhūma bhāvī bhūtasya api bhāvasya vināśaḥ hetu antaraapekṣaṇāt iti kārya viruddha aupalabdhiḥ yathā na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni śīta kāraṇāni santi vahneḥ iti vyāpaka viruddha aupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra tuṣāra sparśaḥ vahneḥ iti kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ yathā na atra dhūmaḥ vahni abhāvāt iti kāraṇa viruddha aupalabdhiḥ yathā na asya roma harṣa ādi viśeṣāḥ saṃnihita dahana viśeṣa tvāt iti kāraṇa viruddha kārya aupalabdhiḥ yathā na roma harṣa ādi viśeṣa yukta puruṣavān ayam pradeśaḥ dhūmāt iti ime sarve kārya anupalabdhi ādayaḥ daśaanupalabdhi prayogāḥ svabhauvaanupalabdhau saṃgraham upayānti pāraṃparyeṇa artha antara vidhi pratiṣedhāyām prayoga bhede api prayoga darśana abhyāsāt svayam api evam vyavaccheda pratītiḥ bhavati iti sva arthe api anumāne asyāḥ prayoga nirdeśaḥ sarvatra ca asyām abhāva vyavahāra sādhanyām anupalabdhau yeṣām svabhāva viruddha ādīnām upalabdhyā kāraṇa ādīnām anupalabdhyā ca pratiṣedha ukta s teṣām upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptānām eva upalabdhiḥ anupalabdhiḥ ca veditavyā anyeṣām virodha kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddheḥ pramāṇa nivṛtta v api arthaa bhāvaa siddheḥ iti trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam para artham anumānam kāraṇe kārya aupacārāt tad dvividham prayoga bhedāt sādharmya vaidharmya vacana iti na anayoḥ arthataḥ kaścid bhedaḥ anyatra prayoga bhedāt tatra sādharmyavat prayogaḥ yad upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam san na upalabhyate saḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ siddhaḥ yathā anyaḥ kaścid dṛṣṭaḥ śaśa viṣāṇa ādiḥ na upalabhyate ca kaścid pradeśa viśeṣa upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ ghaṭa iti anupalabdhi prayogaḥ tathā svabhāva hetoḥ prayogaḥ yad sat tad sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ iti śuddhasya svabhāva hetoḥ prayogaḥ yad utpattimat tad anityam iti svabhāva bhūta dharma bhedena svabhāvasya prayogaḥ yad kṛtakam tad anityam iti upādhi bhedena apekṣita para vyāpāraḥ hi bhāvaḥ svabhāva niṣpattau kṛtaka iti evam pratyaya bheda bhedi tvāt ayaḥ api draṣṭavyāḥ san utpattimān kṛtakaḥ vā śabda iti pakṣa dharma aupadarśanam sarva ete sādhana dharmā yathāsvam pramāṇaiḥ siddha sādhana dharma mātra anubandha eva sādhya dharmaḥ avagantavyāḥ tasya eva tad svabhāvasya ca hetu tvāt vastu tas tayoḥ tādātmyam tad niṣpattau aniṣpannasya tad svabhāva tvaa bhāvāt vyabhicāra sambhavāt ca kārya hetoḥ prayogaḥ yatra dhūmas tatra agniḥ yathā mahānasa ādau asti ca iha dhūma iti iha api siddha eva kārya kāraṇa bhāve kāraṇe sādhye kārya hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ vaidharmyavataḥ prayogaḥ yad sat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam tad upalabhyata eva yathā nīla ādi viśeṣaḥ na ca evam iha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya sata upalabdhiḥ ghaṭasya iti anupalabdhi prayogaḥ asati anitya tve na asti eva sattvam utpattimat tvam kṛtaka tvam vā saṃś ca śabda utpattimān kṛtakaḥ vā iti svabhāva hetoḥ prayogaḥ asati agnau na bhavati eva dhūmaḥ atra ca asti dhūma iti kārya hetoḥ prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa api hi prayoge arthāt vaidharmya gatiḥ iti asati tasmin sādhyena hetoḥ anvayaa bhāvāt tathā vaidharmyeṇa api anvaya gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhyaa bhāve hetu abhāvasya asiddheḥ na hi svabhāva pratibandhe asati ekasya nivṛtta v aparasya niyamena nivṛttiḥ sa ca dvi prakāraḥ sarvasya tādātmya lakṣaṇa s tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ ca iti uktam tena hi nivṛttim kathayatā pratibandhaḥ darśanīyaḥ tasmāt nivṛtti vacanam ākṣipta pratibandha aupadarśanam eva bhavati yad ca pratibandha aupadarśanam tad eva anvaya vacanam iti ekena api vākyena anvaya mukhena vyatireka mukhena vā prayuktena sa pakṣaa sa pakṣayoḥ liṅgasya sat asattva khyāpanam kṛtam bhavati iti na avaśyam vākya dvaya prayogaḥ anupalabdhau api yad sat upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam tad upalabhyata eva iti ukte anupalabhyamānam tādṛśam asad iti pratīteḥ anvaya siddheḥ dvayoḥ api anayoḥ prayogayoḥ na avaśyam pakṣa nirdeśaḥ yasmāt sādharmyavat prayoge api yad upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam san na upalabhyate saḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ na upalabhyate ca atra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ ghaṭa iti ukte sāmarthyāt eva na iha ghaṭa iti bhavati tathā vaidharmyavat prayoge api yaḥ sat vyavahāra viṣaya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ sa upalabhyata eva na tathā atra tādṛśaḥ ghaṭa upalabhyata iti ukte sāmarthyāt eva na iha sat vyavahāra viṣaya iti bhavati kīdṛśaḥ punar pakṣa iti nirdeśyaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva svayam iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣa iti sva rūpeṇa iti sādhya tvena iṣṭaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva iti sādhya tvena eva iṣṭaḥ na sādhana tvena api yathā śabdasya anitya tve sādhye cākṣuṣa tvam hetuḥ śabde asiddha tvāt sādhyam na punar tad iha sādhya tvena eva iṣṭam sādhana tvena abhidhānāt svayam iti vādinā yaḥ tadā sādhanam āha etena yadi api kvacid śāstre sthitaḥ sādhanam āha tad śāstra kāreṇa tasmin dharmiṇy aneka dharma abhyupagame api yaḥ tadā tena vādinā dharmaḥ svayam sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ sa eva sādhyaḥ na itara iti uktam bhavati iṣṭa iti yatra arthe vivādena sādhanam upanyastam tasya siddhim icchatā saḥ anuktaḥ api vacanena sādhyaḥ tad adhikaraṇa tvāt vivādasya yathā para arthaḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṃghāta tvāt śayana āsana ādi aṅgavat iti atra ātma arthā iti anuktā api ātma artha tā sādhyā tena na ukta mātram eva sādhyam iti uktam bhavati anirākṛta iti etad lakṣaṇa yoge api yaḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ api arthaḥ pratyakṣaa numāna pratīti sva vacanaiḥ nirākriyate na sa pakṣa iti pradarśana artham tatra pratyakṣa nirākṛtaḥ yathā aśrāvaṇaḥ śabda iti anumāna nirākṛtaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabda iti pratīti nirākṛtaḥ yathā acandraḥ śaśī iti sva vacana nirākṛtaḥ yathā na anumānam pramāṇam iti catvāraḥ pakṣa ābhāsā nirākṛtā bhavanti evam siddhasya asiddhasya api sādhana tvena abhimatasya svayam vādinā tadā sādhayitum aniṣṭasya ukta mātrasya ca viparyayeṇa sādhyaḥ tena eva sva rūpeṇa abhimataḥ vādina iṣṭaḥ anirākṛtaḥ pakṣa iti pakṣa lakṣaṇam anavadyam darśitam bhavati trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam para arthaa numānam iti uktam tatra trayāṇām rūpāṇām ekasya api rūpasya anuktau sādhana ābhāsaḥ uktau api asiddhau sandehe vā pratipādya pratipādakayoḥ ekasya rūpasya dharmi sambandhasya asiddhau sandehe vā asiddhaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ yathā anityaḥ śabda iti sādhye cākṣuṣa tvam ubhayaa siddham cetanās tarava iti sādhye sarva tvac apaharaṇe maraṇam prativādya siddham vijñāna aindriya āyuḥ nirodha lakṣaṇasya maraṇasya anena abhyupagamāt tasya ca taruṣu asambhavāt acetanāḥ sukha ādaya iti sādhye utpattimatvam vā sāṃkhyasya svayam vādinaḥ asiddham tathā svayam tad āśrayaṇasya vā sandehe asiddhaḥ yathā bāṣpa ādi bhāvena sandihyamānaḥ bhūta saṃghātaḥ agni siddhau upadiśyamānaḥ sandigdhaa siddhaḥ yathā iha nikuñje mayūraḥ kekāyitād iti tad āpāta deśa vibhrame dharmya siddhau api asiddhaḥ yathā sarvagata ātmā iti sādhye sarvatra upalambhamāna guṇa tvam tathā ekasya rūpasya asapakṣe asattvasya asiddhau anaikāntikaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ yathā śabdasya anityatva ādike dharme sādhye prameyatva ādi kaḥ dharmaḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sarvatra eka deśe vā vartamānaḥ tathā asya eva rūpasya sandehe api anaikāntika eva yathā asarvajñaḥ kaścid vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ rāga ādimān vā sādhye vaktṛtva ādikaḥ dharmaḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikaḥ sarvajñaḥ vaktā na upalabhyate iti evaṃprakārasya anupalambhasya adṛśya ātma viṣaya tvena sandeha hetu tvāt tatas asarvajña viparyayāt vaktṛtva ādeḥ vyāvṛttiḥ sandigdhā vaktṛtva sarvajña tvayoḥ virodhaa bhāvāt ca yaḥ sarvajñaḥ sa vaktā na bhavati iti adarśane api vyatirekaḥ na sidhyati sandehāt dvividhaḥ hi padārthānām virodhaḥ avikala kāraṇasya bhavataḥ anya bhāve abhāvāt virodha gatiḥ śīta auṣṇa sparśavat paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tayā vā bhāvaa bhāvavat sa ca dvividhaḥ api virodhaḥ vaktṛtva sarvajña tvayoḥ na sambhavati na ca aviruddha vidheḥ anupalabdhau api abhāva gatiḥ rāga ādīnām vacana ādeś ca kārya kāraṇa bhāvaa siddheḥ artha antarasya ca akāraṇasya nivṛttau na vacana ādeḥ nivṛttiḥ iti sandigdha vyatirekaḥ anaikāntikaḥ vacana ādiḥ dvayaḥ rūpayoḥ viparyaya siddhau viruddhaḥ kayoḥ dvayoḥ sa pakṣe sattvasya asapakṣe ca asattvasya yathā kṛtaka tvam prayatna anantarīyaka tvam ca nitya tve sādhye viruddhaḥ hetvābhāsaḥ anayoḥ sa pakṣe asattvam asapakṣe ca sattvam iti viparyaya siddhiḥ etau ca sādhya viparyaya sādhanāt viruddhau nanu ca tṛtīyaḥ api iṣṭa vighāta kṛt viruddhaḥ yathā parārthāḥ cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ saṃghāta tvāt śayana āsana ādi aṅgavat iti tad iṣṭa saṃhata pāra arthya viparyaya sādhanāt viruddhaḥ sa iha kasmān na uktaḥ anayoḥ antar bhāvāt na hi ayam ābhyām sādhya viparyaya sādhana tvena bhidyate na hi iṣṭauktayoḥ sādhya tvena kaścid viśeṣa iti dvayaḥ rūpayoḥ ekasya asiddhau aparasya ca sandehe anaikāntikaḥ yathā vīta rāgaḥ kaścid sarvajñaḥ vā vaktṛ tvāt iti vyatirekaḥ atra asiddhaḥ sandigdhaḥ anvayaḥ sarvajña vīta rāgayoḥ viprakarṣāt vacana ādeḥ tatra sattvam asattvam vā sandigdham anayoḥ eva dvayaḥ rūpayoḥ sandehe anaikāntikaḥ yathā sa ātmakam jīvat śarīram prāṇa ādimat tvāt iti na hi sa ātmaka nirātmakābhyām anyaḥ rāśiḥ asti yatra ayam prāṇa ādiḥ vartate ātmanaḥ vṛtti vyavacchedābhyām sarva saṃgrahāt na api anayoḥ ekatra vṛtti niścayaḥ sa ātmaka tvena anātmaka tvena vā prasiddhe prāṇa ādeḥ asiddheḥ tasmāt jīvat śarīra sambandhī prāṇa ādiḥ sa ātmakāt anātmakāc ca sarvasmāt vyāvṛtta tvena asiddheḥ tābhyām na vyatiricyate na tatra anveti eka ātmani api asiddheḥ na api sa ātmakāt anātmakāc ca tasya anvaya vyatirekayoḥ abhāva niścayaḥ ekaabhāva niścayasya apara bhāva niścayana āntarīyaka tvāt anvaya vyatirekayoḥ anyonya vyavaccheda rūpa tvāt tatas eva anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sandehāt anaikāntikāḥ sādhya aitarayoḥ atas niścayaa bhāvāt evam eṣām trayāṇām rūpāṇām ekaikasya dvayoḥ dvayoḥ vā rūpayoḥ asiddhau sandehe vā yathāyogam asiddha viruddhaanaikāntikāḥ trayaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ viruddha avyabhicāry api saṃśaya hetuḥ uktaḥ sa iha kasmān na uktaḥ anumāna viṣaye asambhavāt na hi sambhavaḥ asti kārya svabhāvayoḥ ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ anupalambhasya ca viruddha tāyāḥ na ca anyaḥ avyabhicārī tasmāt avastu darśana bala pravṛttam āgama āśrayam anumānam āśritya tad artha vicāreṣu viruddha avyabhicārī sādhana doṣa uktaḥ śāstra kārāṇām artheṣu bhrāntyā viparīta svabhāva aupasaṃhāra sambhavāt na hi asya sambhavaḥ yathā avasthita vastu sthitiṣu ātma kāryaanupalambheṣu tatra udāharaṇam yad sarva deśa avasthitaiḥ sva sambandhibhiḥ yugapad abhisambadhyate tad sarva gatam yathā ākāśam abhisambadhyate ca sarva deśa avasthitaiḥ sva sambandhibhiḥ yugapad sāmānyam iti tad sambandhi svabhāva mātra anubandhinī tad deśa saṃnihita svabhāva tā na hi yaḥ yatra na asti tad deśam ātmanā vyāpnoti iti svabhāva hetu prayogaḥ dvitīyaḥ api prayogaḥ yad upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam san na upalabhyate na tad tatra asti tad yathā kvacid avidyamānaḥ ghaṭaḥ na upalabhyate ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sāmānyam vyakti antarāleṣu iti ayam anupalambhaḥ svabhāvaḥ ca paraspara viruddha artha sādhanāt ekatra saṃśayam janayataḥ tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ uktaḥ tāvatā ca artha pratītiḥ iti na pṛthak dṛṣṭāntaḥ nāma sādhana avayavaḥ kaścid tena na asya lakṣaṇam pṛthak ucyate gata artha tvāt hetoḥ sa pakṣa eva sattvam asa pakṣāt ca sarvatas vyāvṛttī rūpam uktam abhedena punar viśeṣeṇa kārya svabhāvayoḥ ukta lakṣaṇayoḥ janma tanmātra anubandhau darśanī yaa vaktau tad ca darśayatā yatra dhūmas tatra agniḥ asati agnau na kvacid dhūmaḥ yathā mahān asa etarayoḥ yatra kṛtaka tvam tatra anitya tvam anitya tvaa bhāvaḥ kṛtaka tvaa sambhavaḥ yathā ghaṭa ākāśayoḥ iti darśanīyam na hi anyathā sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sat asat tve yathā ukta prakāre śakye darśayitum tad kārya tā niyamaḥ kārya liṅgasya svabhāva liṅgasya ca svabhāvena vyāptiḥ asmin ca arthe darśite darśita eva dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati etāvān mātra rūpa tvāt tasya iti etena eva dṛṣṭānta doṣā api nirastā bhavanti yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ amūrta tvāt karmavat paramāṇuvat ghaṭavat iti ete dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ sādhya sādhana dharmaubhaya vikalāḥ tathā sandigdha sādhya dharma ādayaḥ ca yathā rāga ādimān ayam vacanāt rathyā puruṣavat maraṇa dharmaḥ ayam puruṣaḥ rāga ādimat tvāt rathyā puruṣavat asarvajñaḥ ayam rāga ādima tvād rathyā puruṣavat iti tathā ananvayaḥ apradarśita anvayaḥ ca yathā yaḥ uktā sa rāga ādimān iṣṭa puruṣavat anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ghaṭavat iti tathā viparīta anvayaḥ yad anityam tad kṛtakam iti sādharmyeṇa dṛṣṭānta doṣāḥ vaidharmyeṇa api paramāṇuvat karmavat ākāśavat iti sādhyādi vyatirekiṇaḥ tathā sandigdha sādhya vyatireka ādayaḥ yathā asarva jñāḥ kapilādayaḥ anāptā vā avidyamāna sarvajña tāāptatā liṅga bhūta pramāṇa atiśaya śāsana tvāt iti atra vaidharmya audāharaṇam yaḥ sarvajña āptaḥ vā sa jyotiḥ jñāna ādikam upadiṣṭavān yathā ṛṣabha vardhamāna ādiḥ iti tatra asarvajña tā anāptayoḥ sādhya dharmayoḥ sandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ sandigdha sādhana vyatirekaḥ yathā na trayī vidā brāhmaṇena grāhya vacanaḥ kaścid vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ rāga ādimat tvāt iti atra vaidharmya audāharaṇam ye grāhya vacanā na te rāgādimantaḥ tad yathā gautamādayaḥ dharma śāstrāṇām praṇetāra iti gautama ādibhyaḥ rāga ādimattvasya sādhana dharmasya vyāvṛttiḥ sandigdhā sandigdhaubhaya vyatirekaḥ yathā avīta rāgāḥ kapila ādayaḥ parigraha agraha yogāt iti atra vaidharmyeṇa udāharaṇam yaḥ vīta rāgaḥ na tasya parigraha āgrahaḥ yathā ṛṣabha ādeḥ iti ṛṣabha ādeḥ avīta rāgatva parigraha āgraha yogayoḥ sādhya sādhana dharmayoḥ sandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ avyatirekaḥ yathā avīta rāgaḥ ayam vaktṛ tvāt vaidharmyeṇa udāharaṇam yatra avīta rāga tvam na asti na sa vaktā yathā upalakhaṇḍa iti yadi api upala khaṇḍāt ubhayam vyāvṛttam tathā api sarvaḥ vīta rāgaḥ na vaktā iti vyāptyā vyatirekaa siddheḥ avyatirekaḥ apradarśita vyatirekaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ākāśavat iti vaidharmyeṇa viparīta vyatirekaḥ yathā yad akṛtakam tad nityam bhavati iti na hi ebhiḥ dṛṣṭānta ābhāsaiḥ hetoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇam sa pakṣa eva sattvam vipakṣe ca sarvatra asattvam eva niścayena śakyam darśayitum viśeṣa lakṣaṇam vā tad arthāpattyā eṣām nirāsaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ dūṣaṇā nyūna tāādi uktiḥ ye pūrvam nyūna tāādayaḥ sādhana doṣā uktā as teṣām udbhāvanam dūṣaṇam tena paraiṣṭa artha siddhi pratibandhāt dūṣaṇa ābhāsāḥ tu jātayaḥ abhūta doṣa audbhāvanāni jāti uttarāṇi iti
 pramāṇam avisaṃvādi jñānam artha kriyā sthitiḥ avisaṃvādanam śabde api abhiprāya nivedanāt vaktṛ vyāpāra viṣayaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ buddhau prakāśate prāmāṇyam tatra śabdasya na artha tadtva nibandhanam gṛhīta grahaṇān na iṣṭam sāṃvṛtam dhī pramāṇa tā pravṛtteḥ tad pradhāna tvāt heya upādeya vastuni viṣaya ākāra bhedāt ca dhiyaḥ adhigama bhedataḥ bhāvāt eva asya tad bhāve svarūpasya svatas gatiḥ prāmāṇyam vyavahāreṇa śāstram moha nivartanam ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ vā svarūpa adhigateḥ param prāptam sāmānya vijñānam avijñāte sva lakṣaṇe yaj jñānam iti abhiprāyāt sva lakṣaṇa vicārataḥ tadvat pramāṇam bhagavān abhūta vinivṛttaye bhūta uktiḥ sādhana apekṣā tatas yuktā pramāṇa tā nityam pramāṇam na eva asti prāmāṇyāt vastu saṃgateḥ jñeya anitya tayā tasyāḥ adhrauvyāt krama janmanaḥ nityāt utpatti viśleṣāt apekṣāyā ayogataḥ kathaṃcid na upakārya tvāt anitye api apramāṇa tā sthitvā pravṛtti saṃsthāna viśeṣa artha kriyā ādiṣu iṣṭa siddhiḥ asiddhiḥ vā dṛṣṭānte saṃśayaḥ athavā siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat saṃniveśa ādi tad yuktam asmāt yad anumīyate vastu bhede prasiddhasya śabda sāmānyāt abhedinaḥ na yuktā anumitiḥ pāṇḍu dravyāt iva hutāśane anyathā kumbhakāreṇa mṛd vikārasya kasyacid ghaṭa ādeḥ karaṇāt sidhyet valmīkasya api tad kṛtiḥ sādhyena anugamāt kārye sāmānyena api sādhane sambandhi bhedāt bheda ukti doṣaḥ kārya samaḥ mataḥ jāty antare prasiddhasya śabda sāmānya darśanāt na yuktam sādhanam gaḥ tvāt śabda ādīnām viṣāṇivat vivakṣā paratantra tvān na śabdāḥ santi kutra vā tad bhāvāt artha siddhau tu sarvam sarvasya sidhyai etena kāpila ādīnām acaitanya ādi cintitam anitya ādeś ca caitanyam maraṇāt tvac apohataḥ vastu svarūpe asiddhe ayam nyāyaḥ siddhe viśeṣaṇam abādhakam asiddhau api ākāśa āśrayavat dhvaneḥ asiddhau api śabdasya siddhe vastuni sidhyati aulūkyasya yathā bauddhena uktam mūrtya ādi sādhanam tasya eva vyabhicāra ādau śabde api avyabhicāriṇī doṣavat sādhanam jñeyam vastunaḥ vastu siddhitaḥ yathā tad kāraṇam vastu tathā eva tad akāraṇam yadā ta kāraṇam kena matam na iṣṭam akāraṇam śāstra oṣadha abhisambandhāt caitrasya vraṇa rohaṇe asambaddhasya kim sthāṇoḥ kāraṇa tvam na kalpyate svabhāva bhedena vinā vyāpāraḥ api na yujyate nityasya avyatireki tvāt sāmarthyam ca duranvayam yeṣu satsu bhavati eva yad tebhyaḥ anyasya kalpane tad hetu tvena sarvatra hetūnām anavasthitiḥ svabhāva pariṇāmena hetuḥ aṅkura janmani bhūmi ādis tasya saṃskāre tad viśeṣasya darśanāt yathā viśeṣeṇa vinā viṣaya indriya saṃhatiḥ buddheḥ hetuḥ tathā idam ced na tatra api viśeṣataḥ pṛthak pṛthak aśaktānām svabhāva atiśaye asati saṃhatau api asāmarthyam syāt siddhaḥ atiśaya s tatas tasmāt pṛthak aśakteṣu yeṣu sambhāvyate guṇaḥ saṃhatau hetu tā teṣām na īśvara ādeḥ abhedataḥ prāmāṇyam ca parokṣa artha jñānam tad sādhanasya ca abhāvān na asti anuṣṭhānam iti kecid pracakṣate jñānavān mṛgyate kaścid tad ukta pratipattaye ajñā upadeśa karaṇe vipralambhana śaṅkibhiḥ tasmāt anuṣṭheya gatam jñānam asya vicāryatām kīṭa saṃkhyā parijñānam tasya naḥ kva upayujyate heya upādeya tattvasya hāni upāyasya vedakaḥ yaḥ pramāṇam asau iṣṭaḥ na tu sarvasya vedakaḥ dūram paśyatu vā mā vā tattvam iṣṭam tu paśyatu pramāṇam dūra darśī ced eta gṛdhrān upāsmahe sādhanam karuṇā abhyāsāt sa buddheḥ deha saṃśrayāt asiddhaḥ abhyāsa iti ced na āśraya pratiṣedhataḥ prāṇa apāna indriya dhiyām dehāt eva na kevalāt sva jāti nirapekṣāṇām janma janma parigrahe atiprasaṅgāt yad dṛṣṭam pratisandhāna śaktimat kim āsīt tasya yad na asti paścāt yena na sandhimat na sa kaścid pṛthivī ādeḥ aṃśaḥ yatra na jantavaḥ saṃsveda ja ādyā jāyante sarvam bīja ātmakam tatas tad sva jāty anapekṣāṇām akṣa ādīnām samudbhave pariṇāmaḥ yathā ekasya syāt sarvasya aviśeṣatas pratyekam upadhāte api na indriyāṇām manaḥ mateḥ upaghātaḥ asti bhaṅge asya as teṣām bhaṅgaḥ ca dṛśyate tasmāt sthiti āśrayaḥ buddheḥ buddhim eva samāśritaḥ kaścid nimittam akṣāṇām tasmāt akṣāṇi buddhitaḥ yādṛśy ākṣepikā sā āsīt paścāt api astu tādṛśī tad jñānaiḥ upakārya tvāt uktam kāya āśritam manaḥ yadi api akṣaiḥ vinā buddhiḥ na tāni api tayā vinā tathā api anyonya hetu tvam tatas api anyonya hetuke na akramāt kramiṇaḥ bhāvaḥ na api apekṣā aviśeṣiṇaḥ kramāt bhāvantī dhīḥ kāyāt kramam tasya api śaṃsati pratikṣaṇam apūrvasya pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ bhavet tasya hetuḥ atas hetuḥ dṛṣṭa eva astu sarvadā citta antarasya sandhāne kaḥ virodhaḥ antya cetasaḥ tadvat api arthataḥ cittam asandhānam kutaḥ matam asiddha arthaḥ pramāṇena kim siddhāntaḥ anugamyate hetoḥ vaikalyatas tad ced kim tad eva atra na uditam tad dhīvat grahaṇa prāpteḥ manaḥ jñānam na sa indriyāt jñāna utpādana sāmarthya bhedān na sakalāt api acetana tvāt na anyasmāt hetv abhedāt saha sthitiḥ akṣavat rūpa rasavat artha dvāreṇa vikriyā sattā upakāriṇī yasya nityam tad anubandhataḥ sa hetuḥ saptamī tasmāt utpādāt iti ca ucyate astu upakāra kaḥ vā api kadācid citta santateḥ vahni ādivat ghaṭa ādīnām vinivṛttiḥ na tāvatā anivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ ca dehe tiṣṭhati cetasaḥ tad bhāve bhāvāt vaśya tvāt prāṇa apānau tatas na tad preraṇa ākarṣaṇe vāyoḥ prayatnena vinā kutas nirhrāsa atiśaya āpattiḥ nirhrāsa atiśayāt tayoḥ tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ api tayoḥ na tulyam citta kāraṇe sthiti āvedhakam anya t ca yatas kāraṇam iṣyate na doṣaiḥ viguṇaḥ dehaḥ hetuḥ varty ādivat yadi mṛte śamīkṛte doṣe punar ujjīvanam bhavet nivṛtte api anale kāṣṭha vikāra avinivṛttivat tasya anivṛttiḥ iti ced na cikitsā prayogataḥ apunarbhāvataḥ kiṃcid vikāra jananam kvacid kiṃcid viparyayāt agniḥ yathā kāṣṭha suvarṇayoḥ ādyasya anyaḥ api asaṃhāryaḥ pratyāneya s tu yad kṛtaḥ vikāraḥ syāt punarbhāvaḥ tasya hemni khara tvavat durlabha tvāt samādhātuḥ asādhyam kiṃcid īritam āyuḥ kṣayāt vā doṣe tu kevale na asti asādhyatā mṛte viṣa ādi saṃhārāt tad daṃśa c chedataḥ api vā vikāra hetoḥ vigame sa na ucchvasiti kim punar upādāna avikāreṇa na upādeyasya vikriyā kartum śakya avikāreṇa mṛdaḥ kuṇḍa ādinaḥ yathā avikṛtya hi yad vastu yaḥ padārthaḥ vikāryate upādānam na tad tasya yuktam gaḥ gavaya ādivat cetaḥ śarīrayoḥ evam tad hetoḥ kārya janmanaḥ sahakārāt saha sthānam agni tāmra drava tvavat anāśrayāt sat asatoḥ na āśrayaḥ sthiti kāraṇam sataś ced āśrayaḥ na asyāḥ sthātuḥ avyatirekataḥ vyatireke api tad hetuḥ tena bhāvasya kim kṛtam avināśa prasaṅgaḥ sa nāśa hetoḥ mataḥ yadi tulyaḥ prasaṅga s tatra api kim punar sthiti hetunā ānāśaka āgamāt sthānam tatas ced vastu dharmatā nāśasya satya bādhaḥ asau iti kim sthiti hetunā yathā jala ādeḥ ādhāra iti ced tulyam atra ca pratikṣaṇa vināśe hi bhāvānām bhāva santateḥ tathā utpatteḥ sa hetu tvāt āśrayaḥ ayuktam anyathā syāt ādhāraḥ jala ādīnām gamana pratibandhataḥ agatīnām kim ādhāraiḥ guṇa sāmānya karmaṇām etena samavāyaś ca samavāyī ca kāraṇam vyavasthita tvam jāty ādeḥ n nirastam anapāśrayāt paratas bhāva na āśaḥ ced tasya kim sthiti hetunā sa vinaśyet vinā api anyaiḥ n na śaktāḥ sthiti hetavaḥ sthitimān sa āśrayaḥ sarvaḥ sarva utpattau ca sa āśrayaḥ tasmāt sarvasya bhāvasya na vināśaḥ kadācana svayam vinaśvara ātmā ced tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ svayam na naśvara ātmā ced tasya kaḥ sthāpakaḥ paraḥ buddhi vyāpāra bhedena nirhrāsa atiśayauv api prajñā ādeḥ bhavataḥ deha nirhrāsa atiśayau vinā idam dīpa prabhā ādīnām āśritānām na vidyate syāt tatas api viśeṣaḥ asya na citte anupakāriṇi rāga ādi vṛddhiḥ puṣṭy ādeḥ kadācid sukha duḥkha jā tayoś ca dhātu sāmya ādeḥ antararthasya saṃnidheḥ etena saṃnipāta ādeḥ smṛti bhraṃśa ādayaḥ gatāḥ vikārayati dhīḥ eva abhyantarartha viśeṣa jā śārdūla śoṇita ādīnām santāna atiśaye kvacid moha ādayaḥ sambhavanti śravaṇa īkṣaṇataḥ yathā tasmāt svasya eva saṃskāram niyamena anuvartate yathā śruta ādi saṃskāraḥ kṛtaś cetasi cetasi kālena vyajyate abhedāt syāt dehe api tatas guṇaḥ ananya sattva na iyasya hīna sthāna parigrahaḥ ātma snehavataḥ duḥkha sukha tyāga āpti vāñchayā duḥkhe viparyāsa matis tṛṣṇā ca ābandha kāraṇam janminaḥ yasya te na staḥ na sa janma adhigacchati gati āgatī na dṛṣṭe ced indriyāṇām apāṭavāt adṛṣṭiḥ manda netrasya tanu dhūma āgatiḥ yathā tanu tvān mūrtam api tu kiṃcid kvacid aśaktimat jalavat sūtavat hemni na adṛṣṭeḥ asad eva vā pāṇi ādi kampe sarvasya kampa prāpteḥ virodhinaḥ ekasmin karmaṇaḥ ayogāt syāt pṛthak siddhiḥ anyathā ekasya ca āvṛttau sarvasya āvṛttiḥ syāt anāvṛttau dṛśyeta rakte ca ekasmin rāgaḥ araktasya vā gatiḥ na asti eka samudāyaḥ asmāt aneka tve api pūrvavat aviśeṣāt aṇu tvāt ca na gatiḥ ced na sidhyati aviśeṣaḥ viśiṣṭānām aindriya tvam atas anaṇuḥ etena āvaraṇa ādīnām abhāvaḥ ca nirākṛtaḥ katham vā sūta hema ādi miśram tapta upala ādi vā dṛśyam pṛthak aśaktānām akṣa ādīnām gatiḥ katham saṃyogāt ced samānaḥ atra prasaṅgaḥ hema sūtayoḥ dṛśyaḥ saṃyoga iti ced kutaḥ adṛṣṭa āśraye gatiḥ rasa rūpa ādi yogaḥ ca viruddha upacārataḥ iṣṭas/ ced buddhi bhedaḥ astu paṅktiḥ dīrghā iti vā katham saṃkhyā saṃyoga karma ādeḥ api tadvat svarūpataḥ abhilāpa at ca bhedena rūpam buddhau na bhāsate śabda jñāne vikalpena vastu bheda anusāriṇā guṇa ādiṣu iva kalpya arthe naṣṭa ajāteṣu vā yathā mataḥ yadi upacāraḥ atra sa iṣṭaḥ yad nibandhanaḥ sa eva sarva bhāveṣu hetuḥ kim na iṣyate tayoḥ upacāraḥ na sarvatra yadi bhinna viśeṣaṇam mukhyam iti eva ca kutaḥ abhinne bhinna artha tā iti ced anartha antara hetu tve api aparyāyaḥ sita ādiṣu saṃkhyā ādi yoginaḥ śabdāḥ tatra api artha antaram yadi guṇa dravya aviśeṣaḥ syāt bhinnaḥ vyāvṛtti bhedataḥ syāt anartha antara artha tve api akarma adravya śabdavat vyatirekī iva yad ca api sūcyate bhāva vācibhiḥ saṃkhyā ādi tadvataḥ śabdaiḥ tad dharma antara bhedakam śruti s tad mātra jijñāsoḥ na vā kṣipta akhilā parā bhinnam dharmam iva ācaṣṭe yogaḥ aṅgulyā iti kvacid yuktā aṅgulī iti sarveṣām ākṣepāt dharmi vācinī khyāta eka artha abhidhāne api tathā vihita saṃsthitiḥ rūpa ādi śakti bhedānām anākṣepeṇa vartate tad samāna phalā ahetu vyavacchede ghaṭa śrutiḥ atas na rūpam ghaṭa iti eka adhikaraṇā śrutiḥ bhedaḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ jāti samudāya abhidāyinoḥ rūpa ādayaḥ ghaṭasya iti tad sāmānya upasarjanāḥ tad śakti bhedāḥ khyāpyante vācyaḥ anyaḥ api anayā diśā hetu tve ca samastānām eka aṅga vikale api na pratyekam api sāmarthye yugapad bahu sambhavaḥ na aneka tvasya tulya tvāt prāṇa apānau niyāmakau ekatve api bahu vyakti s tad hetoḥ nitya saṃnidheḥ na aneka hetuḥ iti ced na aviśeṣāt kramāt api na eka prāṇe api aneka artha grahaṇān niyamas tatas ekayā aneka vijñāne buddhyā astu sakṛt eva tad avirodhāt krameṇa api mā bhūt tad aviśeṣatas bahavaḥ kṣaṇikāḥ prāṇā asvajātīyakāḥ kila tādṛśām eva cittānām kalpyante yadi kāraṇam kramavantaḥ katham te syuḥ kramavat hetunā vinā pūrva sva jāti hetu tve na syāt ādyasya sambhavaḥ tad hetuḥ tādṛśaḥ na asti sati vā aneka tā dhruvam prāṇānām bhinna deśa tvāt sakṛt janma dhiyāmataḥ yadi eka kālikaḥ anekaḥ api eka caitanya kāraṇam ekasya api na vaikalye syāt manda śvasita ādiṣu atha hetuḥ yathābhāvam jñāne api syāt viśiṣṭa tā na hi tad tasya kāryam yadi asya bhedān na bhidyate vijñānam śakti niyamāt ekam ekasya kāraṇam anya artha asakti viguṇe jñāne anartha antara grahāt śarīrāt sakṛt utpannā dhīḥ sva jātyā niyamyate paratas ced samarthasya dehasya viratiḥ kutas anāśrayān nivṛtte syāt śarīre cetasaḥ sthitiḥ kevalasya iti ced citta santānam sthiti kāraṇam tad hetu vṛtti lābhāya na aṅgatām yadi gacchati hetuḥ deha antara utpattau pañca āyatanam aihikam tad aṅga bhāva hetutva niṣedhe anupalambhanam aniścaya karam proktam indriya ādy api śeṣavat dṛṣṭā ca śaktiḥ pūrveṣām indriyāṇām sva jātiṣu vikāra darśanāt siddham aparāpara janma ca śarīrāt yadi tad janma prasaṅgaḥ pūrvavat bhavet cittāt ced tatas eva astu janma deha antarasya ca tasmāt na hetu vaikalyāt sarveṣām antya cetasām asandhiḥ īdṛśam tena śeṣavat sādhanam matam abhyāsena viśeṣe api laṅghana udaka tāpavat svabhāva atikramaḥ mā bhūd iti ced āhitaḥ sa ced punar yatnam apekṣeta yadi syāt asthira āśrayaḥ viśeṣaḥ na eva bardheta svabhāvaḥ ca na tādṛśaḥ tatra upayukta śaktīnām viśeṣa anuttarān prati sādhanānām asāmarthyān nityam ca anāśraya sthiteḥ viśeṣasya asvabhāva tvāt vṛddhau api āhitaḥ yadā na apekṣeta punar yatnam yatnaḥ anyaḥ syāt viśeṣa kṛt kāṣṭha pārada hema ādeḥ agni ādeḥ iva cetasi abhyāsa jāḥ pravartante sva rasena kṛpā ādayaḥ tasmāt sa teṣām utpannaḥ svabhāvaḥ jāyate guṇaḥ tad uttara uttaraḥ yatnaḥ viśeṣasya vidhāyakaḥ yasmāt ca tulya jātīya pūrva bīja pravṛddhayaḥ kṛpā ādi buddhayaḥ tāsām sati abhyāse kutas sthitiḥ na ca evam laṅghanāt eva laṅghanam bala yatnayoḥ tad hetvoḥ sthita śakti tvāl laṅghanasya sthita ātma tā tasya ādau deha vaiguṇyāt paścātvat avilaṅghanam śanais yatnena vaiguṇye niraste sva bale sthitiḥ kṛpā sva bīja prabhavā sva bīja prabhavaiḥ na ced vipakṣaiḥ bādhyate ced te prayāti atyanta sa ātma tām tathā hi mūlam abhyāsaḥ pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ parasya tu kṛpā vairāgya bodha ādeś citta dharmasya pāṭave kṛpā ātmaka tvam abhyāsāt ghṛṇā vairāgya rāgavat niṣpanna karuṇā utkarṣa para duḥkha kṣameḥ itas dayāvān duḥkha hāna artham upāyeṣu abhiyujyate parokṣa upeya tad hetoḥ tad ākhyānam hi duṣkaram yukty āgamābhyām vimṛśan duḥkha hetum parīkṣate tasya anitya ādi rūpām ca duḥkhasya eva viśeṣaṇaiḥ yatas tathā sthite hetau nivṛttiḥ na iti paśyati phalasya hetoḥ hāna artham tad vipakṣam parīkṣate sādhyate tad vipakṣaḥ api hetaḥ rūpa avabodhataḥ ātma ātmīya graha kṛtaḥ snehaḥ saṃskāra gocaraḥ hetuḥ virodhī nairātmya darśanam tasya bādhakam bahuśas bahudhā upāyam kālena bahunā asya ca gacchanti abhyasyatas tatra guṇa doṣāḥ prakāśatām buddheḥ ca pāṭavāt hetoḥ vāsanātaḥ prahīyate padārtha vṛtteḥ khaṅga ādeḥ viśeṣaḥ ayam mahā muneḥ upāya abhyāsa eva ayam tādarthyā c śāsanam matam niṣpatteḥ prathamam bhāvāt hetuḥ uktam idam dvayam hetoḥ prahāṇam tri guṇam sugata tvam aniśrayāt duḥkhasya śastam nairātmya dṛṣṭeḥ tad yuktitaḥ api vā punar āvṛttiḥ iti uktau janma doṣa samudbhavau ātma darśana bījasya hānāt apunar āgamaḥ tad bhūta bhinna ātma tayā aśeṣam akleśa nirjaram kāya vāc buddhi vaiguṇyam mārga ukty apaṭu tā api vā aśeṣa hānam abhyāsāt ukty ādeḥ doṣa saṃkṣayaḥ na iti eke vyatirekaḥ asya sandigdha avyabhicāry atas akṣayi tvam ca doṣāṇām nitya tvāt anupāyataḥ upāyasya aparijñānāt iti vā parikalpayet hetumat tvāt viruddhasya hetoḥ abhyāsataḥ kṣayāt hetu svabhāva jñānena tad jñānam api sādhyate tāyaḥ sva dṛṣṭa mārga uktiḥ vaiphalyāt vakti na anṛtam dayālu tvāt para artham ca sarva ārambha abhiyogataḥ tatas pramāṇam tāyaḥ vā catuḥsatya prakāśanam duḥkham saṃsāriṇaḥ skandhā rāga ādeḥ pāṭava īkṣaṇāt abhyāsāt na yadṛcchātaḥ ahetoḥ janma virodhataḥ vyabhicārān na vāta ādi dharmaḥ prakṛti saṃkarāt adoṣaḥ ced tad anyaḥ api dharmaḥ kim tasya na īkṣyate na sarva dharmaḥ sarveṣām sama rāga prasaṅgataḥ rūpa ādivat adoṣaḥ ced tulyam tatra api codanam ādhipatyam viśiṣṭānām yadi tatra na karmaṇām viśeṣe api ca doṣānām aviśeṣāt asiddha tā na vikārāt vikāreṇa sarveṣām na ca sarvajāḥ kāraṇe vardhamāne ca kārya hāniḥ n na yujyate tāpa ādiṣu iva rāga ādeḥ vikāraḥ api sukha ādi jaḥ vaiṣamya jena duḥkhena rāgasya anudbhavaḥ yadi vācyam kena udbhavaḥ sāmyān mada vṛddhiḥ smaras tatas rāgī viṣam adoṣaḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ sāmye api na aparaḥ kṣayāt asṛk srutaḥ api anye na eka strī niyataḥ madaḥ te na ekasyām na tīvraḥ syāt aṅga rūpa ādy api iti ced na sarveṣām anekāntān na ca api aniyataḥ bhavet aguṇa grāhiṇaḥ api syāt aṅgam saḥ api guṇa grahaḥ yadi sarvā guṇa grāhī syāt hetoḥ aviśeṣatas yad avasthaḥ mataḥ rāgī na dveṣī syāt ca tādṛśaḥ tayoḥ asama rūpa tvān niyamaḥ ca atra na īkṣyate sa jāti vāsanā bheda pratibaddha pravṛttayaḥ yasya rāga ādayas tasya na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ etena bhūta dharma tvam niṣiddham niśrayasya ca niṣedhān na pṛthivī ādi niśritā dhavalā ādayaḥ tad upādāya śabdaḥ ca hetv arthaḥ sva āśrayeṇa ca avinirbhāga varti tvāt āśrayā ayuktam anyathā mada ādi śakteḥ iva ced vinirbhāgaḥ na vastunaḥ śaktiḥ artha antaram vastu naśyet na āśritam āśraye tiṣṭhati avikale yāti tad tulyam ced na bhedataḥ bhūta cetanayoḥ bhinna pratibhāsa avabodhataḥ āvikāram ca kāyasya tulya rūpam bhavet manaḥ rūpa ādivat vikalpasya kā eva artha paratantra tā anapekṣya yadā kāyam vāsanā bodha kāraṇam jñānam syāt kasyacid kiṃcid kadācid tena kiṃcana avijñānasya vijñāna anupādāna āt ca sidhyati vijñāna śakti sambandhāt iṣṭaḥ ced sarva vastunaḥ etad sāṃkhya paśoḥ kaḥ anyaḥ sa lajjaḥ vaktum īhate adṛṣṭa pūrvam asti iti tṛṇa agre kariṇām śatam yad rūpam dṛśyatām yātam tad rūpam prāṅ na dṛśyate śatadhā viprakīrṇe api hetau tad vidyate katham rāga ādy aniyamaḥ apūrva prādurbhāve prasajyate bhūta ātma tā anatikrānteḥ sarvaḥ rāga ādimān yadi sarvaḥ samāna rāgaḥ syāt bhūta atiśayataḥ na ced bhūtānām prāṇitā bhede api ayam bhedaḥ yad āśrayaḥ tad nirhrāsa atiśayavat tad bhāvāt tāni hāpayet na ced bhede api rāga ādi hetu tulya ātma tā akṣayaḥ sarvatra rāgaḥ sadṛśaḥ syāt hetoḥ sadṛśā ātmanaḥ na hi gaḥ pratyayasya asti samāna artha bhuvaḥ kvacid tāratamyam pṛthivī ādau prāṇitā ādeḥ iha api vā auṣṇyasya tāratamye api na anuṣṇaḥ agniḥ kadācana tathā iha api iti ced na agneḥ auṣṇyāt bheda niṣedhataḥ tāratamya anubhavinaḥ yasya anyasya sataḥ guṇāḥ te kvacid pratihanyante tad bhede dhavalā ādivat rūpa ādi van na niyamas teṣām bhūta avibhāgataḥ tad tulyam ced na rāga ādeḥ saha utpatti prasaṅgataḥ vikalpya viṣaya tvāt ca viṣayā na niyāmakāḥ sabhāga hetu virahāt rāga ādeḥ niyamaḥ na vā sarvadā sarva buddhīnām janma vā hetu saṃnidheḥ kadācid upalambhāt tad adhruvam doṣa niśrayāt duḥkham hetu vaśa tvāt ca na ca ātmā na api adhiṣṭhitam na akāraṇam adhiṣṭhātā nityam vā janakam katham tasmāt anekam ekasmāt bhinna kālam na jāyate kārya anutpādataḥ anyeṣu saṃgateṣu api hetuṣu hetv antara anumānam syāt na etad nityeṣu vidyate kādācid ka tayā siddhā duḥkhasya asya sa hetu tā nityam sattvam asattvam vā ahetoḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt taikṣṇya ādīnām yathā na asti kāraṇam kaṇḍaka ādiṣu tathā akāraṇam etad syāt iti kecid pracakṣate sati eva yasmin yaj janma vikāre vā api vikriyā tad tasya kāraṇam prāhuḥ tad teṣām api vidyate sparśasya rūpa hetu tvāt darśane asti nimitta tā nityānām pratiṣedhena na īśvara ādeś ca sambhavaḥ asāmarthyāt atas hetuḥ bhava vāñchā parigrahaḥ yasmāt deśa viśeṣasya tad prāpti āśākṛtaḥ nṛṇām sā bhava icchā āpty anāpti icchoḥ pravṛttiḥ sukha duḥkhayoḥ yatas api prāṇinaḥ kāma vibhava icche ca te mate sarvatra ca ātma snehasya hetu tvāt sampravartate asukhe sukha saṃjñasya tasmāt tṛṣṇā bhava āśrayaḥ virakta janma adṛṣṭeḥ iti ācāryāḥ sampracakṣate adeha rāga adṛṣṭeḥ ca dehāt rāga samudbhavaḥ nimitta upagamāt iṣṭam upādānam tu vāryate imān tu yuktiman vicchan bādhate sva matam svayam janmanā sahabhāvaḥ ced jātānām rāga darśanāt sabhāga jāteḥ prāk siddhiḥ kāraṇa tve api na uditam ajñānam uktā tṛṣṇā eva santāna preraṇād bhave ānantaryān na karma api sati tasmin asambhavāt tad anātyantikam hetoḥ pratibandha ādi sambhavāt saṃsāri tvāt anirmokṣaḥ na iṣṭa tvāt aprasiddhitaḥ yāvat ātmani na premṇaḥ hāniḥ sa paritasyati tāvat duḥkhitam āropya na ca svasthaḥ avatiṣṭhate mithyā adhyāropa hāna artham yatnaḥ asati api moktari avasthā vīta rāgāṇām dayayā karmaṇā api vā ākṣipte avinivṛtti iṣṭeḥ sahakāri kṣayāt alam na ākṣeptum aparam karma bhava tṛṣṇā vilaṅghinām duḥkha jñāne aviruddhasya pūrva saṃskāra vāhinī vastu dharma udaya utpattiḥ na sā sattva anurodhinī ātma antara samāropāt rāgaḥ dharme atad ātmake duḥkha santāna saṃsparśa mātreṇa eva dayā udayaḥ mohaś ca mūlam doṣāṇām sa ca sattva grahaḥ vinā tena ādya hetau na dveṣaḥ na doṣaḥ atas kṛpā matā na amuktiḥ pūrva saṃskāra kṣaye anya apratisandhitaḥ akṣīṇa śaktiḥ saṃskāraḥ yeṣām tiṣṭhanti te anaghāḥ manda tvāt karuṇāyāḥ ca na yatnaḥ sthāpane mahān tiṣṭhanti eva para adhīnāḥ yeṣām tu mahatī kṛpā satkāya dṛṣṭeḥ vigamāt ādya eva abhavaḥ bhavet mārge ced sahaja ahāneḥ na hānau vā bhavaḥ kutas sukhī bhave ayam duḥkhī vā mā bhūvam iti tṛṣyataḥ yā eva aham iti dhīḥ sā eva sahajam sattva darśanam na hi apaśyan aham iti snihyati ātmani kaścana na ca ātmani vinā premṇā sukha kāmaḥ abhidhāvati duḥkha utpādasya hetu tvam bandhaḥ nityasya tad kutas aduḥkha utpāda hetu tvam mokṣaḥ nityasya tad kutas anitya tvena yaḥ avācyaḥ sa hetuḥ n na hi kasyacid bandha mokṣau avācye api na vidyete katham ca na nityam tam āhuḥ vidvāṃsaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ na naśyati tyaktvā imām hrepaṇīm dṛṣṭim atas nityaḥ sa ucyatām uktaḥ mārgasya tad abhyāsāt āśrayaḥ parivartate sātmye api doṣa bhāvaḥ ced mārgavan na avibhutvataḥ viṣaya grahaṇam dharmaḥ vijñānasya yathā asti saḥ gṛhyate saḥ asya
