janakaḥ vidyamāna ātmanā iti ca eṣā prakṛtiḥ asya as tad nimitta antarataḥ skhalat vyāvṛttau pratyaya apekṣam adṛḍham sarpa buddhivat prabhāsvaram idam cittam prakṛtyā āgantavaḥ malāḥ tad prāk api asamarthānām paścāt śaktiḥ kva tad maye na alam praroḍhum atyantam syandinyām agnivat bhuvi bādhaka utpatti sāmarthya garbhe śaktaḥ api vastuni nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnavat tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātatas ātma graha eka yoni tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvataḥ rāga pratighayoḥ bādhā bhede api na parasparam moha avirodhān maitrī ādeḥ na atyantam doṣa nigrahaḥ tad mūlāḥ ca malāḥ sarve sa ca sat kāya darśanam vidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa tvāc caittatvena upalabdhitaḥ mithyā upalabdhiḥ ajñāna yukteḥ ca anyat ayuktimat vyākhyeyaḥ atra virodhaḥ yaḥ tad virodhāt ca tad mayaiḥ virodhaḥ śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ sarva doṣaiḥ prasidhyati na akṣayaḥ prāṇi dharma tvāt rūpa ādivat asiddhitaḥ sambandhe pratipakṣasya tyāga saṃsarjanāt api na kāṭhinyavat utpattiḥ punar doṣa virodhinaḥ sa ātma tvena anapāya tvāt anekāntāt ca bhasmavat yaḥ paśyati ātmānam tatra aham iti śāśvataḥ snehaḥ snehāt sukheṣu tṛṣyati tṛṣṇā doṣān tiraskurute guṇa darśī paritṛṣyan mama iti tad sādhanāni upādatte tena ātma abhiniveśaḥ yāvat tāvat sa saṃsāre ātmani sati para saṃjñā sva para vibhāgāt parigraha dveṣau anayoḥ sampratibaddhāḥ sarve doṣāḥ prajāyante niyamena ātmani snihyaṃ tadīye na virajyate na ca asti ātmani nirdoṣe sneha apagama kāraṇam snehaḥ sa doṣa iti ced tatas kim tasya varjanam adūṣite asya viṣaye na śakyam tasya varjanam prahāṇiḥ icchā dveṣa ādeḥ guṇa doṣa anubandhinaḥ tayoḥ adṛṣṭiḥ viṣaye na tu bāhyeṣu yaḥ kramaḥ na hi sneha guṇāt snehaḥ kim tu artha guṇa darśanāt kāraṇe avikale tasmin kāryam kena nivāryate kā vā sa doṣa tā dṛṣṭā snehe duḥkha samāśrayaḥ tathā api na virāgaḥ atra svatva dṛṣṭeḥ yathā ātmani na taiḥ vinā duḥkha hetuḥ ātmā ced te api tādṛśāḥ nirdoṣam dvayam api evam vairāgyam na dvayoḥ tatas duḥkha bhāvanayā asya ac ced ahi daṣṭa aṅga hānivat ātmīya buddhi hānyā atra tyāgaḥ na tu viparyaye upabhoga āśraya tvena gṛhīteṣu indriya ādiṣu svatva dhīḥ kena vāryeta vairāgyam tatra tad kutas pratyakṣam eva sarvasya keśa ādiṣu kalevarāt cyuteṣu sā ghṛṇā buddhiḥ jāyate anyatra sa spṛhā samavāya ādi sambandha janitā tatra hi sva dhīḥ sambandhaḥ sa tathā eva iti dṛṣṭau api na hīyate samavāya ādy abhāve api sarvatra asti upakāritā duḥkha upakārān na bhavet aṅgulyām iva ced sva dhīḥ na hi ekāntena tad duḥkham bhūyasā sa viṣa annavat viśiṣṭa sukha saṃgāt syāt tad viruddhe virāgi tā kiṃcid parityajet saukhyam viśiṣṭa sukha tṛṣṇayā nairātmye tu yathālābham ātma snehāt pravartate alābhe mattakāśinyā dṛṣṭā tiryakṣu kāmitā yasya ātmā vallabhaḥ tasya sa nāśam katham icchati nivṛtta sarva anubhava vyavahāra guṇa āśrayam icchet prema katham premṇaḥ prakṛtiḥ na hi tādṛśī sarvathā ātma grahaḥ sneham ātmani draḍhayati alam ātmīya sneha bījam tad tad avastham vyavasthitam yatne api ātmīya vairāgyam guṇa leśa samāśrayāt vṛttimān pratibadhnāti tad doṣān saṃvṛnoti ca ātmani api virāgaḥ ced na idānīm yaḥ virajyate tyajati asau yathā ātmānam vyarthā atas duḥkha bhāvanā duḥkha bhāvanayā api eṣa duḥkham eva vibhāvayet pratyakṣam pūrvam api tad tathā api na virāgavān yadi api ekatra doṣeṇa tad kṣaṇam calitā matiḥ viraktau na eva tatra api kāmi iva vanita antare tyājya upādeya bhede hi saktiḥ yā eva eka bhāvinī sā bījam sarva saktīnām paryāyeṇa samudbhave nirdoṣa viṣayaḥ snehaḥ nirdoṣaḥ sādhanāni ca etāvat eva ca jagat kva idānīm sa virajyate sa doṣa tā api ced tatra tasya tatra ātmani api sā samā tatra avirakta s tad doṣe kva idānīm sa virajyate guṇa darśana sambhūtam sneham bādhita doṣa dṛś sa ca indriya ādau na tu evam bāla ādeḥ api darśanāt doṣavatī api sadbhāvāt svabhāvāt guṇavatī api anyatra ātmīyatāyām vā vyatīta ādau vihānitaḥ tatas eva ca na ātmīya buddheḥ api guṇa īkṣaṇam kāraṇam hīyate sa api tasmāt na aguṇa darśanāt api ca asad guṇa āropaḥ snehāt tatra hi dṛśyate tasmāt ta kāraṇā bādhī vidhis tam bādhate katham parāpara prārthanā atas vināśa utpatti buddhitaḥ indriya ādeḥ pṛthak bhūtam ātmānam vetti ayam janaḥ tasmāt na ekatva dṛṣṭyā api snehaḥ snihyan sa ātmani upalambha antaraṅgeṣu prakṛtyā eva anurajyate pratyutpannā tu yaḥ duḥkhān nirvedaḥ dveṣa īdṛśaḥ na vairāgyam tadā api asya snehaḥ avasthā antar eṣaṇāt dveṣasya duḥkha yoni tvāt sa tāvan mātra saṃsthitiḥ tasmin nivṛtte prakṛtim svām eva bhajate punar audāsīnyam tu sarvatra hāna upādāna hānitaḥ vāsī candana kalpānām vairāgyam nāma kathyate saṃskāra duḥkha tām matvā kathitā duḥkha bhāvanā sā ca naḥ pratyaya utpattiḥ sā nairātmya dṛś āśrayaḥ yukti s tu śūnyatā dṛṣṭeḥ tad arthāḥ śeṣa bhāvanāḥ anityāt prāha tena eva duḥkham duḥkhān nirātmatām aviraktaḥ ca tṛṣṇāvān sarva ārambha samāśritaḥ saḥ amuktaḥ kleśa karmabhyām saṃsārī nāma tādṛśaḥ ātmīyam eva yaḥ na icchet bhoktā api asya na vidyate ātmā api na tadā tasya kriyā bhogau hi lakṣaṇam tasmāt anādi santāna tulya jātīya bījikām utkhāta mūlām kuruta sattva dṛṣṭim mumukṣavaḥ āgamasya tathā bhāva nibandhanam apaśyatām muktim āgama mātreṇa vadan na paritoṣa kṛt na alam bīja ādi saṃsiddhaḥ vidhiḥ puṃsām ajanmane taila abhyaṅga agni dāha ādeḥ api mukti prasaṅgataḥ prāk guroḥ lāghavāt paścān na pāpa haraṇam kṛtam mā bhūt gauravam eva asya na pāpam guru amūrtitaḥ mithyā jñāna tad udbhūta tarṣa saṃcetanā vaśāt hīna sthāna gatiḥ janma tena tad chin na jāyate tayoḥ eva hi sāmarthyam jātau tad mātra bhavataḥ te cetane svayam karma iti akhaṇḍam janma kāraṇam gati pratītyoḥ kāraṇa anya āśrayas tāni adṛṣṭataḥ adṛṣṭa nāśāt agati s tad saṃskāraḥ na cetanā sāmarthyam karaṇa utpatteḥ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttitaḥ dṛṣṭam buddheḥ n na ca anyasya tāni santi na santi kim dhāraṇa preraṇa kṣobha nirodhāḥ cetanā vaśāḥ na syuḥ teṣām asāmarthye tasya dīkṣā ādy anantaram atha buddheḥ tadā abhāvān na syuḥ sandhīyate malaiḥ buddheḥ teṣām asāmarthye jīvataḥ api syuḥ akṣamāḥ nirhrāsa atiśayāt puṣṭau pratipakṣa sva pakṣayoḥ doṣāḥ sva bīja santānā dīkṣite api anivāritāḥ nityasya nirapekṣa tvāt krama utpattiḥ virudhyate kriyāyām akriyāyām ca kriyā ca sadṛśa ātmanaḥ aikyam ca hetu phalayoḥ vyatireke tatas tayoḥ kartṛ bhoktṛtva hāniḥ syāt sāmarthyam ca na sidhyati anya smaraṇa bhoga ādi prasaṅgāḥ ca na sidhyati asmṛteḥ kasyacid tena hi anubhūteḥ smṛta udbhavaḥ sthiram sukham mama aham ca iti ādi satya catuṣṭaye abhūtān ṣoḍaśa ākārān āropya paritṛṣyati tatra eva tad viruddha ātma tadtva ākāra anurodhinī hanti sā anucarām tṛṣṇām samyak dṛṣṭiḥ su bhāvitā tri hetoḥ n na udbhavaḥ karma dehayoḥ sthitayoḥ api eka abhāvāt vinā bījam na aṅkurasya iva janmanaḥ asambhavāt vipakṣasya na hāniḥ karma dehayoḥ aśakya tvāt ca tṛṣṇāyām sthitāyām punar udbhavāt dvaya kṣaya artham yatne ca vyarthaḥ karma kṣaye śramaḥ phala vaicitrya dṛṣṭeḥ ca śakti bhedaḥ anumīyate karmaṇām tāpa saṃkleśāt na eka rūpāt tatas kṣayaḥ phalam kathaṃcid tad janyam alpam syāt na vijātimat atha api tapasaḥ śaktyā śakti saṃkara saṃkṣayaiḥ kleśāt kutaścid dhīyeta aśeṣam akleśa leśataḥ yadi iṣṭam aparam kleśāt tad tapaḥ kleśa eva ced tad karma phalam iti asmān na śakteḥ saṃkara ādikam utpitsu doṣa nirghāta ādye api doṣa virodhinaḥ tad je karmaṇi śaktāḥ syuḥ kṛta hāniḥ katham bhavet doṣā na karmaṇaḥ duṣṭaḥ karoti na viparyayāt mithyā vikalpena vinā na abhilāṣaḥ sukhāt api tāyāt tadtva sthira aśeṣa viśeṣa jñāna sādhanam bodha artha tvāt gameḥ bāhya śaikṣa aśaikṣa adhika s tatas para artha jñāna ghaṭanam tasmāt tad śāsanam dayā tatas para artha tantra tvam siddha arthasya avirāmataḥ dayayā śreya ācaṣṭe jñānāt satyam sa sādhanam tad ca abhiyogavān vaktum yatas tasmāt pramāṇa tā upadeśa tathā abhāva stutiḥ tad upadeśataḥ pramāṇa tadtva siddhy artham anumāne api avāraṇāt prayoga darśanāt vā asya yad kiṃcid udaya ātmakam nirodha dharmakam sarvam tad iti ādau anekadhā anumāna āśrayaḥ liṅgam avinā abhāva lakṣaṇam vyāpti pradarśanāt hetoḥ sādhyena uktam ca tad sphuṭam mānam dvividham meya dvaividhyāt śakty aśaktitaḥ artha kriyāyām keśa ādiḥ n na arthaḥ anartha adhimokṣataḥ sadṛśa asadṛśa tvāc ca viṣaya aviṣaya tvataḥ śabdasya anya nimittānām bhāve dhīḥ sat asattvataḥ artha kriyā samartham yad tad atra paramārtha sat anyat saṃvṛti sat proktam te sva sāmānya lakṣaṇe aśaktam sarvam iti ced bīja ādeḥ aṅkura ādiṣu dṛṣṭā śaktiḥ matā sā ced saṃvṛtyā astu yathā tathā sā asti sarvatra ced buddheḥ na anvaya vyatirekayoḥ sāmānya lakṣaṇe adṛṣṭeḥ cakṣū rūpa ādi buddhivat etena samaya ābhoga ādy antaraṅga anurodhataḥ ghaṭa utkṣepaṇa sāmānyam saṃkhyā ādiṣu dhiyaḥ gatāḥ keśa ādayaḥ na sāmānyam artha anabhiniveśataḥ jñeya tvena grahāt doṣaḥ na abhāveṣu prasajyate teṣām api tathā abhāve apratiṣedhāt sphuṭa ābhatā jñāna rūpa tayā artha tvāt keśa ādi iti matiḥ punar sāmānya viṣayā keśa pratibhāsam anarthakam jñāna rūpa tayā artha tve sāmānye ced prasajyate tathā iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ artha rūpa tvena samāna tā sarvatra sama rūpa tvāt tad vyāvṛtti samāśrayāt tad avastu abhidheya tvāt sāphalyāt akṣa saṃhateḥ nāma ādi vacane vaktṛ śrotṛ vācya anubandhini asambandhini nāma ādau arthe syāt apravartanam sārūpyāt bhrāntitaḥ vṛttiḥ arthe ced syāt na sarvadā deśa bhrāntiḥ ca na jñāne tulyam utpattitaḥ dhiyaḥ tathāvidhāyāḥ anyatra tatra anupagamāt dhiyaḥ bāhya artha pratibhāsāyāḥ upāye vā apramāṇa tā vijñāna vyatiriktasya vyatireka aprasiddhitaḥ sarva jñāna arthavat tvāc ced svapna ādau anyathā īkṣaṇāt ayuktam na ca saṃskārān nīla ādi pratibhāsataḥ nīla ādy apratighātān na jñānam tad yogya deśakaiḥ ajñātasya svayam jñānān nāma ādy etena varṇitaḥ sā eva iṣṭa arthavatī kena cakṣuḥ ādi matiḥ matā artha sāmarthya dṛṣṭeḥ ced anyat prāptam anarthakam apravṛttiḥ asambandhe api artha sambandhavat yadi atīta anāgatam vācyam na syāt arthena tad kṣayāt sāmānya grahaṇāt śabdāt aprasaṅgaḥ mataḥ yadi tad na kevala sāmānya agrahaṇāt grahaṇe api vā atat samāna tā avyaktī tena nitya upalambhanam nitya tvāt ca yadi vyaktiḥ vyakteḥ pratyakṣatām prati ātmani jñāna janane yad śaktam śaktam eva tad atha aśaktam kadācid ced aśaktam sarvadā eva tad tasya śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā yā svabhāvena saṃsthitā nitya tvāt acikitsyasya kas tām kṣapayitum kṣamaḥ tad ca sāmānya vijñānam anubandhan vibhāvyate nīla ādy ākāra leśaḥ yaḥ sa tasmin kena nirmitaḥ pratyakṣa pratyaya artha tvān na akṣāṇām vyartha tā iti ced sā eva eka rūpāt śabda ādeḥ bhinna ābhāsā matiḥ kutas na jātiḥ jātimat vyakti rūpam yena apara āśrayam siddham pṛthak ced kāryatvam hi apekṣā iti abhidhīyate niṣpatteḥ apara adhīnam api kāryam sva hetutaḥ sambadhyate kalpanayā kim akāryam kathaṃcana anya tve tad asambaddham siddhā atas niḥsvabhāva tā jāti prasaṅgaḥ abhāvasya na apekṣā abhāvatas tayoḥ tasmāt arūpā rūpāṇām āśrayeṇa upakalpitā tad viśeṣa avagāha arthaiḥ jātiḥ śabdaiḥ prakāśyate tasyām rūpa avabhāsaḥ yaḥ tattvena arthasya vā grahaḥ bhrāntiḥ sā anādi kālīna darśana abhyāsa nirmitā arthānām yad ca sāmānyam anya vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam yad niṣṭhās ta ime śabdā na rūpam tasya kiṃcana sāmānya buddhau sāmānyena arūpāyām api īkṣaṇāt artha bhrāntiḥ api iṣyeta sāmānyam sā api abhiplavāt artha rūpa tayā tattvena abhāvāt ca na rūpiṇī niḥsvabhāva tayā avācyam kutaścid vacanān matam yadi vastu na vastūnām avācya tvam kathaṃcana na eva vācyam upādāna bhedāt bheda upacārataḥ atīta anāgate api arthe sāmānya vinibandhanāḥ śrutayaḥ niviśante sat asad dharmaḥ katham bhavet upacārāt tad iṣṭam ced vartamāna ghaṭasya kā pratyāsattiḥ abhāvena yā paṭa ādau na vidyate buddheḥ askhalitā vṛttiḥ mukhya āropitayoḥ sadā siṃhe māṇavake tadvat ghoṣaṇā api asti laukikī yatra rūḍhyā asad arthaḥ api janaiḥ śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ sa mukhya s tatra tad sāmyāt gauṇaḥ anyatra skhalat gatiḥ yathā abhāve api abhāva ākhyām yathā kalpanam eva vā kuryāt aśakte śakte vā pradhāna ādi śrutim janaḥ śabdebhyaḥ yādṛśī buddhiḥ naṣṭe anaṣṭe api dṛśyate tādṛśy eva sat arthānām na etad śrotṛ ādi cetasām sāmānya mātra grahaṇāt sāmānyam cetasoḥ dvayoḥ tasya api kevalasya prāk grahaṇam vinivāritam paraspara viśiṣṭānām aviśiṣṭam katham bhavet rūpam dvi rūpa tāyām vā tad vastu ekam katham bhavet tābhyām tad anyat eva syāt yadi rūpam samam tayoḥ tayoḥ iti na sambandhaḥ vyāvṛttiḥ tu na duṣyate tasmāt samāna tā eva asmin sāmānye avastu lakṣaṇam kāryam ca tad anekam syāt naśvaram ca tad matam vastu sattā anubandhi tvāt vināśasya na nitya tā asambandhaḥ ca jātīnām akārya tvāt arūpa tā yad ca vastu balāj jñānam jāyate tad apekṣyate na saṃketam na sāmānya buddhiṣu etad vibhāvyate yā api abheda anugā buddhiḥ kācid vastu dvaye kṣaṇe saṃketena vinā sā artha pratyāsatti nibandhanā pratyāsattiḥ vinā jātyā yatheṣṭā cakṣuḥ ādiṣu jñāna kāryeṣu jātiḥ vā yayā anveti vibhāgataḥ kathaṃcid api vijñāne tad rūpa anavabhāsataḥ yadi nāma indriyāṇām syāt draṣṭā bhāseta tad vapuḥ rūpavat tvāt na jātīnām kevalānām adarśanāt vyakti grahe ca tad śabda rūpāt anyan na dṛśyate jñāna mātra artha karaṇe api ayogya matā eva tad tad ayogya tayā arūpam tad hi avastuṣu lakṣaṇam yathā ukta viparītam yad tad sva lakṣaṇam iṣyate sāmānyam trividham tad ca bhāva abhāva ubhaya āśrayāt yadi bhāva āśrayam jñānam bhāve bhāva anubandhataḥ na ukta uttara tvāt dṛṣṭa tvāt atīta ādiṣu ca anyathā bhāva dharmatva hāniḥ ced bhāva grahaṇa pūrvakam tad jñānam iti adoṣaḥ ayam meyam tu ekam sva lakṣaṇam tasmāt artha kriyā siddheḥ sat asattā vicāraṇāt tasya sva para rūpābhyām gateḥ meya dvayam matam ayathā abhiniveśena dvitīyā bhrāntiḥ iṣyate gatiḥ ced para rūpeṇa na ca bhrānteḥ pramāṇa tā abhiprāya avisaṃvādāt api bhrānteḥ pramāṇa tā gatiḥ api anyathā dṛṣṭā pakṣaḥ ca ayam kṛta uttaraḥ maṇi pradīpa prabhayoḥ maṇi buddhyā abhidhāvataḥ mithyā jñāna aviśeṣe api viśeṣaḥ artha kriyām prati yathā tathā ayathārtha tve api anumāna tad ābhayoḥ artha kriyā anurodhena pramāṇa tvam vyavasthitam buddhiḥ yatra artha sāmarthyāt anvaya vyatirekiṇī tasya svatantram grahaṇam atas anyat vastu atīndriyam tasya adṛṣṭa ātma rūpasya gateḥ anyaḥ artha āśrayaḥ tad āśrayeṇa sambandhī yadi syāt gamaka s tadā gamaka anuga sāmānya rūpeṇa eva tadā gatiḥ tasmāt sarvaḥ parokṣaḥ arthaḥ viśeṣeṇa na gamyate yā ca sambandhinaḥ dharmāt gatiḥ dharmiṇi jāyate sā anumānam parokṣāṇām ekam tena eva sādhanam na pratyakṣa parokṣābhyām meyasya anyasya sambhavaḥ tasmāt prameya dvi tvena pramāṇa dvi tvam iṣyate try eka saṃkhyā nirāsaḥ vā prameya dvaya darśanāt ekam eva aprameya tvāt asataḥ ced matam ca naḥ anekāntaḥ aprameya tve asad bhāvasya api niścayāt tad niścaya pramāṇam vā dvitīyam na akṣa jā matiḥ abhāve artha balāj jāte artha śakty anapekṣaṇe vyavadhāna ādi bhāve api jāyeta indriya jā matiḥ abhāve vinivṛttiḥ ced pratyakṣasya eva niścayaḥ viruddham sā eva vā liṅgam anvaya vyatirekiṇī siddham ca para caitanya pratipatteḥ pramā dvayam vyavahāra ādau pravṛtteḥ ca siddha s tad bhāva niścayaḥ pramāṇam avisaṃvādāt ta kvacid vyabhicārataḥ na āśvāsa iti cel liṅgam durdṛṣṭeḥ atad īdṛśam yatas kadācid siddhā asya pratītiḥ vastunaḥ kvacid tad avaśyam tatas jātam tad svabhāvaḥ api vā bhavet sva nimittam svabhāvam vā vinā na arthasya sambhavaḥ yad ca rūpam tayoḥ dṛṣṭam tad eva anyatra lakṣaṇam svabhāve sva nimitte vā dṛśye darśana hetuṣu anyeṣu satsu adṛśye ca sattā vā tadvataḥ katham aprāmāṇye ca sāmānya buddheḥ tal lopa āgataḥ pretya bhāvavat akṣaiḥ ced paryāyeṇa pratīyate tad ca na indriya śakty ādau akṣa buddheḥ asambhavāt abhāva pratipattau syāt buddhi janma animittakam sva lakṣaṇe ca pratyakṣam avikalpa tayā vinā vikalpena na sāmānya grahas tasmin tatas anumā prameya niyame varṇa anitya tā na pratīyate pramāṇam anyat tad buddhiḥ vinā liṅgena sambhavāt viśeṣa dṛṣṭe liṅgasya sambandhasya aprasiddhitaḥ tad pramāṇa antaram meya bahu tvāt bahu tā api vā pramāṇānām anekasya vṛtteḥ ekatra vā yathā viśeṣa dṛṣṭeḥ eka tri saṃkhyā apohaḥ na vā bhavet viṣaya aniyamāt anya prameyasya ca sambhavāt yojanāt varṇa sāmānye na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyeta na avastu rūpam tasya eva tathā siddhe prasādhanāt anyatra na anya siddhiḥ ced na tasya eva prasiddhitaḥ yaḥ hi bhāvaḥ yathābhūtaḥ sa tādṛś liṅga cetasaḥ hetuḥ tad jā tathābhūte tasmāt vastuni liṅgi dhīḥ liṅga liṅgi dhiyoḥ evam pāraṃparyeṇa vastuni pratibandhāt tad ābhāsa śūnyayoḥ api avañcanam tad rūpa adhyavasāyāt ca tayoḥ tad rūpa śūnyayoḥ tad rūpa avañcaka tve api kṛtā bhrānti vyavasthitiḥ tasmāt vastuni boddhavye vyāpakam vyāpya cetasaḥ nimittam tad svabhāvaḥ vā kāraṇam tad ca tad dhiyaḥ pratiṣedha s tu sarvatra sādhyate anupalambhataḥ siddhim pramāṇaiḥ vadatām arthāt eva viparyayāt dṛṣṭā viruddha dharma ukti s tasya tad kāraṇasya vā niṣedhe yā api tasya eva sā apramāṇatva sūcanā anyathā ekasya bhāvasya sadbhāva uktyā parasya tad na astitvam kena gamyeta virodhāt ced asau api siddhaḥ kena asaha sthānāt iti ced tad kutaḥ matam dṛśyasya darśana abhāvāt iti ced sā apramāṇa tā tasmāt sva śabdena uktā api sā abhāvasya prasādhikā yasyāḥ pramāṇam sā avācyaḥ niṣedhas tena sarvathā etena tad viruddha artha kārya uktiḥ upavarṇitā prayogaḥ kevalam bhinnaḥ sarvatra arthaḥ na bhidyate viruddham tad ca sā upāyam avidhāyā api dhāya ca pramāṇa uktiḥ niṣedhe yā na sā nyāya anusāriṇī ukty ādeḥ sarva vid pretya bhāva ādi pratiṣedhavat atīndriyāṇām arthānām virodhasya aprasiddhitaḥ bādhya bādhaka bhāvaḥ kaḥ syātām yad yukti saṃvidau tādṛśaḥ anupalabdha īḥ ced ucyatām sā eva sādhanam aniścaya karam proktam īdṛś kva anupalambhanam tatra atyanta parokṣeṣu sat asat tā viniścayau bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ api vā dharmaḥ sa viruddhaḥ prayujyate yathā agniḥ ahime sādhye sattā vā janma bādhanī yathā vastu eva vastūnām sādhane sādhanam matam tathā vastu eva vastūnām sva nivṛttau nivartakam etena kalpanā nyastaḥ yatra kvacana sambhavāt dharmaḥ pakṣasa pakṣa anyataratva ādiḥ apoditaḥ tatra api vyāpakaḥ dharmaḥ nivṛtteḥ gamakaḥ mataḥ vyāpyasya sva nivṛttiḥ ced paricchinnā kathaṃcana yad apramāṇa tā abhāve liṅgam tasya eva kathyate tad atyanta vimūḍha artham āgopālam asaṃvṛtteḥ etāvat niścaya phalam abhāve anupalambhanam tad ca hetau svabhāve vā adṛśye dṛśya tayā mate anumānāt anitya ādeḥ grahaṇe ayam kramaḥ mataḥ prāmāṇyam eva na anyatra gṛhīta grahaṇān matam na anyāḥ yā anitya tā bhāvāt pūrva siddhaḥ sa ca indriyāt na aneka rūpaḥ vācyaḥ asau vācyaḥ dharmaḥ vikalpa jaḥ sāmānya āśraya saṃsiddhau sāmānyam siddham eva tad tad asiddhau tathā asya eva hi anumānam pravartate kvacid tad aparijñānam sadṛśa apara sambhavāt bhrānteḥ apaśyataḥ bhedam māyā golaka bhedavat tathā hi aliṅgam ābālam asaṃśliṣṭa uttara udayam paśyan paricchinatti eva dīpa ādi nāśinam janaḥ bhāva svabhāva bhūtāyām api śaktau phale adṛśaḥ anānantaryataḥ mohaḥ viniścetuḥ apāṭavāt tasya eva vinivṛtty artham anumāna upavarṇanam vyayasyanti īkṣaṇāt eva sarva ākārān mahā dhiyaḥ vyāvṛtteḥ sarvatas tasmin vyāvṛtti vinibandhanāḥ buddhayaḥ arthe pravartante abhinne bhinna āśrayā iva yathā codanam ākhyāś ca saḥ asati bhrānti kāraṇe pratibhāḥ pratisandhatte sva anurūpāḥ svabhāvataḥ siddhaḥ atra api athavā dhvaṃsaḥ liṅgāt anupalambhanāt prāk bhūtvā hi abhavat bhāvaḥ anitya iti abhidhīyate yasya ubhaya anta vyavadhi sattā sambandha vācinī anitya tā śruti s tena tāvantau iti kau smṛtau prāk paścāt api abhāvaḥ ced sa eva anitya tā na kim ṣaṣṭhī ādy ayogāt iti ced antayoḥ sa katham bhavet sattā sambandhayoḥ dhrauvyād antābhyām na viśeṣaṇam aviśeṣaṇam eva syāt antau ced kārya kāraṇe asambandhān na bhāvasya prāk abhāvam sa vāñchati tad upādhi samākhyāne te api asya ca na sidhyataḥ sattā sva kāraṇa aśleṣa karaṇāt kāraṇam kila sā sattā sa ca sambandhaḥ nityau kāryam atha iha kim yasya abhāvaḥ kriyeta asau na bhāvaḥ prāk abhāvavān sambandha anabhyupagamān nityam viśvam idam tatas tasmāt anartha as kandinyaḥ abhinna artha abhimateṣu api śabdeṣu vācya bhedinyaḥ vyatirekāḥ padam dhiyaḥ viśeṣa pratyabhijñānam na pratikṣaṇa bhedataḥ na vā viśeṣa viṣayam dṛṣṭa sāmyena tad grahāt nidarśanam tad eva iti sāmānya agrahaṇam yadi nidarśana tvāt siddhasya pramāṇena asya kim punar vismṛta tvāt adoṣaḥ ced tad eva anidarśanam dṛṣṭe tad bhāva siddhiḥ ced pramāṇāt anya vastuni tadtva ārope viparyāsas tad siddheḥ apramāṇa tā pratyakṣa itarayoḥ aikyāt eka siddhiḥ dvayoḥ api sandhīyamānam ca anyena vyavasāyam smṛtim viduḥ tal liṅga apekṣaṇān naḥ ced smṛtiḥ na vyabhicārataḥ pratyakṣam kalpanā apoḍham pratyakṣeṇa eva sidhyati pratyātma vedyaḥ sarveṣām vikalpaḥ nāma saṃśrayaḥ saṃhṛtya sarvatas cintām stimitena antara ātmanā sthitaḥ api cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate sā akṣa jā matiḥ punar vikalpayan kiṃcid āsīn me kalpanā īdṛśī icchā ca iti na pūrva ukta avasthāyām indriyāt gatau ekatra dṛṣṭaḥ bhedaḥ hi kvacid na anyatra dṛśyate na tasmāt bhinnam asti anyat sāmānyam buddhy abhedataḥ tasmāt viśeṣa viṣayā sarvā eva indriya jā matiḥ na viśeṣeṣu śabdānām saṃketasya apravṛttitaḥ ananvayāt viśeṣāṇām saṃketasya apravṛttitaḥ viṣayaḥ yaḥ ca śabdānām saṃyojyeta sa eva taiḥ asya idam iti sambandhe yauv arthau pratibhāsinau tayoḥ eva hi sambandhaḥ na tadā indriya gocaraḥ viśada pratibhāsasya tadā arthasya avibhāvanāt vijñāna ābhāsa bhedaḥ ca padārthānām viśeṣakaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ artha avabhāse api yam paraḥ asya iti śaṃsati sa eva yojyate śabdaiḥ n na khalu indriya gocaraḥ avyāvṛta indriyasya anya vāc mātreṇa avibhāvanāt na ca anudita sambandhaḥ svayam jñāna prasaṅgataḥ manasā ūr yugapad vṛtteḥ sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ vimūḍhaḥ laghu vṛtteḥ vā tayoḥ aikyam vyayasyati vikalpa vyavadhānena vicchinnam darśanam bhavet iti ced bhinna jātīya vikalpe anyasya vā katham alāta dṛṣṭivat bhāva pakṣaḥ ced balavān mataḥ anyatra api samānam tad varṇayoḥ vā sakṛc śrutiḥ sakṛt saṃgata sarva artheṣu indriyeṣu iha satsu api pañcabhiḥ vyavadhāne api bhāti avyavahita iva yā sā matiḥ nāma paryanta kṣaṇika jñāna miśraṇāt vicchinna ābhā iti tad citram tasmāt santu sakṛt dhiyaḥ pratibhāsa aviśeṣaḥ ca sā antara anantare katham śuddhe manaḥ vikalpe ca na krama grahaṇam bhavet yaḥ agrahaḥ saṃgate api arthe kvacid āsakta cetasaḥ saktyā anya utpatti vaiguṇyāt codyam vā etad dvayoḥ api śīghra vṛtteḥ alāta ādeḥ anvaya pratighātinī cakra bhrāntim dṛśā dhatte na dṛśām ghaṭanena sā kecid indriya jatva ādeḥ bāla dhīvat akalpanām āhuḥ bālā vikalpe ca hetum saṃketa manda tām teṣām pratyakṣam eva syāt bālānām avikalpanāt saṃketa upāya vigamāt paścāt api bhavet na saḥ manaḥ avyutpanna saṃketam asti tena sa ced mataḥ evam indriya je api syāt śeṣavat ca idam īdṛśam yad eva sādhanam bāle tad eva atra api kathyatām sāmyāt akṣa dhiyām uktam anena anubhava ādikam viśeṣaṇam viśeṣyam ca sambandham laukikīm sthitim gṛhītvā saṃkalayya etad tathā pratyeti na anyathā yathā daṇḍini jāty ādeḥ vivekena anirūpaṇāt tadvatā yojanā na asti kalpanā api atra na asti atas yadi api anvayi vijñānam śabda vyakti avabhāsi tad varṇa ākṛty akṣara ākāra śūnyam gaḥ tvam hi varṇyate samāna tve api tasya eva na īkṣaṇam netra gocaram pratibhāsa dvaya abhāvāt buddheḥ bhedaḥ ca durlabhaḥ samavāya agrahāt akṣaiḥ sambandha adarśanam sthitam paṭas tantuṣu iha iti ādi śabdāḥ ca ime svayam kṛtāḥ śṛṅgaṅ gavi iti loke syāt śṛṅge gauḥ iti alaukikam gava ākhya pariśiṣṭa aṅga viccheda anupalambhanāt taiḥ tantubhiḥ iyam śāṭi iti uttaram kāryam ucyate tantu saṃskāra sambhūtam na eka kālam kathaṃcana kāraṇa āropataḥ kaścid eka apodhārataḥ api vā tantu ākhyām vartayet kārye darśayan na āśrayam śruteḥ upakārya upakāri tvam vicchedāt dṛṣṭiḥ eva vā mukhyam yad askhala j jñānam ādi saṃketa gocaraḥ anumānam ca jāty ādau vastunaḥ na asti bhedini sarvatra vyapadeśaḥ hi daṇḍa ādeḥ api sāṃvṛtāt vastu prāsāda mālā ādi śabdāḥ ca anya anapekṣiṇaḥ gehaḥ yadi api saṃyoga s tad mālā kim nu tad bhavet jātiḥ ced geha ekaḥ api mālā iti ucyeta vṛkṣavat mālā bahu tve tad śabdaḥ katham jāteḥ ajātitas mālā ādau ca mahattva ādiḥ iṣṭaḥ yaḥ ca aupacārikaḥ mukhya aviśiṣṭa vijñāna grāhya tvān na aupacārikaḥ ananya hetu tā tulyā sā mukhya abhimateṣu api padārtha śabdaḥ kam hetum anyam ṣaṭkam samīkṣate yaḥ yathā rūḍhitaḥ siddha s tad sāmya ādya s tathā ucyate mukhyaḥ gauṇaḥ ca bhāveṣu api abhāvasya upacārataḥ saṃketa anvayinī rūḍhiḥ vaktuḥ icchā anvayī ca saḥ kriyate vyavahāra artham chandaḥ śabda aṃśa nāmavat vastu dharma tayā eva artha as tādṛś vijñāna kāraṇam bhede api yatra tad jñānāt tad tathā pratipadyate jñānāni api tathā bhede abheda pratyavamarśane iti etad kārya viśleṣasya anvayaḥ na eka vastunaḥ vastūnām vidyate tasmāt tad niṣṭhā vastuni śrutiḥ bāhya śakti vyavaccheda niṣṭhā abhāve api tad śrutiḥ vikalpa pratibimbeṣu tad niṣṭheṣu nibadhyate tatas anya apoha niṣṭha tvāt uktā anya apoha kṛc śrutiḥ vyatirekī iva yaj jñāne bhāti artha pratibimbakam śabdāt tad api na artha ātmā bhrāntiḥ sā vāsanā udbhavā tasya abhidhāne śrutibhiḥ arthe kaḥ aṃśaḥ avagamyate tasya agatau ca saṃketa kriyā vyarthā tad arthikā śabdaḥ artha aṃśakam āha iti tatra anya apoha ucyate ākāraḥ sa ca na arthe asti tam vadan artha bhāj katham śabdasya anvayinaḥ kāryam arthena anvayinā sa ca ananvayī dhiyaḥ abhedāt darśana abhyāsa nirmitaḥ tad rūpa āropa gatyā anya vyāvṛtta adhigateḥ punar śabda arthaḥ arthaḥ sa eva iti vacanena virudhyate mithyā avabhāsinaḥ vā ete pratyayāḥ śabda nirmitāḥ anuyānti imam artha aṃśam iti vā apoha kṛc śrutiḥ tasmāt saṃketa kāle api nirdiṣṭa arthena saṃyutaḥ sva prati iti phalena anya apohaḥ sambandhyate śrutau anyatra adṛṣṭy apekṣa tvāt kvacid tad dṛṣṭy apekṣaṇāt śrutau sambadhyate apohaḥ na etad vastuni yujyate tasmāt jāty ādi tad yogā na arthe teṣu ca na śrutiḥ saṃyojyate anya vyāvṛttau śabdānām eva yojanāt saṃketa smaraṇa upāyam dṛṣṭa saṃkalana ātmakam pūrva apara parāmarśa śūnye tad cākṣuṣe katham anyatra gata cittaḥ api cakṣuṣā rūpam īkṣate tad saṃketa agrahas tatra spaṣṭa s tad jā ca kalpanā jāyante kalpanāḥ tatra yatra śabdaḥ niveśitaḥ tena icchātaḥ pravarteran na īkṣeran bāhyam akṣa jāḥ rūpam rūpam iti īkṣeta tad dhiyam kim iti īkṣate asti ca anubhavas tasyāḥ saḥ avikalpaḥ katham bhavet tasya eva anubhave dṛṣṭam na vikalpa dvayam sakṛt etena tulya kāla anya vijñāna anubhavaḥ gataḥ smṛtiḥ bhavet atīte ca sā agṛhīte katham bhavet syāt ca anya dhī paricchedā abhinna rūpā sva buddhi dhīḥ atītam apadṛṣṭāntam aliṅgam ca artha darśanam siddham tad kena tasmin hi na pratyakṣam na laiṅgikam tad svarūpa avabhāsinyā buddhyā anantarayā yadi rūpa ādiḥ iva gṛhyeta na syāt tad pūrva dhī grahaḥ saḥ avikalpaḥ sva viṣayaḥ vijñāna anubhavaḥ yathā aśakya samayam tadvat anyat api avikalpakaḥ sāmānya vācinaḥ śabdāḥ tad eka arthā ca kalpanā abhāve nirvikalpasya viśeṣa adhigamaḥ katham asti ced nirvikalpam ca kiṃcid tad tulya hetukam sarvan tathā eva hetoḥ hi bhedāt bhedaḥ phala ātmanām anapekṣita bāhya artha yojanā samaya smṛteḥ tathā anapekṣya samayam vastu śaktyā eva netra dhīḥ saṃketa smaraṇa apekṣam rūpam yadi akṣa cetasi anapekṣya na ced śakyam syāt smṛtau eva liṅgavat tasya as tad saṃgama utpatteḥ akṣa dhīḥ syāt smṛteḥ na vā tatas kāla antare api syāt kvacid vyākṣepa sambhavāt krameṇa ubhaya hetuḥ ced prāk eva syāt abhedataḥ anyaḥ akṣa buddhi hetuḥ ced smṛti s tatra api anarthikā yathā samita siddhy artham iṣyate samaya smṛtiḥ bhedaḥ ca asamitaḥ grāhyaḥ smṛti s tatra kim arthikā sāmānya mātra grahaṇe bheda apekṣā na yujyate tasmāt cakṣuḥ ca rūpām ca pratītya udeti netra dhīḥ sākṣāt ced jñāna janane samarthaḥ viṣayaḥ akṣavat atha kasmāt dvaya adhīna janma tad tena na ucyate samīkṣya gamaka tvam hi vyapadeśaḥ na gṛhyate tad ca akṣa vyapadeśe asti tad dharmaś ca niyojyatām tatas liṅga svabhāvaḥ atra vyapadeśe niyojyatām nivartate avyāpakasya svabhāvasya nivṛttitaḥ saṃcitaḥ samudāyaḥ sāmānyam tatra ca akṣa dhīḥ sāmānya buddhiḥ ca avaśyam vikalpena anubudhyate artha antara abhisambandhāt jāyante ye aṇavaḥ apare uktā as te saṃcitā as te hi nimittām jñāna janmanaḥ aṇūnām sa viśeṣaḥ ca na antareṇa aparān aṇūn tad eka aniyamāj jñānam uktam sāmānya gocaram atha eka āyatana tve api na anekam dṛśyate sakṛt sakṛt graha avabhāsaḥ kim viyukteṣu tila ādiṣu pratyuktam lāghavam ca atra teṣu eva krama pātiṣu kim na akrama grahas tulya kālāḥ sarvāḥ ca buddhayaḥ kāścid tāsu akrama ābhāsāḥ kramavatyaḥ aparāḥ ca kim sarva artha grahaṇe tasmāt akramaḥ ayam prasajyate na ekam citra pataṃga ādi rūpam vā dṛśyate katham citram tad ekam iti ced idam citrataram tatas na ekam svabhāvam citram hi maṇi rūpam yathā eva tad nīla ādi pratibhāsaḥ ca tulya ś citra paṭa ādiṣu tatra avayava rūpam ced kevalam dṛśyate tathā nīla ādīni nirasya anya t citram citram yad īkṣase tulya artha ākāra kāla tve na upalakṣitayoḥ dhiyoḥ nānā arthā kramavatyā ekā kim eka arthā akramā aparā vaiśvarūpya āt dhiyām eva bhāvānām viśva rūpa tā tad ced anaṅgam kena iyam siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ vijātīnām anārambhān na ālekhya ādau vicitra dhīḥ arūpa tvāt na saṃyogaḥ citraḥ bhakteḥ ca na āśrayaḥ pratyekam avicitra tvāt gṛhīteṣu krameṇa ca na citra dhī saṃkalanam anekasya ekayā agrahāt nānā arthā ekā bhavet tasmāt siddhāntaḥ api avikalpikā vikalpayan api eka artham yatas anyat api paśyati citra avabhāseṣu artheṣu yadi eka tvam na yujyate sā eva tāvat katham buddhiḥ ekā citra avabhāsinī idam vastu bala āyātam yad vadanti vipaścitaḥ yathā yathārthāḥ cintyante viśīryante tathā tathā kim syāt sā citra tā ekasyām na syāt tasyām matauv api yadi idam svayam arthānām rocate tatra ke vayam tasmāt na artheṣu na jñāne sthūla bhāsaḥ tad ātmanaḥ ekatra pratiṣiddha tvāt bahuṣu api na sambhavaḥ paricchedaḥ antar anyaḥ ayam bhāgaḥ bahis iva sthitaḥ jñānasya abhedinaḥ bheda pratibhāsaḥ hi upaplavaḥ tatra ekasya api abhāvena dvayam api avahīyate tasmāt tad eva tasya api tattvam yā dvaya śūnyatā tad bheda āśrayiṇī ca iyam bhāvānām bheda saṃsthitiḥ tad upaplava bhāve ca teṣām bhedaḥ api upaplavaḥ na grāhya grāhaka ākāra bāhyam asti ca lakṣaṇam atas lakṣaṇa śūnya tvāt niḥsvabhāvāḥ prakāśitāḥ vyāpāra upādhikam sarvam skandha ādīnām viśeṣataḥ lakṣaṇam sa ca tattvam na tena api ete vilakṣaṇāḥ yathā sva pratyaya apekṣāt avidyā upapluta ātmanām vijñaptiḥ vitatha ākārā jāyate timira ādivat asaṃvidita tad tvā ca sā sarva apara darśanaiḥ asambhavāt vinā teṣām grāhya grāhaka viplavaiḥ tad upekṣita tadtva arthaiḥ kṛtvā gaja nimīlanam kevalam loka buddhyā eva bāhya cintā pratanyate nīla ādiś citra vijñāne jñāna upādhiḥ ananya bhāj aśakya darśana s tam hi patati arthe vivecayan yad yathā bhāsate jñānam tad tathā eva prakāśate iti nāma eka bhāvaḥ syāt citra ākārasya cetasi paṭa ādi rūpasya ekatve tathā syāt aviveki tā vivekī na vivakṣā anyat avivekī ca na īkṣate kaḥ vā virodhaḥ bahavaḥ saṃjāta atiśayāḥ pṛthak bhaveyuḥ kāraṇam buddheḥ yadi na ātma indriya ādivat hetu bhāvāt ṛte na anyā grāhyatā nāma kācana tatra buddhiḥ yad ābhāsā tasya as tad grāhyam ucyate katham vā avayavī grāhyaḥ sakṛt sva avayavaiḥ saha na hi gaḥ pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sāsnā ādīnām adarśane guṇa pradhāna adhigamaḥ saha api abhimataḥ yadi sampūrṇa aṅgaḥ na gṛhyeta sakṛn na api guṇa ādimān vivakṣā paratantra tvāt viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyayoḥ yad aṅga bhāvena upāttan tad tena eva hi gṛhyate svatas vastu antara abhedāt guṇa ādeḥ bhedakasya ca agrahāt bheda buddhiḥ syāt paśyataḥ api apara aparam guṇa ādi bheda grahaṇān nānātva pratipad yadi astu nāma tathā api eṣām bhavet sambandhi saṃkaraḥ śabda ādīnām aneka tvāt siddhaḥ aneka grahaḥ sakṛt saṃniveśa graha ayogāt agrahe saṃniveśinām sarvatas vinivṛttasya vinivṛttiḥ yatas yatas tad bheda unnīta bhedaḥ asau dharmiṇaḥ aneka rūpa tā te kalpitā rūpa bhedā nirvikalpasya cetasaḥ na vicitrasya citra ābhāḥ kādācid kasya gocaraḥ yadi api asti sitatva ādiḥ yādṛś indriya gocaraḥ na saḥ abhidhīyate śabdaiḥ jñānayaḥ rūpa bhedataḥ eka artha tve api buddhīnām nānā āśrayatā sa ced śrotṛ ādi cittāni idānīm bhinna arthāni iti tad kutas jātaḥ nāma āśrayaḥ anyonyaḥ cetasām tasya vastunaḥ ekasya eva kutaḥ rūpam bhinna ākāra avabhāsi tad vṛtteḥ dṛśya aparāmarśena abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ darśanāt pratyabhijñānam gava ādīnām nivāritam anvayāt ca anumānam yad abhidhāna vikalpayoḥ dṛśye gava ādau jāty ādeḥ tad api etena dūṣitam darśanāni eva bhinnāni api ekām kurvanti kalpanām pratyabhijñāna saṃkhyātām svabhāvena iti varṇitam pūrva anubhūta grahaṇe mānasasya apramāṇa tā adṛṣṭa grahaṇe andha ādeḥ api syāt artha darśanam kṣaṇika tvāt atītasya darśane ca na sambhavaḥ vācyam akṣaṇika tve syāl lakṣaṇam sa viśeṣaṇam niṣpādita kriye kaṃcid viśeṣam asamādadhat karmaṇi aindriyam anyat vā sādhanam kim iti iṣyate sakṛt bhāvaḥ ca sarvāsām dhiyām tad bhāva janmanām anyaiḥ akārya bhedasya tad apekṣa avirodhataḥ tasmāt indriya vijñāna anantara pratyaya udbhavaḥ manaḥ anyam eva gṛhṇāti viṣayam na andha dṛś tatas sva artha anvaya artha apekṣā eva hetuḥ indriya jā matiḥ tatas anya grahaṇe api asya niyata grāhyatā matā tad atulya kriyā kālaḥ katham sva jñāna kālikaḥ sahakāri bhavet artha iti ced akṣa cetasaḥ asataḥ prāk asāmarthyāt paścāt ca anupayogataḥ prāgbhāvaḥ sarva hetūnām na atas arthaḥ sva dhiyā saha bhinna kālam katham grāhyam iti ced grāhyatām viduḥ hetu tvam eva yukti jñā jñāna ākāra arpaṇa kṣamam kāryam hi aneka hetu tve api anukurvat udeti yad tad tena arpita tad rūpam gṛhītam iti ca ucyate aśakya samayaḥ hi ātmā rāga ādīnām ananya bhāj teṣām atas sva saṃvittiḥ na abhijalpa anuṣaṅgiṇī avedakāḥ parasya api te svarūpam katham viduḥ eka artha āśrayiṇā vedyā vijñānena iti kecana tad atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ tad sukha ādi kim ajñānam vijñāna abhinna hetu jam sā arthe sati indriye yogye yathāsvam api cetasi dṛṣṭam janma sukha ādīnām tad tulyam manasām api asatsu satsu ca eteṣu na janma ajanma vā kvacid dṛṣṭam sukha ādeḥ buddheḥ vā ta tatas na anyatas ca te sukha duḥkha ādi bhedaḥ ca teṣām eva viśeṣataḥ tasyāḥ eva yathā buddheḥ māndya pāṭava saṃśrayāḥ yasya arthasya nipātena te jātā dhī sukha ādayaḥ tam muktvā pratipadyeta sukha ādīn eva sā katham avicchinnā na bhāseta tad saṃvittiḥ krama grahe tal lāghavāc ced tad tulyam iti asaṃvedanam na kim na ca ekayā dvaya jñānam niyamāt akṣa cetasaḥ sukha ādy abhāve api arthāc ca jāteḥ tad śakty asiddhitaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ca sāmarthye dvayoḥ nīla ādivat sukham gṛhyeta kevalam tasya tad hetv artham agṛhṇataḥ na hi saṃvedanam yuktam arthena eva saha grahe kim sāmarthyam sukha ādīnām na iṣṭā dhīḥ yad tad udbhavā vinā arthena sukha ādīnām vedane cakṣuḥ ādibhiḥ rūpa ādiḥ stry ādi bhedaḥ akṣaṇā na gṛhyeta kadācana na hi sati antaraṅge arthe śakteḥ dhīḥ bāhya darśanī artha grahe sukha ādīnām tad jānām syāt avedanam dhiyoḥ yugapad utpattau tad tad viṣaya sambhavāt sukha duḥkha vidau syātām sakṛt arthasya sambhave sati āntare api upādāne jñāne duḥkha ādi sambhavaḥ na upādānam viruddhasya tad ca ekam iti ced matam avijñānasya vijñānam kena upādāna kāraṇam ādhipatyam tu kurvīta tad viruddhe api dṛśyate akṣṇoḥ yathā eka ālokaḥ naktaṃcara tad anyayoḥ rūpa darśana vaiguṇya avaiguṇye kurute sakṛt tasmāt sukha ādayaḥ arthānām sva saṃkrānta avabhāsinām vedakāḥ sva ātmanaḥ ca eṣām arthebhyaḥ janma kevalam artha ātmā sva ātma bhūtaḥ hi teṣām taiḥ anubhūyate tena artha anubhava khyātiḥ ālambas tu tad ābhatā kaścid bahis sthitān eva sukha ādīn apracetanān grāhyān āha na tasya api sakṛt yuktaḥ dvaya grahaḥ sukha ādy abhinna rūpa tvāt nīla ādeś ced sakṛt grahaḥ bhinna avabhāsinoḥ grāhyam cetasos tad abhedi kim tasya aviśeṣe bāhyasya bhāvanā tāratamyataḥ tāratamyam ca buddhau syāt na prīti paritāpayoḥ sukha ādy ātma tayā buddheḥ api yadi avirodhitā sa idānīm katham bāhyaḥ sukha ādy ātmā iti gamyate agrāhya grāhaka tvāt ced bhinna jātīyayoḥ agrāhakaḥ syāt sarvasya tatas hīyeta bhoktṛtā kārya kāraṇa tā anena pratyukta akārya kāraṇe grāhya grāhaka tā abhāvāt bhāve anyatra api sā bhavet tasmāt ta āntarā eva saṃvedya tvāt ca cetanāḥ saṃvedanam na yad rūpam na hi tad tasya vedanam atat svabhāvaḥ anubhavaḥ bauddhāṃ tān samavaiti ced muktvā adhyakṣa smṛta ākārām saṃvittim buddhiḥ atra kā tān tān artha anupādāya sukha duḥkha ādi vedanam ekam āvirbhavat dṛṣṭam na dṛṣṭam tu anyat antarā saṃsargāt avibhāgaḥ ced ayaḥ golaka vahnivat bheda abheda vyavasthā evam ucchinnā sarva vastuṣu abhinna vedanasya aikye yad na evam tad vibhedavat sidhyet asādhana tve asya na siddham bheda sādhanam bhinna ābhaḥ sita duḥkha ādiḥ abhinnaḥ buddhi vedane abhinna ābhe vibhinne ced bheda abhedau kim āśrayau tiraskṛtānām paṭunā api ekadā bheda darśanāt pravāhe vitti bhedānām siddhā bheda vyavasthitiḥ prāk uktam yoginām jñānam teṣām tad bhāvanām ayam vidhūta kalpanā jālam spaṣṭam eva avabhāsate kāma śoka bhaya unmāda caura svapna ādy upaplutāḥ abhūtān api paśyanti puratas avasthitān iva na vikalpa anubaddhasya spaṣṭa artha pratibhāsitā svapne api smaryate smārtam ca tad tādṛś arthavat aśubhā pṛthivī kṛtsna ādy abhūtam api varṇyate spaṣṭa ābham nirvikalpam ca bhāvanā bala nirmitam tasmāt bhūtam abhūtam vā yad yad eva abhibhāvyate bhāvanā pariniṣpattau tad sphuṭa akalpa dhī phalam tatra pramāṇam saṃvādi yad prāṅ nirṇīta vastuvat tad bhāvanā jam pratyakṣam iṣṭam śeṣā upaplavāḥ śabda artha grāhi yad yatra tad jñānam tatra kalpanā svarūpam ca na śabda artha s tatra adhyakṣam atas akhilam trividham kalpanā jñānam āśraya upaplava udbhavam avikalpakam ekam ca pratyakṣa ābham caturvidham anakṣajatva siddhy artham ukte dve bhrānti darśanāt siddha anumā ādi vacanam sādhanāya eva pūrvayoḥ saṃketa saṃśraya anya artha samāropa vikalpane pratyakṣa asan nivṛtti tvāt kadācid bhrānti kāraṇam yathā eva iyam parokṣa artha kalpanā smaraṇa ādikā samaya apekṣiṇī na artham pratyakṣam pratyavasyati tathā anubhūta smaraṇam antareṇa ghaṭa ādiṣu na pratyayaḥ anuyaṃ tad ca pratyakṣāt parihīyate apavādaḥ caturthaḥ atra tena uktam upaghāta jam kevalam tatra timiram upaghāta upalakṣaṇam mānasam tad api iti eke teṣām granthaḥ virudhyate nīla dvi candra ādi dhiyām hetuḥ akṣāṇi api iti ayam pāraṃparyeṇa hetuḥ ced indriya jñāna gocare vicāryamāṇe prastāvaḥ mānasasya iha kīdṛśaḥ kim vā aindriyam yad akṣāṇām bhāva abhāva anurodhi ced tad tulyam vikriyā vac ced sā iva iyam kim niṣidhyate sarpa ādi bhrānti vac ca asyāḥ syāt akṣa vikṛtau api nivṛttiḥ na nivarteta nivṛtte api akṣa viplave kadācid anya santāne tathā eva api eta vācakaiḥ dṛṣṭa smṛtim apekṣeta na bhāseta parisphuṭam suptasya jāgrataḥ vā api yā eva dhīḥ sphuṭa bhāsinī sā nirvikalpa ubhayathā api anyathā eva vikalpikā tasmāt tasya avikalpe api prāmāṇyam pratiṣidhyate visaṃvādāt tad artham ca pratyakṣa ābham dvidhā uditam kriyā sādhanam iti eva sarvam sarvasya karmaṇaḥ sādhanam na hi tad tasyāḥ sādhanam yā kriyā yatas tatra anubhava mātreṇa jñānasya sadṛśa ātmanaḥ bhāvyam tena ātmanā yena pratikarma vibhajyate anātma bhūtaḥ bhedaḥ asya vidyamānaḥ api hetuṣu bhinne karmaṇi abhinnasya na bhedena niyāmakaḥ tasmāt yatas asya ātma bhedaḥ asya adhigatiḥ iti ayam kriyāyāḥ karma niyamaḥ siddhā sā tad prasādhanā arthena ghaṭayati enām na hi muktvā artha rūpa tām anyaḥ sva bheda at jñānasya bhedakaḥ api kathaṃcana tasmāt prameya adhigateḥ sādhanam meya rūpa tā sādhane anyatra tad karma sambandhaḥ na prasidhyati sā ca tasya ātma bhūtā eva tena na artha antaram phalam dadhānam tad ca tām ātmani artha adhigamana ātmanā savya apāram iva ābhāti vyāpāreṇa sva karmaṇi tad vaśāt tad vyavasthānāt akārakam api svayam yathā phalasya hetūnām sadṛśa ātma tayā udbhavāt hetu rūpa grahaḥ loke kriyāvat tve api kathyate ālocanā akṣa sambandha viśeṣaṇa dhiyāmataḥ na iṣṭam prāmāṇyam eteṣām vyavadhānāt kriyām prati sarveṣām upayoge api kārakāṇām kriyām prati yad antyam bhedakam tasya as tad sādhakatamam matam sarva sāmānya hetu tvāt akṣāṇām asti na īdṛśam tad bhede api hi abhinnasya tasya idam iti tad kutas etena śeṣam vyākhyātam viśeṣaṇa dhiyām punar atādrūpye na bhedaḥ api tadvat anya dhiyaḥ api vā na iṣṭaḥ viṣaya bhedaḥ api kriyā sādhanayoḥ dvayoḥ eka artha tve dvayam vyartham na ca syāt krama bhāvitā sādhya sādhana tā bhāvaḥ sakṛt bhāve dhiyaḥ aṃśayoḥ tad vyavasthā āśraya tvena sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ sarva ātmanā api sambaddham kaiścid eva avagamyate dharmaiḥ sa niyamaḥ na syāt sambandhasya aviśeṣatas tad abhede api bhedaḥ ayam yasmāt tasya pramāṇa tā saṃskārāt ced atādrūpye na tasya api avyavasthiteḥ kriyā karaṇayoḥ aikya virodha iti ced asat dharma bheda abhyupagamāt vastu abhinnam iti iṣyate evaṃprakārā sarvā eva kriyā kāraka saṃsthitiḥ bhāve hi abhinna abhimateṣu adhyāropeṇa vṛttitaḥ kā artha saṃvid yad eva idam pratyakṣam prativedanam tad artha vedanam kena tādrūpyāt vyabhicāri tad atha saḥ anubhavaḥ kva asya tad eva idam vicāryate sarūpavanti tad kena sthūla ābhāsaḥ ca te aṇavaḥ tad na artha rūpa tā tasya satya artha avyabhicāriṇī tad saṃvedana bhāvasya na samarthā prasādhane tad sārūpya tad utpattī yadi saṃvedya lakṣaṇam saṃvedyam syāt samāna artham vijñānam samanantaram idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vedam iti yatra avasāya dhīḥ sa tasya anubhavaḥ sā eva pratyāsattiḥ vicāryate dṛśya darśanayoḥ yena tasya tad sādhanam matam tayoḥ sambandham āśritya draṣṭuḥ eṣa viniścayaḥ ātmā sa tasya anubhavaḥ sa ca na anyasya kasyacid pratyakṣa prativedya tvam api tasya tad ātma tā na anyaḥ anubhāvya s tena asti tasya na anubhavaḥ paraḥ tasya api tulya codyatvāt svayam sā eva prakāśate nīla ādi rūpas tasya asau svabhāvaḥ anubhavaḥ ca saḥ nīla ādy anubhavaḥ khyātaḥ svarūpa anubhavaḥ api san prakāśamānaḥ tādātmyāt svarūpasya prakāśakaḥ yathā prakāśaḥ abhimata s tathā dhīḥ ātma vedinī tasya āś ca artha antare vedye durghaṭau vedya vedakau avedya vedaka ākārā yathā bhrāntaiḥ nirīkṣyate vibhakta lakṣaṇa grāhya grāhaka ākāra viplavā tathā akṛta vyavasthā iyam keśa ādi jñāna bhedavat yadā tadā na saṃcodya grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇā tadā anya saṃvidaḥ abhāvāt sva saṃvid phalam iṣyate yadi bāhyaḥ anubhūyeta kaḥ doṣaḥ na eva kaścana idam eva kim uktam syāt sa bāhyaḥ arthaḥ anubhūyeta yadi buddhi s tad ākārā sā asti ākāra niveśinī sā bāhyāt anyatas vā iti vicāram idam arhati darśana upādhi rahitasya agrahāt tad grahe grahāt darśanam nīla nirbhāsam na arthaḥ bāhyaḥ asti kevalaḥ kasyacid kiṃcid eva antar vāsanāyāḥ prabodhakam tatas dhiyām viniyamaḥ na bāhya artha vyapekṣayā tasmāt dvi rūpam asti ekam yad evam anubhūyate smaryate ca ubhaya ākārasya asya saṃvedanam phalam yadā niṣpanna tad bhāva iṣṭaḥ aniṣṭaḥ api vā paraḥ vijñapti hetuḥ viṣaya s tasya āś ca anubhavas tathā yadā sa viṣayam jñānam jñāna aṃśe artha vyavasthiteḥ tadā ya ātma anubhavaḥ sa eva artha viniścayaḥ yadi iṣṭa ākāra ātmā syāt anyathā vā anubhūyate iṣṭaḥ aniṣṭaḥ api vā tena bhavati arthaḥ praveditaḥ vidyamāne api bāhya arthe yathā anubhavam eva saḥ niścita ātmā sva rūpeṇa na aneka ātmatva doṣataḥ yadi bāhyam na vidyeta kasya saṃvedanam bhavet yadi agatyā svarūpasya bāhyasya eva na kim matam abhyupāye api bhedena na syāt anubhavaḥ dvayoḥ adṛṣṭa āvaraṇān naḥ ced na nāma artha vaśā gatiḥ tam aneka ātmakam bhāvam eka ātma tvena darśayet tad adṛṣṭam katham nāma bhavet arthasya vedakam iṣṭa aniṣṭa avabhāsinyaḥ kalpanā na akṣa dhīḥ yadi aniṣṭa ādau asandhānam dṛṣṭam tatra api cetasām tasmāt prameye bāhye api yuktam sva anubhavaḥ phalam yatas svabhāvaḥ asya yathā tathā eva artha viniścayaḥ tadā artha ābhāsatā eva asya pramāṇam na tu san api grāhaka ātmā apara artha tvāt bāhyeṣu artheṣu apekṣyate yasmāt yathā niviṣṭaḥ asau artha ātmā pratyaye tathā niścīyate niviṣṭaḥ asau evam iti ātma saṃvidaḥ iti artha saṃvid sā eva iṣṭā yatas artha ātmā na dṛśyate tasyāḥ buddhi niveśya arthaḥ sādhanam tasya sā kriyā yathā niviśate saḥ arthaḥ tathā hi sa prakāśate artha sthiteḥ tad ātma tvāt sva vid api arthavin matā tasmāt viṣaya bhedaḥ api na sva saṃvedanam phalam uktam svabhāva cintāyām tādātmyāt artha saṃvidaḥ tathā avabhāsamānasya tādṛśaḥ anya adṛśaḥ api vā jñānasya hetuḥ arthaḥ api iti arthasya iṣṭā prameya tā yathā kathaṃcid na asya artha rūpam yuktyā avabhāsinaḥ avibhāgaḥ api buddhy ātma viparyāsita darśanaiḥ grāhya grāhaka saṃvitti bhedavān iva lakṣyate mantra ādy upapluta akṣāṇām yathā mṛd śakala ādayaḥ anyathā eva avabhāsante tad rūpa rahitā api tathā eva adarśanāt teṣām anupapluta cakṣuṣām dūre yathā vā maruṣu mahān alpaḥ api dṛśyate yathā anudarśanam ca iyam meya māna phala sthitiḥ kriyate avidyamānā api grāhya grāhaka saṃvidām anyathā ekasya bhāvasya nānā rūpa avabhāsinaḥ satyam katham syuḥ ākāra aḥ tad eka tvasya hānitaḥ anyasya anyatva hāneś ca na abhedaḥ arūpa darśanāt rūpa abhedam hi paśyantī dhīḥ abhedam vyavasyati bhāvā yena nirūpyante tad rūpam na asti tattvataḥ yasmāt ekam anekam vā rūpam teṣām na vidyate sādharmya darśa nāl loke bhrāntiḥ n nāma upajāyate atadātmani tādātmya vyavasāyena na iha tad adarśana at jagat yasmin ekasya api tad ātmanaḥ asti iyam api yā tu antar upaplava samudbhavā doṣa udbhavā prakṛtyā sā vitatha pratibhāsinī anapekṣita sādharmya dṛś ādis taimira ādivat tatra buddheḥ paricchedaḥ grāhaka ākāra sammataḥ tādātmyāt ātma vid tasya sa tasyāḥ sādhanam tatas tatra ātma viṣaye māne yathā rāga ādi vedanam iyam sarvatra saṃyojyā māna meya phala sthitiḥ tatra api anubhava ātma tvāt te yogyāḥ sva ātma saṃvidi iti sā yogya tā mānam ātmā meyaḥ phalam sva vid grāhaka ākāra saṃkhyātā pariccheda ātma tā ātmani sā yogya tā iti ca proktam pramāṇam sva ātma vedanam sarvam eva hi vijñānam viṣayebhyaḥ samudbhavat tad anyasya api hetu tve katham syāt viṣaya ākṛtiḥ yathā eva āhāra kāla ādeḥ hetu tve apatya janmani pitroḥ tad ekasya ākāram dhatte na anyasya kasyacid tad hetu tvena tulye api tad anya viṣayam matam viṣaya tvam tad aṅgena tad abhāve na tad bhavet anartha ākāra śaṅkā syāt api arthavati cetasi atīta artha grahe siddhe dvi rūpatva ātma vedane nīla ādy ābhāsa bheditvān na arthaḥ jātiḥ atadvatī sā vā anityā na jātiḥ syāt nityā vā janikā katham nāma ādikam niṣiddham prāṅ na ayam arthavatām kramaḥ icchā mātra anubandhi tvāt artha śaktiḥ n na sidhyati smṛtiḥ ca īdṛgvidham jñānam tasya āś ca anubhavāt bhavaḥ sa ca artha ākāra rahitaḥ sā idānīm tadvatī katham na arthāt bhāvaḥ tadā abhāvāt syāt tathā anubhave api saḥ ākāraḥ sa ca na arthasya spaṣṭa ākāra vivekataḥ vyatiriktam tam ākāram pratīyāt aparas tathā nityam ātmani sambandhe pratīyāt kathitam ca na ekā ekena abhisambandhe pratisandhiḥ na yujyate eka artha abhiniveśa ātmā pravaktṛ śrotṛ cetasoḥ tad eka vyavahāraḥ ced sādṛśyāt atad abhayoḥ bhinna ātma arthaḥ katham grāhya s tadā syāt dhīḥ anarthikā tad ca anubhava vijñānam ubhaya aṅga avalambinā eka ākāra viśeṣeṇa tad jñānena anubadhyate anyathā hi atad ākāram katham jñāne adhirohati eka ākāra uttaram jñānam tathā hi uttaram uttaram tasya artha rūpeṇa ākārauv ātma ākāraḥ ca kaścana dvitīyasya tṛtīyena jñānena hi vivicyate artha kārya tayā jñāna smṛtau artha smṛteḥ yadi bhrāntyā saṅkalanam jyotiḥ manaskāre ca sā bhavet sarveṣām api kāryāṇām kāraṇaiḥ syāt tathā grahaḥ kulāla ādi vivekena na smaryeta ghaṭas tatas yasmāt atiśayāt jñānam artha saṃsarga bhājanam sārūpyāt tad kim anyat syāt dṛṣṭeḥ ca yamala ādiṣu ādyā anubhaya rūpa tve hi eka rūpe vyavasthitam dvitīyam vyatiricyeta na parāmarśa cetasā artha saṃkalana aśleṣā dhīḥ dvitīya avalambate nīla ādi rūpeṇa dhiyam bhāsamānām puras tatas anyathā hi ādyam eva ekam saṃyojyeta artha sambhavāt jñānam na adṛṣṭa sambandham pūrva arthena uttarottaram sakṛt saṃvedyamānasya niyamena dhiyā saha viṣayasya tatas anya tvam kena ākāreṇa sidhyati bhedaḥ ca bhrānti vijñānaiḥ dṛśyeta indā iva advaye saṃvitti niyamaḥ na asti bhinnayoḥ nīla pītayoḥ na arthaḥ asaṃvedanaḥ kaścid anarthasya api vedanam dṛṣṭam saṃvedyamānam tad tayoḥ na asti viveki tā tasmāt arthasya durvāram jñāna kāla avabhāsinaḥ jñānāt avyatireki tvam hetu bheda anumā bhavet abhāvāt akṣa buddhīnām satsu api anyeṣu hetuṣu niyamam yadi na brūyāt pratyayāt samanantarāt bījāt aṅkura janma agneḥ dhūmāt siddhiḥ atīdṛśī bāhya artha āśrayiṇī yā api kāraka jñāpaka sthitiḥ sā api tad rūpa nirbhāsāḥ tathā niyata saṃgamāḥ buddhiḥ āśritya kalpyeta yadi kim vā virudhyate anagni janyaḥ dhūmaḥ syāt tad kāryāt kāraṇe agatiḥ na syāt kāraṇa tāyām vā kuta ekāntatas gatiḥ tatra api dhūma ābhāsā dhīḥ prabodha paṭu vāsanām gamayet agni nirbhāsām dhiyam eva na pāvakam tad yogya vāsanā garbha eva dhūma avabhāsinīm vyanakti citta santānaḥ dhiyam dhūmaḥ agnitas tatas asti eṣa viduṣām vādaḥ bāhyam tu āśritya varṇyate dvairūpyam saha saṃvitti niyamāt tad ca sidhyate jñānam indriya bhedena paṭu manda āvila ādikām pratibhāsa bhidām arthe bibhrad ekatra dṛśyate arthasya abhinna rūpa tvāt eka rūpam bhavet manaḥ sarvam tad artham arthāc ced tasya na asti tad ābhatā artha āśrayeṇa udbhavatas tad rūpam anukruvataḥ tasya kenacid aṃśena paratas api bhidā bhavet tathā hi āśritya pitaram tad rūpaḥ api sutaḥ pituḥ bhedam kenacid aṃśena kutaścid avalambate mayūra candraka ākāram nīla lohita bhāsvaram sampaśyanti pradīpa ādeḥ maṇḍalam manda cakṣuṣaḥ tasya tad bāhya rūpa tve kā prasanna īkṣaṇe akṣamā bhūtam paśyan ca tad darśī katham ca upahata indriyaḥ śodhitam timireṇa asya vyaktam cakṣuḥ atīndriyam paśyataḥ anya akṣa dṛśye arthe tad avyaktam katham punar āloke akṣa manaskārāt anyasya ekasya gamyate śaktiḥ hetuḥ tatas na anyaḥ ahetuḥ ca viṣayaḥ katham sa eva yadi dhī hetuḥ kim pradīpam apekṣate dīpa mātreṇa sadbhāvāt ubhayam na api kāraṇam dūra āsanna ādi bhedena vyakta avyaktam na yujyate tad syāt āloke bhedāt ced tad pidhāna apidhānayoḥ tulyā dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭiḥ vā sūkṣmaḥ aṃśas tasya kaścana ālokena na mandena dṛśyate atas bhidā yadi ekatve arthasya bāhyasya dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas aneka tve aṇuśaḥ bhinnaḥ dṛśya adṛśya bhidā kutas māndya pāṭau abhedena bhāsaḥ buddhi bhidā yadi bhinne anyasmin abhinnasya kutaḥ bhedena bhāsanam mandam tad api tejaḥ kim āvṛtteḥ iha sā na kim tanu tvāt tejasaḥ api etad asti anyatra api atānavam ati āsanne ca su vyaktam tejas tad syāt ati sphuṭam tatra api adṛṣṭam āśritya bhavet rūpa antaram yadi anyonya āvaraṇāt teṣām syāt tejaḥ vihati s tatas tatra ekam eva dṛśyeta tasya anāvaraṇe sakṛt paśyet sphuṭa asphuṭam rūpam ekaḥ adṛṣṭena vāraṇe artha anarthau na yena stas tad adṛṣṭam karoti kim tasmāt saṃvid yathā hetu jāyamāna artha saṃśrayāt pratibhāsa bhidām dhatte śeṣāḥ kumati durnayāḥ jñāna śabda pradīpānām pratyakṣasya itarasya vā janaka tvena pūrveṣām kṣaṇikānām vināśataḥ vyaktiḥ kutaḥ asatām jñānāt anyasya anupakāriṇaḥ vyaktau vyajyeta sarvaḥ artha s tad hetoḥ niyamaḥ yadi na eṣā api kalpanā jñāne jñānam tu artha avabhāsataḥ tam vyanakti iti kathyeta tad abhāve api tad kṛtam na ākārayati ca anyaḥ arthaḥ anupakārāt saha uditaḥ vyaktaḥ na ākārayan jñānam sva ākāreṇa katham bhavet vajra upala ādiḥ api arthaḥ sthiraḥ saḥ anya anapekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvasya janayet jñānāni jagataḥ samam kramāt bhavanti tāni asya sahakāry upakārataḥ āhuḥ pratikṣaṇam bhedam sa doṣaḥ atra api pūrvavat saṃvedanasya tādātmye na vivādaḥ asti kasyacid tasya artha rūpa tā siddhā sā api sidhyati saṃsmṛteḥ bhedena ananubhūteḥ bhinna vibhakte sva gocaraiḥ evam etad na khalu evam iti sā syāt na bhedinī na ca anubhava mātreṇa kaścid bhedaḥ vivecakaḥ vivekinī na ca aspaṣṭa bhede dhīḥ yamala ādivat dvairūpya sādhanena api prāyas siddham sva vedanam svarūpa bhūta ābhāsasya tadā saṃvedana īkṣaṇāt dhiyā atad rūpayā jñāne niruddhe anubhavaḥ kutas svam ca rūpam na sā vetti iti utsannaḥ anubhavaḥ arthinaḥ bahis mukham ca tad jñānam bhāti artha pratibhāsavat buddheḥ ca grāhikā buddhiḥ nityam antarmukhā ātmani yaḥ yasya viṣaya ābhāsas tam vetti na tad iti api prāptā kā saṃvid anyā asti tādrūpyāt iti ced matam prāptam saṃvedanam sarva sadṛśānām parasparam buddhiḥ sarūpā tad vic ced na idānīm vid sa rūpikā svayam saḥ anubhavas tasyāḥ na sa sārūpya kāraṇaḥ kriyā karma vyavasthāya aḥ tal loke syāt nibandhanam svabhāva bhūta tad rūpa saṃvid āropa viplavāt nīla ādeḥ anubhūta ākhyā na anubhūteḥ para ātmanoḥ dhiyaḥ nīla ādi rūpa tve bāhyaḥ arthaḥ kim pramāṇakaḥ dhiyaḥ anīla ādi rūpa tve sa tasya anubhavaḥ katham yadā saṃvedana ātma tvam na sārūpya nibandhanam siddham tad svata eva asya kim arthena upanīyate sarva ātmanā hi sārūpye jñānam ajñāna tām vrajet sāmye kenacid aṅgena syāt sarvam sarva vedanam yathā nīla ādi rūpa tvāt nīla ādy anubhavaḥ mataḥ tathā anubhava rūpa tvāt tasya api anubhavaḥ bhavet na anubhūtaḥ anubhava iti arthavat tad viniścayaḥ tasmāt adoṣa iti ced na arthe api asti eṣa sarvadā kasmāt vā anubhave na asti sati sattā nibandhane api ca idam yad ābhāti dṛśyamāne sita ādike puṃsām sita ādy abhivyakti rūpam saṃvedanam sphuṭam tad kim sita ādy abhivyakteḥ para rūpam atha ātmanaḥ para rūpe aprakāśāyām vyaktau vyaktam katham sitam jñānam vyaktiḥ na sā vyaktā iti avyaktam akhilam jagat vyakteḥ vyakti antara vyaktau api doṣa prasaṅgataḥ dṛṣṭyā ca ajñāta sambandham viśinaṣṭi tayā katham yasmāt dvayoḥ eka gatau na dvitīyasya darśanam dvayoḥ saṃsṛṣṭayoḥ dṛṣṭau syāt dṛṣṭam iti niścayaḥ sarūpam darśanam yasya dṛśyate anyena cetasā dṛṣṭa ākhyā tatra ced siddham sārūpye asya sva vedanam atha ātma rūpan naḥ vetti para rūpasya vid katham sārūpyāt vedanā ākhyā ca prāk eva pratipāditā dṛṣṭayoḥ eva sārūpya grahaḥ artham ca na dṛṣṭavān prāk katham darśanena asya sārūpyam saḥ adhyavasyati sārūpyam api na icchet yaḥ tasya na ubhaya darśanam tadā arthaḥ jñānam iti ca jñāte ca iti gatā kathā atha svarūpam sā tarhi svayam eva prakāśate yad tasyām aprakāśāyām arthaḥ syāt aprakāśitaḥ etena anātma vid pakṣe sarva artha adarśanena ye apratyakṣām dhiyam prāhuḥ te api nirvarṇita uttarāḥ āśraya ālambana abhyāsa bhedāt bhinna pravṛttayaḥ sukha duḥkha abhilāṣa ādi bhedā buddhaya eva tāḥ pratyakṣāḥ tad viviktam ca na anyat kiṃcid vibhāvyate yad tad jñānam paraḥ api enām bhuñjīta anyena vid yadi tad jā tad pratibhāsā vā yadi dhīḥ vetti na aparā ālambamānasya anyasya api asti avaśyam idam dvayam atha na utpadyate tasmāt na ca tad pratibhāsinī sā dhīḥ n nirviṣayā prāptā sāmānyam ca tad agrahe na gṛhyata iti proktam na ca tad vastu kiṃcana tasmāt artha avabhāsaḥ asau na anyas tasyāḥ dhiyas tatas siddhe pratyakṣa bhāva ātma vidau gṛhṇāti tad punar na adhyakṣam iti ced eṣa kutaḥ bhedaḥ samarthayoḥ adṛṣṭa eka artha yoga ādeḥ saṃvidaḥ niyamaḥ yadi sarvathā anyaḥ na gṛhṇīyāt saṃvid bhedaḥ api apoditaḥ yeṣām ca yoginaḥ anyasya pratyakṣeṇa sukha ādikam vidanti tulya anubhavāḥ tadvat te api syuḥ āturāḥ viṣaya indriya sampāta abhāvāt teṣām tad udbhavam na udeti duḥkham iti ced na vai duḥkha samudbhavaḥ duḥkha asaṃvedanam kim tu duḥkha jñāna samudbhavaḥ na hi duḥkha ādy asaṃvedyam pīḍā anugraha kāraṇam bhāsamānam sva rūpeṇa pīḍā duḥkham svayam yadā na tad ālambanam jñānam na tadā evam prayujyate bhinne jñānasya sarvasya tena ālambana vedane artha sārūpyam ālamba ātmā vittiḥ svayam sphuṭaḥ api ca adhyakṣatā abhāve dhiyaḥ syāl liṅgataḥ gatiḥ tad ca akṣam arthaḥ dhīḥ pūrvaḥ manaskāraḥ api vā bhavet kārya kāraṇa sāmagryām asyām sambandhinā aparam sāmarthya adarśanāt tatra na indriyam vyabhicārataḥ tathā arthaḥ dhī manaskārau jñānam tau ca na sidhyataḥ na aprasiddhasya liṅga tvam vyaktiḥ arthasya ced matā liṅgam sā eva nanu jñānam vyaktaḥ arthaḥ anena varṇitaḥ vyaktau ananubhūtāyām tad vyaktatva aviniścayāt atha arthasya eva kaścid sa viśeṣaḥ vyaktiḥ iṣyate na anutpāda vyayavataḥ viśeṣaḥ arthasya kaścana tad iṣṭau vā pratijñānam kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ prasajyate sa ca jñātaḥ athavā ajñātaḥ bhavet jñātasya liṅga tā yadi jñāte aparicchinne jñātaḥ asau iti tad kutas jñāta tvena aparicchinnam api tad gamakam katham adṛṣṭa dṛṣṭayaḥ anyena draṣṭā dṛṣṭā na hi kvacid viśeṣaḥ saḥ anya dṛṣṭau api asti iti syāt sva dhī gatiḥ tasmāt anumitiḥ buddheḥ sva dharma nirapekṣiṇaḥ kevalān na artha dharmāt kaḥ sva dharmaḥ sva dhiyaḥ paraḥ yaḥ pratyakṣaḥ dhiyaḥ hetuḥ tulya kāraṇa janmanaḥ tasya bhedaḥ kutaḥ buddheḥ vyabhicāry anya jaḥ ca saḥ rūpa ādīn pañca viṣayāni indriyāṇi upalambhanam muktvā na kāryam aparam tasyāḥ samupalabhyate tatra atyakṣam dvayam pañcasv artheṣu ekaḥ api na īkṣyate rūpa darśanataḥ jātaḥ yaḥ anyathā vyasta sambhavaḥ yad evam apratītam tal liṅgam iti api alaukikam vidyamāne api liṅge tām tena sārdham apaśyataḥ katham prati iti liṅgam hi na adṛṣṭasya prakāśakam tatas eva asya liṅgāt prāk prasiddheḥ upavarṇane dṛṣṭānta antara sādhya tvam tasya api iti anavasthitiḥ iti arthasya dhiyaḥ siddhiḥ na arthāt tasyāḥ kathaṃcana tad aprasiddhau arthasya svayam eva aprasiddhitaḥ pratyakṣām ca dhiyam dṛṣṭvā tasya āś ca iṣṭa abhidhā ādikam para citta anumānam ca na syāt ātmani adarśanāt sambandhasya manaḥ buddhau artha liṅga aprasiddhitaḥ prakāśitā katham vā syāt buddhiḥ buddhy antareṇa vaḥ aprakāśa ātmanoḥ sā syāt vyaṅgya vyañjaka tā kutas viṣayasya katham vyaktiḥ prakāśe rūpa saṃkramāt sa ca prakāśa s tad rūpaḥ svayam eva prakāśate tathā abhyupagame buddheḥ buddhau buddhiḥ sva vedikā siddhā anyathā tulya dharmā viṣayaḥ api dhiyā saha iti prakāśa rūpā naḥ svayam dhīḥ samprakāśate anyaḥ asyām rūpa saṃkrāntyā prakāśaḥ samprakāśate sādṛśye api hi dhīḥ anyā prakāśyā na tayā matā svayam prakāśanāt artha s tad rūpeṇa prakāśate yathā pradīpayoḥ dīpa ghaṭayoḥ ca tad āśrayaḥ vyaṅgya vyañjaka bhāvena vyavahāraḥ pratanyate viṣaya indriya mātreṇa na dṛṣṭam iti niścayaḥ tasmāt yatas ayam tasya api vācyam anyasya darśanam smṛteḥ api ātma vid siddhā jñānasya anyena vedane dīrgha ādi grahaṇam na syāt bahu mātra anavasthiteḥ avasthitā akramāyām sakṛt ābhāsanān matau varṇaḥ syāt akramaḥ dīrghaḥ kramavān akramām katham upakuryāt asaṃśliṣyan varṇa bhāgaḥ parasparam akrameṇa grahāt anta kramavat dhīś ca naḥ bhavet āntyam pūrva sthitāt ūrdhvam vardhamānaḥ dhvaniḥ bhavet sthāne svayam na naśyet sā paścāt api aviśeṣatas doṣaḥ ayam sakṛt utpanna akrama varṇa sthitau api sakṛt yatna udbhavāt vyarthaḥ syāt yatnaḥ ca uttarottaraḥ vyaktau api eṣa varṇānām doṣaḥ samanuṣajyate anekayā tad grahaṇe yā antyā dhīḥ sā anubhūyate na dīrgha grāhikā sā ca tad na syāt dīrgha dhī smṛtiḥ pṛthak pṛthak ca buddhīnām saṃvittau tad dhvaniḥ śruteḥ avicchinna ābhatā na syāt ghaṭanam ca nirākṛtam vicchinnam śṛṇvataḥ api asya yadi avicchinna vibhramaḥ hrasva dvayoc cāraṇe api syāt avicchinna vibhramaḥ vicchinne darśane ca akṣād avicchinna adhiropaṇam na akṣāt sarva akṣa buddhīnām vitathatva prasaṅgataḥ sarva antyaḥ api hi varṇa ātmā nimeṣa tulita sthitiḥ sa ca kramāt aneka aṇu sambandhena nitiṣṭhati eka aṇu atyaya kālaḥ ca kālaḥ alpīyān kṣaṇaḥ mataḥ buddhiḥ ca kṣaṇikā tasmāt kramāt varṇān prapadyate iti varṇeṣu rūpa ādau avicchinna avabhāsinī vicchinnā api anyayā buddhiḥ sarvā syāt vitatha arthikā ghaṭanam yad ca bhāvānām anyatra indriya vibhramāt bheda alakṣaṇa vibhrāntam smaraṇam tad vikalpakam tasya spaṣṭa avabhāsi tvam jalpa saṃsargiṇaḥ kutas na akṣa grāhye asti śabdānām yojanā iti vivecitam vicchinnam paśyataḥ api akṣaiḥ ghaṭayet yadi kalpanā arthasya tad saṃvitteḥ ca satatam bhāsamānayoḥ bādhake asati san nyāye vicchinna iti tad kutas buddhīnām śakti niyamāt iti ced sa kutaḥ mataḥ yugapad buddhy adṛṣṭeḥ ced tad eva idam vicāryate tāsām samāna jātīye sāmarthya niyamaḥ bhavet tathā hi samyak lakṣyante vikalpāḥ krama bhāvinaḥ etena yaḥ samakṣe arthe pratyabhijñāna kalpanām spaṣṭa avabhāsāam pratyakṣām kalpayet saḥ api vāritaḥ keśa golaka dīpa ādau api spaṣṭa avabhāsanāt pratīta bhede api adhyakṣā dhīḥ katham tādṛśī bhavet tasmāt na pratyabhijñānāt varṇa ādy ekatva niścayaḥ pūrva anubhūta smaraṇāt tad dharma āropaṇāt vinā sa eva ayam iti jñānam na asti tad ca akṣa je kutas na ca artha jñāna saṃvittyoḥ yugapad sambhavaḥ yatas lakṣyate pratibhāsau dvau na artha artha jñānayoḥ pṛthak na hi artha ābhāsi ca jñānam arthaḥ bāhyaś ca kevalaḥ eka ākāram atigrāhye bheda abhāva prasaṅgataḥ su upalakṣyeṇa bhedena yau saṃvittau na lakṣitau artha artha pratyayau paścāt smaryete tau pṛthak katham krameṇa anubhava utpāde api artha artha manasā ūr ayam pratibhāsasya nānātva codya doṣaḥ duruddharaḥ artha saṃvedanam tāvat tatas artha ābhāsa vedanam na hi saṃvedanam śuddham bhavet arthasya vedanam tathā hi nīla ādy ākāra eka ekam ca vedanam lakṣyate na tu nīla ābhe vedane vedanam param jñāna antareṇa anubhavaḥ bhavet tatra api ca smṛtiḥ dṛṣṭā tad vedanam kena tasya api anyena ced imām mālām jñāna vidām kaḥ ayam janayati anubandhinīm pūrvā dhīḥ sā eva ced na syāt saṃcāraḥ viṣaya antare tām grāhya lakṣaṇa prāptām āsannām janikām dhiyam agṛhītvā uttaram jñānam gṛhṇīyāt aparam katham ātmani jñāna janane svabhāve niyatām ca tām kaḥ nāma anyaḥ vibadhnīyāt bahis aṅge antaraṅgikām bāhyaḥ saṃnihitaḥ api arthaḥ tām vibandhum hi na prabhuḥ dhiyam na anubhavet kaścid anyathā arthasya saṃnidhau na ca saṃnihita arthā asti daśā kācid atas dhiyaḥ utsanna mūlā smṛtiḥ api utsannā iti ujjvalam matam atīta ādi vikalpānām yeṣām na arthasya saṃnidhiḥ saṃcāra kāraṇa abhāvāt utsīdet artha cintanam ātmani jñāna janane śakti saṃkṣayataḥ śanais viṣaya antara saṃcāraḥ yadi sā eva artha dhīḥ kutas śakti kṣaye pūrva dhiyaḥ na hi dhīḥ prāk dhiyā vinā anya artha asakti viguṇe jñāne jñāna udaya agateḥ sakṛt vijātīya jātau api ekena paṭīyasā cittena āhita vaiguṇyāt ālayān na anya sambhavaḥ na apekṣeta anyathā sāmyam manaḥ vṛtteḥ manaḥ antaram manaḥ jñāna krama utpattiḥ api apekṣā prasādhanī ekatvān manasaḥ anyasmin saktasya anya agateḥ yadi jñāna antarasya anudayaḥ na kadācid saha udayāt sama vṛttau ca tulya tvāt sarvadā anya agatiḥ bhavet janma ca ātma manaḥ yoga mātrajānām sakṛt bhavet ekā eva ced kriyā ekaḥ syāt kim dīpaḥ aneka darśanaḥ krameṇa api na śaktam syāt paścāt api aviśeṣatas anena deha puruṣau uktau saṃskārataḥ yadi niyamaḥ sa kutas paścāt buddheḥ ced astu sammatam na grāhyatā anyā jananāt jananam grāhya lakṣaṇam agrāhyam na hi tejaḥ asti na ca saukṣmya ādy anaṃśake grāhyatā śakti hāniḥ syāt na anyasya janana ātmanaḥ grāhyatāyā na khalu anyaj jananam grāhya lakṣaṇe sākṣān na hi anyathā buddhe rūpa ādiḥ upakārakaḥ grāhyatā lakṣaṇāt anyas tad bhāva niyamaḥ asya kaḥ buddheḥ api tad asti iti sā api tattve vyavasthitā grāhya upādāna saṃvittī cetasaḥ grāhya lakṣaṇam rūpa ādeś cetasaḥ ca evam aviśuddha dhiyam prati grāhya lakṣaṇa cintā iyam acintyā yoginām gatiḥ tatra sūkṣma ādi bhāvena grāhyam agrāhyatām vrajet rūpa ādi buddheḥ kim jātam paścāt yad prāṅ na vidyate sati sva dhī grahe tasmāt sā eva anantara hetu tā cetasaḥ grāhyatā sā eva tatas na artha antarā gatiḥ nānā eka śakty abhāve api bhāvaḥ nānā eka kārya kṛt prakṛtyā eva iti gaditam nānā ekasmān na ced bhavet na kiṃcid ekam ekasmāt sāmagryāḥ sarva sambhavaḥ ekam syāt api sāmagrayoḥ iti uktam tad aneka kṛt artham pūrvam ca vijñānam gṛhṇīyāt yadi dhīḥ parā pūrva apara artha bhāsi tvā c cintā ādau eka cetasi abhilāpa dvayam nityam syāt dṛṣṭa kramam akramam dvis dvis ekam ca bhāseta bhāsanāt ātma tad vidoḥ viṣaya antara saṃcāre yadi antyam na anubhūyate para anubhūtivat sarvān anubhūtiḥ prasajyate ātma anubhūtam pratyakṣam na anubhūtam paraiḥ yadi ātma anubhūtiḥ sā siddhā kṛtaḥ yena evam ucyate vyakti hetv aprasiddhiḥ syāt na vyakteḥ vyaktam icchataḥ vyakti asiddhau api vyaktam yadi vyaktam idam jagat parasya pratipādya tvāt adṛṣṭaḥ api svayam paraiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sādhanam iti eke tad kṣepāya ātma dṛś vacaḥ anumā viṣaye na iṣṭam parīkṣita parigrahāt vācaḥ prāmāṇyam asmin hi na anumānam pravartate bādhanāya āgamasya ukteḥ sādhanasya param prati saḥ apramāṇam tadā asiddham tad siddham akhilam tatas tad āgamavataḥ siddham yadi kasya ka āgamaḥ bādhyamānaḥ pramāṇena sa siddhaḥ katham āgamaḥ tad viruddha abhyupagamas tena eva ca katham bhavet tad anya upagame tasya tyāga aṅgasya apramāṇa tā tad kasmāt sādhanam na uktam sva pratītiḥ yad udbhavā yuktyā yayā āgamaḥ grāhyaḥ grāhikā asya api sā na kim prākṛtasya sataḥ prāk yaiḥ pratipatti akṣa sambhavau sādhanaiḥ sādhanāni artha śakti jñāne asya tāni alam vicchinna anugamā ye ca sāmānyena api agocarāḥ sādhya sādhana cintā asti na teṣu artheṣu kācana puṃsām abhiprāya vaśāt tadtva atattva vyavasthitau luptau hetu tad ābhāsau tasya vastu asamāśrayāt san arthaḥ jñāna sa apekṣaḥ na asan jñānena sādhakaḥ sataḥ api vastu asaṃśliṣṭā asaṃgatyā sadṛśī gatiḥ liṅgam svabhāvaḥ kāryam vā dṛśya adarśanam eva vā sambaddham vastutas siddham tad asiddham kim ātmanaḥ pareṇa api anyatas gantum ayuktam para kalpitaiḥ prasaṅgaḥ dvaya sambandhāt eka abhāve anya hānaye tad artha grahaṇam śabda kalpanā āropita ātmanām aliṅgatva prasiddhy artham arthāt artha prasiddhitaḥ kalpanā āgamayoḥ kartuḥ icchā mātra anurodhataḥ vastunaḥ ca anyathā abhāvāt kalpitā vyabhicāriṇaḥ arthāt artha gateḥ śaktiḥ pakṣa hetv abhidhānayoḥ na arthe tena tayoḥ n na asti svatas sādhana saṃsthitiḥ tad pakṣa vacanam vaktuḥ abhiprāya nivedane pramāṇam saṃśaya utpatteḥ tatas sākṣān na sādhanam sādhyasya eva abhidhānena pāraṃparyeṇa na api alam śaktasya sūcakam hetu vacaḥ aśaktam api svayam hetv artha viṣaya tvena tad aśakta uktiḥ īritā śaktis tasya api ced hetu vacanasya pravartanāt tad saṃśayena jijñāsoḥ bhavet prakaraṇa āśrayaḥ vipakṣa upagame api etad tulyam iti anavasthitiḥ antaraṅgam tu sāmarthyam triṣu rūpeṣu saṃsthitam tatra smṛti samādhānam tad vacasya iva saṃsthitam akhyāpite hi viṣaye hetu vṛtteḥ asambhavāt viṣaya khyāpanāt eva siddhau ced tasya śakta tā vyāpti pūrve vinā api asmāt kṛtakaḥ śabda īdṛśaḥ sarve anityā iti prokte api arthāt tad nāśa dhīḥ bhavet anuktā api pakṣasya siddheḥ apratibandhataḥ triṣu anyatam arūpasya eva anuktiḥ nyūna tā uditā sādhya uktim vā pratijñām sa vadan doṣaiḥ na yujyate sādhana adhikṛteḥ eva hetvābhāsa prasaṅgataḥ aviśeṣa uktiḥ api eka jātīye saṃśaya avahā anyathā sarva sādhya ukteḥ pratijñā tvam prasajyate siddha ukteḥ sādhana tvāt ced parasya api na duṣyate idānīm sādhya nirdeśaḥ sādhana avayavaḥ katham sa ābhāsa ukty ādy upakṣepa parihāra viḍambanā asambaddhā tathā hi eṣa na nyāya iti sūcitam gamya artha tve api sādhya ukteḥ asammohāya lakṣaṇam tad catur lakṣaṇam rūpa nipāta iṣṭa svayam padaiḥ asiddha asādhana artha ukta vādy abhyupagama grahaḥ anuktaḥ api icchayā vyāptaḥ sādhya ātma artha van mataḥ sarva anya iṣṭa nivṛttau api āśaṅkā sthāna vāraṇam vṛttau svayam śruteḥ prāha kṛtā ca eṣā tad arthikā viśeṣas tad vyapekṣātaḥ kathitaḥ dharma dharmiṇoḥ anuktā api vāñchāyā bhavet prakaraṇāt gatiḥ ananvayaḥ api dṛṣṭānte doṣa s tasya yathā uditaḥ ātmā paraś ced saḥ asiddha iti tatra iṣṭa ghāta kṛt sādhanam yad vivāde na nyastam tad ced na sādhyate kim sādhyam anyathā aniṣṭam bhavet vaiphalyam eva vā sa dvitīya prayogeṣu niranvaya viruddhate etena kathite sādhyam sāmānyena atha sammatam tad eva artha antara abhāvāt deha anāptau na sidhyate vācyam śūnyam pralapatām tad etad jāḍya cintitam tulyam nāśe api ced śabda ghaṭa bhedena kalpane na siddhena vināśena tadvataḥ sādhanāt dhvaneḥ tathā artha antara bhāve syāt tadvān kumbhaḥ api anitya tā viśiṣṭā dhvaninā anveti naḥ ced na ayoga vāraṇāt dvividhaḥ hi vyavacchedaḥ viyoga apara yogayoḥ vyavacchedāt ayoge tu na anyena ananvaya āgamaḥ sāmānyam eva tad sādhyam na ca siddha prasādhanam viśiṣṭam dharmiṇā tad ca na niranvaya doṣavat etena dharmi dharmābhyām viśiṣṭau dharma dharmiṇau pratyākhyātau nirākurvan dharmiṇy evam asādhanāt samudāya apavādaḥ hi na dharmiṇi virudhyate sādhyam yatas tathā na iṣṭam sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ atra kevalaḥ ekasya dharmiṇaḥ śāstre nānā dharma sthitau api sādhyaḥ syāt ātmanā eva iṣṭa iti upāttā svayam śrutiḥ śāstra abhyupagamāt eva sarva ādānāt prabādhane tatra ekasya api doṣaḥ syāt yadi hetu pratijñayoḥ śabda nāśe prasādhye syāt gandhe bhū guṇa tā kṣateḥ hetuḥ viruddhaḥ aprakṛteḥ naḥ ced anyatra sā samā atha atra dharmī prakṛta s tatra śāstra artha bādhanam atha vādi iṣṭatām brūyāt dharmi dharma ādi sādhanaiḥ kaiścid prakaraṇaiḥ icchā bhavet sā gamyate ca taiḥ balāt tava icchā iyam iti vyaktam īśvara ceṣṭitam vadan na kārya liṅgām tām vyabhicāreṇa bādhyate anāntarīyake ca arthe bādhite anyasya kā kṣatiḥ uktam ca na āgama apekṣam anumānam sva gocare siddham tena su siddham tad na tadā śāstram īkṣyate vāda tyāga s tadā syāt ced na tadā anabhyupāyataḥ upāyaḥ hi abhyupāye ayam anaṅgam sa tadā api san tathā viśuddhe viṣaya dvaye śāstra parigraham cikīrṣoḥ sa hi kālaḥ syāt tadā śāstreṇa bādhanam tad virodhena cintāyāḥḥ tad siddha artheṣu ayogataḥ tṛtīya sthāna saṃkrāntau nyāyaḥ śāstra parigrahaḥ tatra api sādhya dharmasya sambaddhasya eva bādhanam parihāryam na ca anyeṣām anavasthā prasaṅgataḥ kena iyam sarva cintāsu śāstram grāhyam iti sthitiḥ kṛtā idānīm asiddhāntaiḥ grāhyaḥ dhūmena na analaḥ riktasya jantoj jātasya guṇa doṣam apaśyataḥ vilabdhā bata kena amī siddhānta viṣam agrahāḥ yadi sādhana ekatra sarvam śāstram nidarśane darśayet sādhanam syāt iti eṣā lokottarā sthitiḥ asambaddhasya dharmasya kim asiddhau na sidhyati hetuḥ tad sādhanāya uktaḥ kim duṣṭas tatra sidhyati dharmān anupanīya eva dṛṣṭānte dharmiṇaḥ akhilān vāc dhūma ādeḥ janaḥ anveti caitanya dahana ādikam svabhāvam kāraṇam vā arthaḥ avyabhicāreṇa sādhayan kasyacid vāda bādhāyām svabhāvān na nivartate prapadyamānaḥ ca anyas tam na antarīyakam īpsitaiḥ sādhya arthaiḥ hetunā tena katham apratipāditaḥ uktaḥ anuktaḥ api ced hetuḥ virodhaḥ vādinaḥ atra kim na hi tasya ukti doṣeṇa sa jātaḥ śāstra bādhanam bādhakasya abhidhānāc ced doṣaḥ yadi vadet na saḥ kim na bādheta saḥ akurvan na yuktam kena duṣyati anyeṣu hetvābhāseṣu sva iṣṭasya eva aprasādhanāt duṣyet vyartha abhidhānena na atra tasya prasādhanāt yadi kiṃcid kvacid śāstre na yuktam pratiṣidhyate bruvāṇaḥ yuktam api anyat iti rāja kula sthitiḥ sarvān arthān samīkṛtya vaktum śakyam na sādhanam sarvatra tena utsanne ayam sādhya sādhana saṃsthitiḥ viruddhayoḥ eka dharmiṇy ayogāt astu bādhanam viruddha ekāntikena atra tadvat asti virodhitā abādhya bādhaka tve api tayoḥ śāstra artha viplavāt asambandhe api bādhā ced syāt sarvam sarva bādhakam sambandha s tena tatra eva bādhanāt asti ced asat hetoḥ sarvasya cintya tvāt sva sādhye guṇa doṣayoḥ na antarīyaka tā sādhye sambandhaḥ sā iha na īkṣyate kevalam śāstra pīḍā iha doṣaḥ sā anya kṛte samā śāstra abhyupagamāt sādhyaḥ śāstra dṛṣṭaḥ khilaḥ yadi pratijñā asiddha dṛṣṭānta hetu vādaḥ prasajyate uktayoḥ sādhana tvena naḥ ced īpsita vādataḥ nyāya prāptam na sādhya tvam vacanāt vinivartate anīpsitam asādhyam ced vādinā anyaḥ api anīpsitaḥ dharmaḥ asādhya s tadā asādhyam bādhamānam virodhi kim pakṣa lakṣaṇa bāhya arthaḥ svayam śabdaḥ api anarthakaḥ śāstreṣu icchā pravṛtty arthaḥ yadi śaṅkā kutaḥ anu iyam saḥ aniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇena gṛhṇan kena nivāryate niṣiddhaḥ ced pramāṇena vācā kena pravartyate pūrvam api eṣa siddhāntam sva icchayā eva gṛhītavān kathaṃcid anyam sa punar grahītum labhate na kim dṛṣṭeḥ vipratipattīnām atra akarṣīt svayam śrutim iṣṭa akṣatim asādhya tvam anavasthām ca darśayan samaya āhita bhedasya parihāreṇa dharmiṇaḥ prasiddhasya gṛhīti artham jagāda anyaḥ svayam śrutim vicāra prastuteḥ eva prasiddhaḥ siddha āśrayaḥ sva icchā kalpita bhedeṣu padārtheṣu avivādataḥ asādhyatām atha prāha siddha ādeśena dharmiṇaḥ sva rūpeṇa eva nirdeśya iti anena eva tad gatam siddha sādhana rūpeṇa nirdeśasya hi sambhave sādhya tvena eva nirdeśya iti idam phalavat bhavet anumānasya sāmānya viṣaya vam ca varṇitam iha evam na hi anukte api kiṃcid pakṣe virudhyate kuryāt ced dharmiṇam sādhyam tatas kim tad na śakyate kasmāt hetv anvaya abhāvān na ca doṣa s tayoḥ ayam uttara avayava apekṣaḥ na doṣaḥ pakṣa iṣyate tathā hetv ādi doṣaḥ api pakṣa doṣaḥ prasajyate sarvaiḥ pakṣasya bādhātas tasmāt tad mātra liṅginaḥ pakṣa doṣā matā na anye pratyakṣa ādi virodhavat hetv ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ bādhyam muktvā pakṣasya lakṣaṇam ucyate parihāra artham avyāpti vyatirekayoḥ svayam nipāta rūpa ākhyā vyatirekasya bādhikāḥ saha anirākṛtena iṣṭa śrutiḥ avyāpti bādhanī sādhya abhyupagamaḥ pakṣa lakṣaṇam teṣu apakṣatā nirākṛte bādhanataḥ śeṣe alakṣaṇa vṛttitaḥ svayam iṣṭa abhidhānena gata arthe api avadhāraṇe kṛtya antena abhisambandhāt uktam kāla antara cchide iha anaṅgam iṣeḥ n niṣṭhā tena īpsita pade punar aṅgam eva tathā asiddha hetv ādi pratiṣidhyate avācaka tvāt ca ayuktam tena iṣṭam svayam ātmanā anapekṣya akhilam śāstram tad abhīṣṭasya sādhya tā tena anabhīṣṭa saṃsṛṣṭasya iṣṭasya api hi bādhane yathā sādhyam abādhātaḥ pakṣa hetū na duṣyataḥ aniṣiddhaḥ pramāṇābhyām sa ca upagama iṣyate sandigdhe hetu vacanāt vyastaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ anumānasya bhedena sā bādhā uktā caturvidhā tatra abhyupāyaḥ kārya aṅgam svabhāva aṅgam jagat sthitiḥ ātma aparodha abhimataḥ bhūta niścaya yukta vāc āptaḥ sva vacanam śāstram ca evam uktam samatvataḥ yathā ātmanaḥ apramāṇa tve vacanam na pravartate śāstra dṛṣṭe tathā na arthe vicāraḥ tad anāśraye tad prastāva āśraya tve hi śāstram bādhakam iti amum vaktum artham sva vācā asya sahoktiḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye udāharaṇam api atra sadṛśam tena varṇitam pramāṇānām abhāve hi śāstra vācoḥ ayogataḥ sva vāc virodhe vispaṣṭam udāharaṇam āgame diś mātra darśanam tatra pretya dharmaḥ sukha pradaḥ śāstriṇaḥ api atadālambe viruddha uktau tu vastuni na bādhā pratibandhaḥ syāt tulya kakṣyatayā dvayoḥ yathā sva vāci tad ca asyāḥ tadā sva vacana ātmakam tayoḥ pramāṇam yasya asti tad syāt anyasya bādhakam pratijñām anumānam vā pratijñā apeta yuktikā tulya kakṣyā yathārtham vā bādheta katham anyathā prāmāṇyam āgamānām ca prāk eva vinivāritam abhyupāya vicāreṣu tasmāt doṣaḥ ayam iṣyate tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśanāya pṛthak kṛtaḥ anumāna abahiḥ bhūtaḥ api abhyupāyaḥ prabādhanāt anyathā atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt vyartha tā vā pṛthak kṛteḥ bhedaḥ vāc mātra vacane pratibandhaḥ sva vācy api tena abhyupagamāt śāstram pramāṇam sarva vastuṣu bādhakam yadi na icchet sa bādhakam kim punar bhavet sva vāc virodhaḥ abhedaḥ syāt sva vāc śāstra virodhayoḥ puruṣa icchā kṛtā ca asya paripūrṇā pramāṇa tā tasmāt prasiddheṣu artheṣu śāstra tyāge api na kṣatiḥ parokṣeṣu āgama aniṣṭau na cintā eva pravartate virodha udbhāvana prāyā parīkṣā api atra tad yathā adharma mūlam rāga ādi snānam ca adharma śodhanam śāstram yad siddhayā yuktyā sva vācā ca na bādhyate dṛṣṭe adṛṣṭe api tad grāhyam iti cintā pravartate artheṣu apratiṣiddha tvāt puruṣa icchā anurodhinaḥ iṣṭa śabda abhidheya tvasya āptaḥ atra akṣata vāc janaḥ uktaḥ prasiddha śabdena dharmas tad vyavahāra jaḥ pratyakṣa ādim iti māna śruty āropeṇa sūcitaḥ tad āśraya bhuvām icchā varti tvāt aniṣedhinām kṛtānām akṛtānām vā yogyam viśvam svabhāvataḥ artha mātra anurodhinyā bhāvinyā bhūtayā api vā bādhyate pratirundhānaḥ śabda yogyatayā tayā tad yogya tā balāt eva vastu tas ghaṭitaḥ dhvaniḥ sarvaḥ asyām apratīte api tasmin tad siddha tā tatas asādhāraṇa tā na syāt bādhā hetoḥ iha anyathā tad niṣedhaḥ anumānāt syāt śabda arthe anakṣa vṛttitaḥ asādhāraṇa tā tatra hetūnām yatra na anvayi sattvam iti abhyudāhāraḥ hetoḥ evam phalaḥ mataḥ saṃketa saṃśrayāḥ śabdāḥ sa ca icchā mātra saṃśrayaḥ na asiddhiḥ śabda siddhānām iti śabda prasiddha vāc anumāna prasādhyeṣu viruddha avyabhicāriṇaḥ abhāvam darśayati evam pratīteḥ anumā tu atas athavā bruvataḥ lokasya anumā abhāva ucyate kim tena bhinna viṣayā pratītiḥ anumānataḥ tena anumānāt vastūnām sat asattā anurodhinaḥ bhinnasya atad vaśād vṛtti s tad icchā jā iti sūcitam candra tām śaśinaḥ anicchan kām pratītim sa vāñchati iti tam praty adṛṣṭāntam tad asādhāraṇam matam na udāharaṇam eva idam adhikṛtya idam ucyate lakṣaṇa tvāt tathā avṛkṣaḥ dhātrī iti uktau ca bādhanāt atra api loke dṛṣṭa tvāt karpūra rajata ādiṣu samayāt vartamānasya kā asādhāraṇa tā abhidhā yadi tasya kvacid sidhyet siddham vastu balena tad prati iti siddha upagame aśaśiny api anivāraṇam tasya vastuni siddhasya śaśiny api anivāraṇam tad vastu abhāve śaśini vāraṇe api na duṣyati tasmāt avastu niyata saṃketa dhvani bhāvinām yogyāḥ padārthā dharmāṇām icchāyā anirodhanāt tām yogyatām nirundhānam saṃketa apratiṣedha jā pratihanti pratīta ākhyā yogya tā viṣayā anumā śabdānām artha niyamaḥ saṃketa anuvidhāyinām na iti anena uktam atra eṣām pratiṣedhaḥ virudhyate naimittikyāḥ śruteḥ artham artham vā pāramārthikam śabdānām pratirundhānaḥ na bādhyas tena varṇitaḥ tasmāt viṣaya bhedasya darśanāya pṛthakkṛtā anumāna abahiḥ bhūtā pratītiḥ api pūrvavat siddhayoḥ pṛthak ākhyāne darśayan ca prayojanam ete sa hetuke prāha na anumā adhyakṣa bādhane tatra api adhyakṣa bādhāyām nānā rūpa tayā dhvanau prasiddhasya śrutau rūpam yad eva pratibhāsate advayam śabala ābhāsasya adṛṣṭeḥ buddhi janmanaḥ tad artha artha uktiḥ asya eva kṣepe adhyakṣeṇa bādhanam tad eva rūpam tatra arthaḥ śeṣam vyāvṛtti lakṣaṇam avastu rūpam sāmānyam atas tad na akṣa gocaraḥ tena sāmānya dharmāṇām apratyakṣatva siddhitaḥ pratikṣepe api abādhā iti śrāvaṇa uktyā prakāśitam sarvathā avācya rūpa tvāt siddhyā tasya samāśrayāt bādhanāt tad balena uktaḥ śravaṇena akṣa gocaraḥ sarvatra vādinaḥ dharmaḥ yaḥ sva sādhya tayā īpsitaḥ tad dharmavati bādhā syāt na anya dharmeṇa dharmiṇi anyathā asya uparodhaḥ kaḥ bādhite anyatra dharmiṇi gata arthe lakṣaṇe na asmin sva dharmi vacanam punar bādhāyām dharmiṇaḥ api syāt bādhā iti asya prasiddhaye āśrayasya virodhena tad āśrita virodhanāt anyathā evaṃvidhaḥ dharmaḥ sādhya iti abhidhānataḥ tad bādhām eva manyeta sva dharmi vacanam tatas nanu etad api artha siddham satyam kecid tu dharmiṇaḥ kevalasya uparodhe api doṣavat tām upāgatāḥ yathā paraiḥ anutpādyā pūrva rūpan na kha ādikam sakṛc śabda ādy ahetu tvāt iti ukte prāha dūṣakaḥ tadvat vastu svabhāvaḥ asan dharmī vyoma ādiḥ iti api na evam iṣṭasya sādhyasya bādhā kvacana vidyate dvayasya api hi sādhya tve sādhya dharma uparodhi yad bādhanam dharmiṇas tatra bādhā iti etena varṇitam tathā eva dharmiṇaḥ api atra sādhya tvāt kevalasya na yadi evam atra bādhā syāt na anya anutpādya śaktikaḥ sakṛc śabda ādy ahetutvāt sukha ādiḥ iti pūrvavat virodhitā bhavet atra hetuḥ aikāntikaḥ yadi krama kriyā anitya tayoḥ avirodhāt vipakṣataḥ vyāvṛtteḥ saṃśayāt eṣa śeṣavat bheda iṣyate svayam iṣṭaḥ yatas dharmaḥ sādhya s tasmāt tad āśrayaḥ bādhyaḥ na kevalaḥ na anya saṃśrayaḥ vā iti sūcitam svayam śrutyā anya dharmāṇām bādhā abādhā iti kathyate tathā sva dharmiṇā anyasya dharmiṇaḥ api iti kathyate sarva sādhana doṣeṇa pakṣa eva uparudhyate tathā api pakṣa doṣa tvam pratijñā mātra saṃjñinaḥ uttara avayava apekṣaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ saḥ anubadhyate tena iti uktam atas apakṣa doṣaḥ asiddha āśraya ādikam dharmi dharma viśeṣāṇām svarūpasya ca dharmiṇaḥ bādhā sādhya aṅga bhūtānām anena eva upadarśitā tatra udāhṛti diś mātram ucyate arthasya dṛṣṭaye dravya lakṣaṇa yuktaḥ anyaḥ saṃyoge arthaḥ asti dṛṣṭi bhāj adṛśyasya aviśiṣṭasya pratijñā niṣprayojanā iṣṭaḥ hi avayavī kāryam dṛṣṭyā adṛśyeṣu asambhavī aviśiṣṭasya ca anyasya sādhane siddha sādhanam gurutva adhogatī syātām yadi asau syāt tulā natiḥ tad nirguṇa kriyas tasmāt samavāyi na kāraṇam tatas eva na dṛśyaḥ asau adṛṣṭeḥ kārya rūpayoḥ tad bādhā anya viśeṣasya na antarīyaka bhāvinaḥ ā sūkṣmāt dravyam ālāyās tulya tvāt aṃśu pātavat dravya antara guru tvasya gatiḥ n na iti aparaḥ abravīt tasya krameṇa saṃyukte pāṃśu rāśau sakṛt yute bhedaḥ syāt gaurave tasmāt pṛthak saha ca tolite krameṇa māṣaka ādīnām saṃkhyā sāmyam na yujyate sarṣapāt ā mahā rāśeḥ uttarottara vṛddhimat guru tvam kāryam ālāya yadi na eva upalakṣyate ā sarṣapāt guru tvam tad durlakṣitam analpakam taulyam tad kāraṇam kārya gaurava anupalakṣaṇāt nanu adṛṣṭaḥ aṃśuvat saḥ arthaḥ na ca tad kāryam īkṣyate gurutva agativat sarva tad guṇa anupalakṣaṇāt māṣaka ādeḥ anādhikyam anatiḥ sā upalakṣaṇam yathāsvam akṣeṇa adṛṣṭe rūpa ādau adhika adhike abhyupāyaḥ sva vāc ādi bādhāyāḥ sambhavena tu udāharaṇam api anyat diśā gamyam yathā uktayā tri kāla viṣaya tvāt tu kṛtyānām atatha ātmakam tathā param pratinyastam sādhyam na iṣṭam tadā api tad pratyāyana adhikāre tu sarva asiddha avarodhinī tasmāt sādhya śrutiḥ n na iṣṭam viśeṣam avalambate tena aprasiddha dṛṣṭānta hetu udāharaṇam kṛtam anyathā śaśa śṛṅga ādau sarva asiddhe api sādhya tā sarvasya ca aprasiddha tvāt kathaṃcid tena na kṣamaḥ karma ādi bheda upakṣepa parihāra avivecane prāk asiddha svabhāva tvāt sādhya avayava iti asat tulya siddhānta tā te hi yena upagama lakṣaṇāḥ samudāyasya sādhya tve api anyonyasya viśeṣaṇam sādhyam dvayam tadā asiddham hetu dṛṣṭānta lakṣaṇam asambhavāt sādhya śabdaḥ dharmi vṛttiḥ yadi iṣyate śāstreṇa alam yathāyogam loka eva pravartatām sādhana ākhyāna sāmarthyāt tad arthe sādhya tā gatā hetv ādi lakṣaṇaiḥ vyāpteḥ anāśaṅkyam ca sādhanam pūrva avadhāraṇe tena pratijñā lakṣaṇa abhidhā vyarthā vyāpti phalā sā uktiḥ sāmarthyāt gamyate tatas viruddha tā iṣṭa asambandhaḥ anupakāra saha āsthitī evam sarva aṅga doṣāṇām pratijñā doṣa tā bhavet pakṣa doṣaḥ para apekṣaḥ na iti ca pratipāditam iṣṭa asambhavy asiddhaḥ ca sa eva syāt nirākṛtaḥ anityatva sa hetu tve śabda evam prakīrtayet dṛṣṭānta ākhyān atas anyat kim asti atra artha anudarśanam viśeṣe bhinnam ākhyāya sāmānyasya anuvartane na tad vyāpteḥ phalam vā kim sāmānyena anuvartane syāt nirākaraṇam śabde sthitena eva iti atas abravīt viruddha viṣaye anyasmin vadan āha anyatām śruteḥ sā ca bheda apratikṣepāt sāmānyānām na vidyate vṛkṣaḥ na śiṃśapā eva iti yathā prakaraṇe kvacid sarva śruteḥ eka vṛttiḥ n niṣedhaḥ syāt na tāvatā jñāpya jñāpakayoḥ bhedāt dharmiṇaḥ hetu bhāvinaḥ asiddheḥ jñāpaka tvasya dharmy asiddhaḥ sva sādhane dharma dharmi vivekasya sarva bhāveṣu asiddhitaḥ sarvatra doṣa s tulya ś ced na saṃvṛtyā viśeṣataḥ parama artha vicāreṣu tathābhūta prasiddhitaḥ tattva anya tvam padārtheṣu sāṃvṛteṣu niṣidhyate anumāna anumeya artha vyavahāra sthiti s tu iyam bhedam pratyaya saṃsiddham avalambya ca kalpyate yathāsvam bheda niṣṭheṣu pratyayeṣu vivekinaḥ dharmī dharmāś ca bhāsante vyavahāraḥ tad āśrayaḥ vyavahāra upanītaḥ atra sa eva aśliṣṭa bheda dhīḥ sādhyaḥ sādhana tām nīta s tena asiddhaḥ prakāśitaḥ bheda sāmānyayoḥ dharma bhedāt aṅga aṅgitā tatas yathā anityaḥ prayatna utthaḥ prayatna utthatayā dhvaniḥ pakṣa aṅga tve api abādha tvān na asiddhiḥ bhinna dharmiṇi yathā aśvaḥ na viṣāṇi tvāt eṣa piṇḍaḥ viṣāṇavān sādhya kāla aṅga tā vā na nivṛtteḥ upalakṣya tad viśeṣaḥ api pratijñā arthaḥ dharma bhedān na yujyate pakṣa dharma prabhedena sukha grahaṇa siddhaye hetu prakaraṇa arthasya sūtra saṃkṣepa ucyate ayogam yogam aparaiḥ atyanta
