ayogam eva ca vyavacchinatti dharmasya nipātaḥ vyatirecakaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyābhyām kriyayā ca saha uditaḥ vivakṣātaḥ prayoge api tasya arthaḥ ayam pratīyate vyavaccheda phalam vākyam yatas caitraḥ dhanurdharaḥ pārthaḥ dhanuḥ dharaḥ nīlam sarojam iti vā yathā pratiyogi vyavacchedas tatra api artheṣu gamyate tathā prasiddheḥ sāmarthyāt vivakṣā anugamāt dhvaneḥ tad ayoga vyavacchedāt dharmi dharma viśeṣaṇam tad viśiṣṭa tayā dharmaḥ na niranvaya doṣa bhāj svabhāva kārya siddhy artham dvau dvau hetu viparyayau vivādāt bheda sāmānye śeṣaḥ vyāvṛtti sādhanaḥ na hi svabhāvāt anyena vyāptiḥ gamyasya kāraṇe sambhavāt vyabhicārasya dvidhā vṛtti phalam tatas prayatna anantaram jñānam prāk sataḥ niyamena na tasya āvṛtty akṣa śabdeṣu sarvathā anupayogataḥ kadācid nirapekṣasya kārya ākṛti virodhataḥ kādācid ka phalam siddham tal liṅgam jñānam īdṛśam etena eva prasiddhaḥ api svabhāvasya pṛthak kṛtiḥ kāryeṇa saha nirdeśe mā jñāsīt sarvam īdṛśam vyutpatty arthī ca hetu uktiḥ ukta artha anumitau kṛtā prabheda mātram ākhyātam lakṣaṇam tu na bhidyate tena atra kārya liṅgena svabhāvaḥ api eka deśa bhāj sadṛśa udāhṛtiḥ ca atas prayatnāt vyakti janmanaḥ yad na antarīyakā sattā yaḥ vā ātmā svar avibhāgavān sa tena avyabhicārī syāt iti artham tad prabhedanam saṃyogi ādiṣu yeṣu asti pratibandhaḥ na tādṛśam na te hetava iti uktam vyabhicārasya sambhavāt sati vā pratibandheḥ tu sa eva gati sādhanaḥ niyamaḥ hi avinā abhāvaḥ anityaḥ ca na sādhanam aikāntika tvam vyāvṛtteḥ avinā abhāva ucyate tad ca na apratibaddheṣu tatas eva anvaya sthitiḥ sva ātma tve hetu bhāve vā siddhe hi vyatirekitā sidhyati atas viśeṣe na vyatirekaḥ na ca anvayaḥ adṛṣṭi mātram ādāya kevalam vyatirekitā uktā anaikāntikas tasmāt anyathā gamakaḥ bhavet prāṇa ādy abhāvaḥ nairātmya vyāptī iti vinivartane ātmanaḥ vinivarteta prāṇa ādiḥ yadi tad ca na anyasya vinivṛttyā anya vinivṛtteḥ ayogataḥ tad ātmā tad prasūta ś ced na etad ātma upalambhane tasya upalabdhau agatau agatau ca prasidhyati te ca atyanta parokṣasya dṛṣṭy adṛṣṭī na sidhyataḥ anyatra adṛṣṭa rūpasya ghaṭa ādau na iti vā kutas ajñāta vyatirekasya vyāvṛtteḥ vyāpitā kutas prāṇa ādeś ca kvacid dṛṣṭyā sattva asattvam pratīyate tathā ātmā yadi dṛśyeta sattva asattvam pratīyate yasya hetoḥ abhāvena ghaṭe prāṇaḥ na dṛśyate dehe api yadi asau na syāt yuktaḥ dehena sambhavaḥ bhinne api kiṃcid sādharmyāt yadi tattvam pratīyate prameya tvāt ghaṭa ādīnām sa ātma tvam kim na mīyate aniṣṭam ced pramāṇam hi sarva iṣṭīnām nibandhanam bhāva abhāva vyavasthām kaḥ kartum tena vinā prabhuḥ smṛti icchā yatna jaḥ prāṇa nimeṣa ādis tad udbhavaḥ viṣaya indriya cittibhyaḥ tāḥ sva jāti samudbhavāḥ anyonya pratyaya apekṣā anvaya vyatireka bhāj etau atyātma bhāvaḥ ayam anavasthā anya kalpane śrāvaṇa tvena tad tulyam prāṇa ādi vyabhicārataḥ na tasya vyabhicāri tvāt vyatireke api ced katham na asādhyāt eva viśleṣaḥ tasya nanu evam ucyate sādhye anuvṛtty abhāvaḥ arthāt tasya anyatra api asau samaḥ asādhyāt eva viccheda iti sādhye astitā ucyate arthāpattyā ata eva uktam ekena dvaya darśanam īdṛś avyabhicāraḥ atas ananvayeṣu na sidhyati pratiṣedha niṣedhaḥ ca vidhānāt kīdṛśaḥ aparaḥ nivṛttiḥ n na asataḥ sādhyāt asādhyeṣu eva naḥ tatas na iti sā eva nivṛttiḥ kim nivṛtteḥ asataḥ matā nivṛtty abhāvaḥ tu vidhiḥ vastu bhāvaḥ asataḥ api san vastu abhāvaḥ tu na asti iti paśya bāndhya vijṛmbhitam nivṛttiḥ yadi tasmin na hetoḥ vṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate sā api na pratiṣedhaḥ ayam nivṛttiḥ kim niṣidhyate vidhānam pratiṣedham ca muktvā śābdaḥ asti na aparaḥ vyavahāraḥ sa ca asatsu na iti prāptā atra mūka tā satām ca na niṣedhaḥ asti saḥ asatsu ca na vidyate jagati anena nyāyena nañ arthaḥ pralayam gataḥ deśa kāla niṣedhaḥ ced yathā asti sa niṣidhyate na tathā na yathā saḥ asti tathā api na niṣidhyate tasmāt āśritya śabda artham bhāva abhāva samāśrayam abāhya āśrayam atra iṣṭam sarvam vidhi niṣedhanam tābhyām sa dharmī sambaddhaḥ khyāti abhāve api tādṛśaḥ śabda pravṛtteḥ asti iti saḥ api iṣṭaḥ vyavahāra bhāj anyathā syāt padārthānām vidhāna pratiṣedhane eka dharmasya sarva ātma vidhāna pratiṣedhanam anānā ātma ātma tayā bhede nānā vidhi niṣedhavat eka dharmiṇy asaṃhāraḥ vidhāna pratiṣedhayoḥ ekam dharmiṇam uddiśya nānā dharma samāśrayam vidhā ekasya tad bhājām iva anyeṣām upekṣakam niṣedhe tad viviktam ca tad anyeṣām apekṣakam vyavahāram asatya artham prakalpayati dhīḥ yathā tam tathā eva avikalpya artha bheda āśrayam upāgatāḥ anādi vāsanā udbhūtam bādhante artham na laukikam tad phalaḥ atat phalaḥ ca arthaḥ bhinna ekas tatas tatas taiḥ taiḥ upaplavaiḥ n nīta saṃcaya apacayaiḥ iva atadvān api sambandhāt kutaścid upanīyate dṛṣṭim bheda āśrayaiḥ te api tasmāt ajñāta viplavāḥ sattā sādhana vṛtteḥ ca sandigdhaḥ syāt asan na saḥ asattvam ca abhyupagamāt apramāṇān na yujyate asataḥ avyatireke api sa pakṣāt vinivartanam sandigdham tasya sandehāt vipakṣāt vinivartanam ekatra niyame siddhe sidhyati anya nivartanam dvairāśye sati adṛṣṭe api syāt adṛṣṭeṣu saṃśayaḥ avyakti vyāpinaḥ api arthāḥ santi tad jāti bhāvinaḥ kvacid na niyamaḥ dṛṣṭyā pārthiva aloha lekhyavat bhāve virodhasya adṛṣṭau kaḥ sandeham nivartayet kvacid viniyamāt kaḥ anyas tad kārya ātma tayā sa ca nairātmyāt api tena asya sandigdham vinivartanam astu nāma tathā api ātmā na anairātmyāt prasidhyati yena asau vyatirekasya na abhāvam bhāvam icchati yathā na avyatireke api prāṇa ādiḥ n na sa pakṣataḥ sa pakṣa avyatirekī ced hetuḥ hetuḥ atas anvayī na anvayy avyatirekī ced anairātmyam na sa ātmakam yad na antarīyakaḥ sva ātmā yasya siddhaḥ pravṛttiṣu nivartakaḥ sa eva atas pravṛttau ca pravartakaḥ na antarīyaka tā sā ca sādhanam samapekṣate kārye dṛṣṭiḥ adṛṣṭiḥ ca kārya kāraṇa tā hi te artha antarasya tad bhāve abhāvaḥ niyamataḥ agatiḥ abhāva asambhavāt teṣām abhāve nitya bhāvinaḥ kārya svabhāva bhedānām kāraṇebhyaḥ samudbhavāt taiḥ vinā bhavataḥ anyasmāt tad jam rūpam katham bhavet sāmagrī śakti bhedāt hi vastūnām viśva rūpa tā sā ced na bhedikā prāptam eka rūpam idam jagat bhedaka abhedaka tve syāt vyāhatā bhinna rūpa tā ekasya nānā rūpa tve dve rūpe pāvaka itarau tad tasya ajananam rūpam anyasya yadi sā eva sā na tasya ajananam rūpam tad tasyāḥ sambhavet katham tatas svabhāvau niyatau anyonyam hetu kāryayoḥ tasmāt sva dṛṣṭau iva tad dṛṣṭe kārye api gamyate ekam katham anekasmāt kledavat dugdha vāriṇaḥ drava śakteḥ yatas kledaḥ sā tu ekā eva dvayoḥ api bhinna abhinnaḥ kim asya ātmā bhinnaḥ atha dravatā katham abhinnā iti ucyate buddheḥ tad rūpāyāḥ abhedataḥ tadvat bhede api dahanaḥ dahana pratyaya āśrayaḥ yena aṃśena adadhad dhūmam tena aṃśena tathā gatiḥ dahana pratyaya aṅgād eva anya apekṣāt samudbhavāt dhūmaḥ atad vyabhicāri iti siddham kāryam tathā param dhūma indhana vikāra aṅga tā pade dahana sthiteḥ anagniḥ ced adhūmaḥ asau sa dhūmaḥ ced sa pāvakaḥ na antarīyaka tā jñeyā yathāsvam hetv apekṣayā svabhāvasya yathā uktam prāk vināśa kṛtaka tvayoḥ ahetutva gati nyāyaḥ sarvaḥ ayam vyatirekiṇaḥ abhyūhyaḥ śrāvaṇatva ukteḥ kṛtāyāḥ sāmya dṛṣṭaye hetu svabhāva vyāvṛttyā eva artha vyāvṛtti varṇanāt siddha udāharaṇā iti ukta anupalabdhiḥ pṛthak na tu tatra api adṛśyāt puruṣāt prāṇa ādeḥ anivartanāt sandeha hetu tā ākhyātyā dṛśya arthe sā iti sūcitam anaṅgīkṛta vastu aṃśaḥ niṣedhaḥ sādhyate nayā vastuni api tu pūrvābhyām paryudāsaḥ vidhānataḥ tatra upalabhyeṣu astitvam upalabdheḥ na ca aparam iti ajña jñāpanāya eka anupākhya udāhṛtiḥ matā viṣaya asattvatas tatra viṣayi pratiṣidhyate jñāna abhidhāna sandeham yathā adāhāt apāvakaḥ tathā anyā na upalabhyeṣu na astitā anupalambhanāt tad jñāna śabdāḥ sādhyante tad bhāvāt tad nibandhanāḥ siddhaḥ hi vyavahāraḥ ayam dṛśya adṛṣṭau asann iti tasyāḥ siddhau asandigdhau tad kāryatve api dhī dhvanī vidyamāne hi viṣaye mohāt atra ananubruvan kevalam siddha sādharmyāt smāryate samayam paraḥ kārya kāraṇa tā yadvat sādhyate dṛṣṭy adṛṣṭitaḥ kārya ādi śabdā hi tayoḥ vyavahārāya kalpitāḥ kāraṇāt kārya saṃsiddhiḥ svabhāva antargamāt iyam hetu prabheda ākhyāyena darśita udāhṛtiḥ pṛthak eka upalambha anubhavāt idam na upalabhe iti buddheḥ upalabhe vā iti kalpikāyāḥ samudbhavaḥ viśeṣaḥ gamyate arthānām viśiṣṭāt eva vedanāt tathābhūta ātma saṃvittiḥ bheda dhī hetuḥ asya ca tasmāt svatas dhiyoḥ bheda siddhi s tābhyām tad arthayoḥ anyathā hi anavasthānāt bhedaḥ sidhyet na kasyacid viśiṣṭa rūpa anubhavān na atas anya anya nirākriyā tad viśiṣṭa upalambhaḥ atas tasya api anupalambhanam tasmāt anupalambhaḥ ayam svayam pratyakṣataḥ gataḥ sva mātra vṛtteḥ gamaka s tad abhāva vyavasthiteḥ anyathā arthasya na astitvam gamyate anupalambhataḥ upalambhasya nāstitvam anyena iti anavasthitiḥ adṛśye niścaya ayogāt sthitiḥ anyatra vāryate yathā aliṅgaḥ anya sattveṣu vikalpa ādiḥ na sidhyati aniścaya phalā hi eṣā na alam vyāvṛtti sādhane ādyā adhikriyate hetoḥ niścayena eva sādhane tasyāḥ svayam prayogeṣu svarūpam vā prayujyate artha bādhana rūpam vā bhāve bhāvāt abhāvataḥ anyonya bheda siddheḥ vā dhruva bhāva vināśavat pramāṇa antara bādhād vā sa apekṣa dhruva bhāvavat hetv antara samūhasya saṃnidhau niyamaḥ kutas bhāva hetu bhavatve kim pāraṃparya pariśramaiḥ nāśanam janayitvā anyam sa hetuḥ tasya nāśanaḥ tam eva naśvaram bhāvam janayet yadi kim bhavet ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tasya siddha ātmanaḥ sataḥ na ātma upakārakaḥ kaḥ syāt tena yaḥ samapekṣyate anapekṣaḥ ca kim bhāvaḥ atathābhūtaḥ kadācana yathā na kṣepa bhāg iṣṭaḥ sa eva udbhūta nāśakaḥ kṣaṇam api anapekṣa tve bhāvaḥ bhāvasya na iti ced bhāvaḥ hi sa tathābhūta u abhāve bhāvaḥ tathā katham ye apara apekṣa tad bhāvāḥ tad bhāva niyatā hi te asambhavāt vibandhe ca sāmagrī kārya karmaṇi anadhyavasita avagāhanam analpa dhī śaktinā api adṛṣṭa parama artha sāram adhika abhiyogaiḥ api matam mama jagati alabdha sadṛśa pratigrāhakam prayāsyati payonidheḥ paya iva sva dehe jarām
 namaḥ samantabhadrāya nyāya vādinam api vādeṣu asad vyavasthā upanyāsaiḥ śaṭhā nigṛhṇanti tad niṣedha artham idam ārabhyate asādhana aṅga vacanam adoṣa udbhāvanam dvayoḥ nigraha sthānam anyat tu na yuktam iti na iṣyate iṣṭasya arthasya siddhiḥ sādhanam tasya nirvartakam aṅgam tasya avacanam tasya aṅgasya anuccāraṇam vādinaḥ nigraha adhikaraṇam tad abhyupagamya apratibhayā tūṣṇīṃbhāvāt sādhana aṅgasya asamarthāt vā trividham eva hi liṅgam apratyakṣasya siddheḥ aṅgam svabhāvaḥ kāryam anupalabdhaḥ ca tasya samarthanam sādhyena vyāptim prasādhya dharmiṇi bhāva sādhanam yathā yad sat kṛtakam vā tad sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ san kṛtakaḥ vā śabda iti atra api na kaścid krama niyamaḥ iṣṭa artha siddheḥ ubhayatra aviśeṣāt dharmiṇi prāk sattvam prasādhya paścāt api vyāptiḥ prasādhyata eva yathā san śabdaḥ kṛtakaḥ vā yaḥ ca evam sa sarvaḥ anityaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ iti atra vyāpti sādhanam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanam yadi na sarvam sat kṛtakam vā pratikṣaṇa vināśi syāt akṣaṇikasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā ayogāt artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇataḥ nivṛttam iti asad eva syāt sarva sāmarthya upākhyā viraha lakṣaṇam hi nirupākhyam iti evam sādhanasya sādhya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa anupadarśane virodha abhāvāt asya viparyaye vṛtteḥ adarśane api san kṛtakaḥ vā syāt nityaś ca iti anivṛttiḥ eva śaṅkāyāḥ tatas vyatirekasya sandehāt anaikāntikaḥ syāt hetvābhāsaḥ na api adarśana mātrād vyāvṛttiḥ viprakṛṣṭeṣu asarva darśinaḥ adarśanasya abhāva asādhanāt arvāk darśanena satām api keṣāṃcid arthānām adarśanāt bādhakam punar pramāṇam yatra krama yaugapadya ayogaḥ na tasya kvacid sāmarthyam asti ca akṣaṇike sa iti pravartamānam asāmarthyam asal lakṣaṇam ākarṣati tena yad sat kṛtakam vā tad anityam eva iti sidhyati tāvatā ca sādhana dharma mātra anvayaḥ sādhya dharmasya svabhāva hetu lakṣaṇam ca siddham bhavati atra api adarśanam apramāṇayataḥ krama yaugapadya ayogasya eva asāmarthyena vyāpti asiddheḥ pūrvakasya api hetoḥ avyāptiḥ iha api punar sādhana upakrame anavasthā prasaṅga iti ced na abhāva sādhanasya adarśanasya apratiṣedhāt yad adarśanam viparyayam sādhayati hetoḥ sādhya viparyaye tad asya viruddha pratyupasthāpanāt bādhakam pramāṇam ucyate evam hi sa hetuḥ sādhya abhāve asan sidhyet yadi tatra pramāṇavatā sva viruddhena bādhyeta anyathā tatra asya bādhaka asiddhau saṃśayaḥ durnivāraḥ na ca sarva anupalabdhiḥ bhāvasya bādhikā tatra sāmarthyam krama akrama yogena vyāptam siddham prakāra antara abhāvāt tena vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ akṣaṇike sāmarthyam bādhata iti krama yaugapadya ayogasya sāmarthya abhāvena vyāpti siddheḥ na anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ evam svabhāva hetu prayogeṣu samarthitam sādhana aṅgam bhavati tasya asamarthanam sādhana aṅga avacanam tad vādinaḥ parājaya sthānam ārabdha artha aprasādhanāt vastutas samarthasya hetoḥ upādāne api sāmarthya apratipādanāt kārya hetau api sādhana aṅgasya samarthanam yad kārya liṅgam kāraṇasya sādhanāya upādīyate tasya tena saha kārya kāraṇa bhāva prasādhanam bhāva abhāva sādhana pramāṇābhyām yathā idam asmin sati bhavati satsu api tad anyeṣu samartheṣu tad hetuṣu tad abhāve na bhavati iti evam hi asya asandigdham tad kāryatvam samarthitam bhavati anyathā kevalam tad abhāve na bhavati iti upadarśane anyasya api tatra abhāve sandigdham asya sāmarthyam anyat tatra samartham tad abhāvāt tad na bhūtam etad nivṛttau punar nivṛttiḥ yadṛcchā saṃvādaḥ mātṛ vivāha ucita deśa janmaḥ piṇḍa kharjūrasya deśa antareṣu mātṛ vivāha abhāve abhāvavat evam samarthitam tad tad kāryam sidhyati siddham sat sva sambhavena tad sambhavam sādhayati kāryasya kāraṇa avyabhicārāt avyabhicāre ca sva kāraṇaiḥ sarva kāryāṇām sadṛśaḥ nyāyaḥ evam asamarthanam kārya hetau api sādhana aṅga avacanam tad vādinaḥ parājaya sthānam asamarthite tasmin kāryatva asiddheḥ artha antarasya tad bhāva apratibaddha svabhāvasya bhāve tad bhāva niyama abhāvāt ārabdha artha asiddheḥ vastutas kāryasya api upādāne tad apratipādanāt anupalabdhau api pratipattuḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhi sādhanam samarthanam tādṛśyā eva anupalabdheḥ asad vyavahāra siddheḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya pratipattṛ pratyakṣa upalabdhi nivṛttau api abhāva asiddheḥ tatra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa antara sākalyam ca svabhāva viśeṣaḥ yad na trividhena viprakarṣeṇa viprakṛṣṭam yad anātma rūpa pratibhāsa vivekena pratipattṛ pratyakṣa pratibhāsa rūpam tādṛśaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha pratyayeṣu tathā anupalabdhaḥ asad vyavahāra viṣayaḥ tatas anyathā sati liṅge saṃśayaḥ atra api sarvam evaṃvidham asad vyavahāra viṣaya iti vyāptiḥ kasyacid asataḥ abhyupagame tal lakṣaṇa aviśeṣāt na hi evaṃvidhasya asattvān abhyupagame anyatra tasya yogaḥ na hi evaṃvidhasya sataḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu anupalabdhiḥ anupalabhyamāṇam tu īdṛśam na asti iti etāvat mātra nimittaḥ ayam asad vyavahāraḥ anyasya tad nimittasya abhāvāt sarva sāmarthya vivekaḥ nimittam iti ced evam etad tasya eva sarva sāmarthya vivekina evam pratītiḥ anyasya tad pratipatti upāya abhāvāt tad pratipattau ca satyām asad vyavahāra iti idam tad nimittam ucyate buddhi vyapadeśa artha kriyābhyaḥ sat vyavahāraḥ viparyaye ca asad vyavahāra iti ced bhavati buddheḥ yathā ukta pratibhāsāyāḥ sat vyavahāraḥ viparyaye asad vyavahāraḥ pratyakṣa aviṣaye tu syāl liṅga jāyā api kutaścid sat vyavahāraḥ asad vyavahāraḥ tu tad viparyaye anaikāntikaḥ viprakṛṣṭe arthe pratipattṛ pratyakṣasya anyasya vā pramāṇasya nivṛttau api saṃśayāt na ca sarve buddhi vyapadeśa as tad bheda abhedau vā vastu sattām vastu bheda abheda sattām vā sādhayanti asatsu api kathaṃcid atīta anāgata ādiṣu nānā eka artha kriyā kāriṣu vā artheṣu tad bhāva sthāpanāya nānā eka ātma abhāve api nānā eka rūpāṇām vṛtteḥ rājā mahā sammataḥ prabhavaḥ rāja vaṃśasya śaṅkhaḥ cakravarttī mahā sammata nirmitasya yūpasya utthāpayitā śaśa viṣāṇam rūpam sa nidarśanam sa pratigham ghaṭaś ca iti na hi sa nidarśana ādi śabdā nānā vastu viṣayā ekatra upasaṃhārāt nānā viṣaya tve api ekatra upasaṃhāraḥ tad nimittānān tatra samavāyāt iti ced āyāse vata ayam tapasvī padārthaḥ patitaḥ aneka sambandhinam upakṛtya anekam śabdam ātmani tebhyaḥ samāśaṃsan sa yaiḥ śakti bhedaiḥ anekam sambandhinam upakaroti taiḥ eva anekam śabdam kim na utthāpayati evam hi anena paraṃpara anusāra pariśramaḥ parihṛtaḥ bhavati nānā śabda utthāpana asāmarthye nānā sambandhy upakāraḥ api mā bhūt anupakāre hi teṣām tad sambandhi tā api na sidhyati ghaṭa iti api ca rūpa ādaya eva bahava eka artha kriyā kāriṇa eka śabda vācyā bhavantu kim artha antara kalpanayā bahavaḥ api hi eka artha kāriṇaḥ bhaveyuḥ cakṣuḥ ādivat tad sāmarthya sthāpanāya tatra eka śabda niyogaḥ api syāt iti yuktam paśyāmaḥ na ca niḥprayojanā lokasya artheṣu śabda yojanā tatra ye arthāḥ saha pṛthak vā eka prayojanās teṣām tad bhāva sthāpanāya hi eka śabdaḥ niyujyate yadi kim syāt tad artha kriyā śakti sthāpanāya niyuktasya samudāya śabdasya eka vacana virodhaḥ api na asti eva sahitānām sā śaktiḥ ekā na pratyekam iti samudāya śabda ekasmin samudāye vācye eka vacanam ghaṭa iti jāti śabdeṣu arthānām pratyekam sahitānām ca śakteḥ nānā ekā ca śaktiḥ iti nānā eka śakti vivakṣāyām bahu vacanam eka vacanam ca icchātaḥ vṛkṣā vṛkṣa iti syāt yadi eṣa niyamaḥ bahuṣu eva bahu vacanam ekasmin eka vacanam iti asmākan tu sāṃketikeṣu artheṣu saṃketa vaśād vṛttiḥ iti anabhiniveśa eva nānā ekaḥ rūpa ādiḥ eka śabda utthāpane śakta iti ced kim vai puruṣa vṛtteḥ anapekṣāḥ śabdān arthāḥ svayam utthāpayanti āhosvit puruṣaiḥ śabdā vyavahāra artham artheṣu niyujyante svayam utthāpane hi bhāva śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā cintyeta na ca tad yuktam puruṣaiḥ teṣām niyoge yatheṣṭam niyuñjīran iti kas tatra upālambhaḥ nimittam ca niyogasya uktam eva api ca yadi na rūpa ādīnām ekena śabdena sambandhaḥ katham ekena eṣām āśraya abhimatena dravyeṇa sambandha iti kevalam ayam asad bhūta abhiniveśa eva na vayam eka sambandha virodhāt ekam śabdam na icchāmaḥ api tu abhinnānām rūpa ādīnām ghaṭa kambala ādiṣu nānā artha kriyā śabda virodhāt ta eka rūpāḥ samudāya antara asambhāvinīm arthakriyām eva na kuryuḥ tena tad prakāśanāya ekaikena api śabdena na ucyeran bhavatu nāma kasyacid ayam vāñcchā bhaveyuḥ eka rūpā rūpa ādayaḥ sarva samudāyeṣu iti kim idam paraspara vivikta rūpa pratibhāsa adhiyakṣa darśanam enām upekṣate aniṣṭam ca idam rūpa ādīnām pratisamudāyam svabhāva bheda upagamāt yadi anya eva rūpa ādibhyaḥ ghaṭa iti ekaḥ syāt kim syāt astu pratyakṣasya sataḥ arūpa ādi rūpasya tad vivekena buddhau sva rūpeṇa pratibhāsena kim āvaraṇam pratibhā samānāḥ ca vivekena pratyakṣā arthā dṛśyante apṛthak deśa tve api gandha rasa ādayaḥ vāta ātapa sparśa ādayaś ca eka indriya grāhya tve api idam eva ca pratyakṣasya pratyakṣa tvam yad anātma rūpa vivekena svarūpasya buddhau samarpaṇam ayam punar ghaṭaḥ amūlya dāna krayī yaḥ svarūpam ca na upadarśayati pratyakṣatām ca svīkartum icchati etena buddhi śabda ādayaḥ api vyākhyātā yadi taiḥ tad sādhanam iṣyate na ca pratyakṣasya anabhibhave rūpa anupalakṣaṇam yena tad sādhanāya liṅgam ucyate apratyakṣa tve api apramāṇasya sattā upagamaḥ na yuktaḥ tad na rūpa ādibhyaḥ anyaḥ ghaṭaḥ evam tāvan na buddhi vyapadeśābhyām sattā vyavahāraḥ sattā bheda abheda vyavahāraḥ vā ata eva na tad viparyayāt viparyayaḥ artha kriyā atas tu sattā vyavahāraḥ syāt na sattā bheda abheda vyavahāraḥ ekasya api aneka artha kriyā darśanāt yathā pradīpasya vijñāna varti vikāra jvālā antara utpādanāni anekasya api cakṣuḥ ādeḥ eka vijñāna kriyā darśanāt na brūmaḥ artha kriyā bheda mātreṇa sattā bheda iti kim tarhi adṛṣṭa artha kriyā bhedena yā artha kriyā yasmin adṛṣṭā punar dṛśyate sā sattā bhedam sādhayati yathā mṛdy adṛṣṭā sati udaka dhāraṇa ādy artha kriyā ghaṭe dṛśyamānā adṛṣṭā api tantuṣu prāvaraṇa ādy artha kriyā paṭe dṛśyata iti sattā bhedaḥ sidhyati evam artha antaram tathā api avayavī na sidhyati yathāpratyayam saṃskāra santatau svabhāva bheda utpatteḥ artha kriyā bhedaḥ araṇi nirmathana avasthā bhedāt iva agneḥ sthūla karīṣa tṛṇa kāṣṭha dahana śakti bhedaḥ tathā yathāpratyayam svabhāva bheda utpatteḥ tantu ādiṣu artha kriyā bhedaḥ etena buddhi vyapadeśa bheda abhedau vyākhyātau tatra yad uktam artha kriyātaḥ sattā vyavahāra siddhiḥ viparyayāt viparyaya iti satyam etad sa eva tu viparyayaḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu na sidhyati tatra punar idam anicchataḥ api āyātam yasya idam sāmarthyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam san na upalabhyate saḥ asad vyavahāra viṣayaḥ sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt sattvasya iti tathā api kaḥ atiśayaḥ pūrvakāt asya na hi svabhāvāt artha antaram sāmarthyam tasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya yaḥ anupalambhaḥ sa svabhāvasya eva iti pūrvakā eva iyam anupalabdhiḥ tasmāt anena kvacid keṣāṃcid asad vyavahāram abhyupagacchatā atas anupalambhāt abhyupagantavyaḥ na vā kvacid viśeṣa abhāvāt saḥ anyatra api tathāvidhe aviśiṣṭa iti saḥ api tathā astu iti vyāptiḥ sarva evaṃvidhaḥ anupalabdhaḥ asad vyavahāra viṣaya iti na eva kaścid kvacid kathaṃcid anupalabdhaḥ api asad vyavahāra viṣaya iti ced sarvasya sarva rūpāṇām sarvadā anivṛtteḥ sarvam sarvatra sarvadā samupayujyeta idam ca na syāt idam atas na ata idam iha idam iha na idam idānīm idam idānīm na idam idam evam idam na evam iti kasyacid api rūpasya kathaṃcid kvacid kadācid viveka hetoḥ abhāvāt ananvaya vyatirekam viśvam syāt bheda abhāvāt avasthā nivṛtti pravṛtti bhedebhyaḥ vyavasthā iti ced nanu ta eva sarva viṣayasya asad vyavahārasya abhāvān na sambhavanti yatas tebhyaḥ vyavasthā syāt kvacid viṣaye asad vyavahāra upagame sa kuta iti vaktavyam na hi anupalambhāt anyaḥ vyavaccheda hetuḥ asti vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām vyavacchede sarvadā anupalambhasya eva sādhana tvāt anupalambhāt eva tad abhyupagame sa yatra eva asti sarvaḥ asad vyavahāra viṣaya iti vaktavyam viśeṣa abhāvāt sarva pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā yatra saḥ asad viṣaya iṣṭa iti ced sukumāra prajñaḥ devānāṃpriyaḥ na sahate pramāṇa cintā vyavahāra parikleśam yena na atra ādaram kṛtavān na hi anumāna ādi nivṛttiḥ abhāvam gamayati vyabhicārāt na sarva pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ asiddheḥ na ātma pratyakṣa aviśeṣa nivṛttiḥ api viprakṛṣṭeṣu tasmāt svabhāva viśeṣaḥ yatas pramāṇān niyamena sat vyavahāram pratipadyate tad nivṛttiḥ tasya asad vyavahāram sādhayati tad svabhāva sattāya as tad pramāṇa sat tayā vyāpteḥ na ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya arthasya pratyakṣāt anya upalabdhiḥ yena anumānāt asya upalabdhiḥ syāt na ca tad rūpa anyathābhāvam antareṇa apratyakṣatā anyathā abhāve ca tad eva na syāt api ca kuta idam amantra oṣadham indrajālam bhāvena śikṣitam yad ayam ajāta anaṣṭa rūpa atiśayaḥ avyavadhāna adūra sthāna s tasya eva tad avasthā indriya ādeḥ eva puruṣasya kadācid pratyakṣaḥ apratyakṣaḥ ca yena kadācid asya anumānam upalabdhiḥ kadācid pratyakṣam kadācid āgamaḥ etasmin eva anatiśaye amīṣām prakārāṇām virodhāt na anatiśaya eka atiśaya nivṛttyā apara atiśaya utpattyā ca vyavahāra bheda upagamāt saḥ atiśaya s tasya ātma bhūtaḥ ananvayaḥ nivartamānaḥ pravartamānaḥ ca katham na svabhāva nānātvam ākarṣayati sukha duḥkhavat sa anvaya tve ca kā kasya pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā iti yad kiṃcid etad athavā yadi kasyacid svabhāvasya pravṛtti nivṛttī svayam abhyanujñāyete tad eva paraḥ bruvāṇaḥ kim iti na anumanyate tasya niranvaya upajanana vināśa upagamāt iti ced kaḥ ayam anvayaḥ nāma bhāvasya janma vināśayoḥ śaktiḥ sā asti eva prāk api janmanaḥ nirodhāt api ūrdhvam tena ayam na apūrvaḥ sarvathā jāyate na pūrvaḥ vināśyati iti yadi sā sarvadā anatiśayā kim idānīm atiśayavat yad kṛtaḥ ayam vyavahāra vibhāgaḥ tā avasthā atiśayavatya iti ced tā avasthāḥ sā ca śaktiḥ kim ekaḥ bhāva āhosvin nānā ekaḥ ced katham idānīm idam ekatra avibhakta ātmani niṣparyāyam paraspara vyāhatam yokṣyate janma ajanma nivṛttiḥ anivṛttiḥ eka tvam nānā tvam pratyakṣatā apratyakṣatā artha kriyā upayogaḥ anupayogaḥ ca iti ādi asti paryāyaḥ avasthā śaktiḥ iti tena avirodha iti ced vismaraṇa śīlaḥ devānāṃpriyaḥ prakaraṇam na lakṣayati śaktiḥ avasthā iti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ avibhāga iti pakṣe ayam virodha uktaḥ atha asti anayoḥ vibhāgaḥ na kaścid virodhaḥ kevalam sa anvayau bhāvasya janma vināśau iti na syāt yasmāt yasya anvayaḥ na tasya janma vināśau yasya ca tau na tasya anvayaḥ tayoḥ abhedāt adoṣa iti ced anuttaram bata doṣa saṅkaṭam atrabhavān dṛṣṭi rāgeṇa praveśyamānaḥ api na ātmānam cetayati abhedaḥ hi nāma aikyam tau iti ca bheda adhiṣṭhānaḥ bhāvikaḥ vyavahāraḥ nivṛtti prādurbhāvayoḥ anivṛtti prādurbhāvau sthitau asthitiḥ iti ādikam nānātva lakṣaṇam ca katham yojyate eṣa hi bhāvānām bheda etad virahaḥ ca abhedaḥ yathā sukha ādiṣu śakty avasthayoḥ ca eka ātmani anyathā bheda abheda lakṣaṇa abhāvāt bheda abhedayoḥ avyavasthā syāt sarvatra tad ātmani prādurbhāvaḥ abhedaḥ viparyaye bhedaḥ yathā mṛd ātmani prādurbhavataḥ ghaṭasya tasmāt abhedaḥ bhedaḥ ca viparyaye sukha duḥkhayoḥ iti idam bheda abheda lakṣaṇam tena avirodha iti ced na vai mṛd ā ātmani ghaṭasya prādurbhāvaḥ kim tarhi mṛd ātmā eva kaścid ghaṭaḥ na hi ekas trailokye mṛd ātmā prativijñapti pratibhāsa bhedāt dravya svabhāva bhedāt evam hi asya api sukha ādiṣu caitanyeṣu ca bheda avagamaḥ samarthaḥ bhavati yadi evam bhedaḥ syāt sati api etasmin kasyacid ātmanaḥ anvayāt aikyam iti ced sukha ādiṣu api ayam prasaṅgaḥ caitanyeṣu ca na ca ghaṭa ādiṣu api sarva ātmanā anvayaḥ avaiśvarūpya saha utpatty ādi prasaṅgāt na ca ghaṭam mṛd ātmānam ca kaścid vivekena upalakṣayati yena evam syāt idam iha prādurbhūtam iti na hi adhiṣṭhāna adhiṣṭhāninoḥ vivekena anupalakṣaṇe evam bhavati na ca śakteḥ śakty ātmani prādurbhāva iti tasyāḥ sva ātmanaḥ abhedaḥ na syāt etena pariṇāmaḥ pratyuktaḥ yaḥ api hi kalpayet yaḥ yasya pariṇāmaḥ sa tasmāt abhinna iti na hi śakteḥ ātma apariṇāma iti kim ca idam uktam bhavati pariṇāma iti avasthitasya dravyasya dharma antara nivṛttiḥ dharma antara prādurbhāvaḥ ca pariṇāmaḥ yad tad dharma antaram nivartate prādurbhavati ca kim tad tad eva avasthitam dravyam syāt tatas artha antaram vā anya vikalpa abhāvāt yadi tad tad eva tasya avasthānam na nivṛtti prādurbhāvau iti kasya tau iti vaktavyam avasthitasya dharma antaram iti ca na sidhyati na hi tad eva tasya anapāśrita vyapekṣa abhedam dharma antaram bhavati atha dravyāt artha antaram dharmaḥ tadā tasya nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām na dravyasya pariṇatiḥ na hi artha antara gatābhyām nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām artha antarasya pariṇatiḥ caitanye api prasaṅgāt dravyasya dharma iti ca vyapadeśaḥ na sidhyati sambandha abhāvāt na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt anyaḥ vastu sambandhaḥ asti na ca anayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ svayam atada ātmanaḥ atat kāraṇa tvāt dharmasya dravyāt artha antara bhūta tvāt artha antara tve api dharma kāraṇa tve dharma antarasya kāryasya utpādanāt dravyasya pariṇāma iti iṣṭam syāt tad aviruddham anyasya api hetu phala santāne mṛd dravya ākhye pūrvakān mṛt piṇḍa dravyāt kāraṇāt uttarasya ghaṭa dravyasya kāryasya utpattau mṛd dravyam pariṇatam iti vyavahārasya upagamāt na ca dharmasya dravyāt tattva anya tvābhyām anyaḥ vikalpaḥ sambhavati ubhayathā api na pariṇāmaḥ na nirvivekam dravyam eva dharmaḥ na api dravyāt artha antaram kim tarhi dravyasya saṃniveśaḥ avasthā antaram yathā aṅgulīnām muṣṭiḥ na hi aṅguly eva nirvivekā muṣṭiḥ prasāritānām amuṣṭi tvāt na api artha antaram pṛthak svabhāvena anupalabdheḥ iti ced na muṣṭeḥ aṅguli viśeṣa tvāt aṅgulya eva hi kāścid muṣṭiḥ na sarvāḥ na hi prasāritā aṅgulyaḥ nirviveka svabhāvā muṣṭy aṅgulyaḥ avasthā dvaye api ubhaya pratipatti prasaṅgāt ya eva hi khalu vivekaḥ svabhāva bhūtaḥ sa eva vastu bheda lakṣaṇam sukha duḥkhavat para bhūte ca viveka utpāde aṅgulyaḥ prasāritā eva upalabhyeran na hi svayam svabhāvāt acyutasya artha antara utpāde anyathā upalabdhiḥ atiprasaṅgāt nanu uktam na dravyam eva nirvivekam avasthā na api dravyāt artha antaram iti uktam idam na punar yuktam na hi sataḥ vastunaḥ tattva anya tve muktvā anyaḥ prakāraḥ sambhavanti tayoḥ vastuni paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa tvena eka tyāgasya apara upādāna na antarīyaka tvāt aṅgulīṣu punar pratikṣaṇa vināśinīṣu anyā eva prasāritāḥ anyā muṣṭiḥ tatra muṣṭy ādi śabdā viśeṣa viṣayāḥ aṅgulī śabdaḥ sāmānya viṣayaḥ bīja aṅkura ādi śabdavat vrīhi ādi śabda vac ca tena aṅgulyaḥ prasāritā na muṣṭiḥ tad yadi prāk asad eva kāraṇe kāryam bhavet kim na sarvaḥ sarvasmāt bhavati na hi asattve kaścid viśeṣa iti nanu sarvatra sarvasya sattve api ayam tulyaḥ doṣaḥ na hi sattve kaścid viśeṣaḥ viśeṣe vā sa viśeṣas traiguṇyāt bhinnaḥ syāt tad bhāve viśeṣasya ananvayāt sataś ca sarva ātmanā niṣpanna avasthāyām iva kim jāyate sādhana vaiphalyam ca sādhyasya kasyacid abhāvāt yasya kasyacid atiśayasya tatra kathaṃcid asata utpattau saḥ atiśaya s tatra asan katham jāyate jātau vā sarvaḥ sarvasmāj jāyeta iti tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ na atiśaya s tatra sarvathā na asti kathaṃcid sata eva bhāvāt iti ced yathā na asti sa prakāraḥ tatra asan katham jāyeta na ca sarvathā sataḥ kaścid janma artha iti uktam asataḥ api kāryasya kāraṇāt utpāde yaḥ yaj janana svabhāvaḥ tatas eva tasya janma na anyasmāt iti niyamaḥ tasya api sa svabhāva niyamaḥ sva hetoḥ iti anādi bhāva svabhāva niyamaḥ api ca yadi mṛt piṇḍe ghaṭaḥ asti katham tad avasthāyām na paścātvat upalabdhiḥ tad artha kriyā vā vyakteḥ aprādurbhāvāt iti ced tasya eva tad artha kriyā ādi bhāve ghaṭa tvāt tad rūpasya ca prāk asattvāt katham ghaṭaḥ asti na hi rūpa antarasya sattve rūpa antaram asti na ca rūpa pratibhāsa bhede vastu abhedaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt tasmāt ya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta svabhāvaḥ anupalabdhaḥ sa na asti eva na hi tasya tad svabhāva sthitau anupalabdhiḥ tad asthitiḥ ca atattvam paraspara svabhāva asthitayoḥ iva duḥkha sukhayoḥ iti vyāptiḥ asad vyavahāra niścayena anupalabdhi viśeṣasya tena anupalabdhyā kasyacid vyavacchedam prasādhayatā tasya yathā ukta upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ upadarśa niyā upadarśya anupalabdhi nirdeśaḥ samarthanam svabhāva anupalabdhau vyāpaka anupalabdhau api dharmayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvam prasādhya vyāpakasya nivṛtti prasādhanam samarthanam kāraṇa anupalabdhau api kārya kāraṇa bhāvam prasādhya kāraṇasya nivṛtti prasādhanam samarthanam tad viruddha upalabdhiṣu api dvayoḥ viruddhayoḥ ekasya viruddhasya upadarśanam samarthanam evam anupalabdhau sādhana aṅgasya asamarthanam sādhana aṅga avacanam tad vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam asamarthane tasmin sādhya asiddheḥ athavā sādhyate tena pareṣām apratītaḥ artha iti sādhanam trirūpa hetu vacana samudāyaḥ tasya aṅgam pakṣa dharma ādi vacanam tasya ekasya api avacanam asādhana aṅga vacanam tad api vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam tad avacane hetu rūpasya eva avacanena siddheḥ abhāvāt athavā tasya eva sādhanasya yad na aṅgam pratijñā upanaya nigamana ādi tasya asādhana aṅgasya sādhana vākye upādānam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam vyartha abhidhānāt anvaya vyatirekayoḥ vā sādharmyavati vaidharmyavati ca sādhana prayoga ekasya eva abhidhānena siddheḥ bhāvāt dvitīyasya asāmarthyam iti tasya api asādhana aṅgasya abhidhānam nigraha sthānam vyartha abhidhānāt eva nanu ca viṣaya upadarśanāya pratijñā vacanam asādhana aṅgam api upadeyam eva na vaiyarthyāt asati api pratijñā vacane yathā uktāt sādhana vākyāt bhavati eva iṣṭa artha siddhiḥ iti apārthakam tasya upādānam yadi ca viṣaya upadarśanam antareṇa pratīteḥ anutpattiḥ katham na pratijñā sādhana avayavaḥ na hi pakṣa dharma ādi vacanasya api prati iti hetu bhāvāt anyaḥ sādhana arthaḥ sa pratijñā vacane api tulya iti katham na sādhanam kevalasya asāmarthyāt asādhana tvam iti ced tad tulyam pakṣa dharma vacanasya api iti tad api na sādhana avayavaḥ syāt na hi pakṣa dharma vacanāt kevalāt pratipatteḥ utpattiḥ etena saṃśaya utpattiḥ pratyuktā pakṣa dharma vacanāt api kevalāt apradarśite sambandhe saṃśaya utpatteḥ tasmāt vyartham eva sādhana vākye pratijñā vacana upādānam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam athavā sādhanasya siddheḥ yad na aṅgam asiddhaḥ viruddhaḥ anaikāntikaḥ vā hetvābhāsaḥ tasya api vacanam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam asamartha upādānāt tathā sādhya ādi vikalasya ananvaya apradarśita anvaya ādeḥ api dṛṣṭānta ābhāsasya asādhana aṅgasya vacanam api vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam asamartha upādānāt eva na hi taiḥ hetoḥ sambandhaḥ śakyate pradarśayitum apradarśanāt asāmarthyam athavā siddhiḥ sādhanam tad aṅgam dharmaḥ yasya arthasya vivāda āśrayasya vāda prastāva hetoḥ sa sādhana aṅgaḥ tad vyatirekeṇa aparasya api ajijñāsitasya viśeṣasya śāstra āśraya vyāja ādibhiḥ prakṣepaḥ ghoṣaṇam ca para vyāmohana anubhāṣaṇa śakti vighāta ādi hetoḥ tad api asādhana aṅga vacanam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam aprastuta abhidhānāt tathā viśeṣa sahitasya arthasya prativādinaḥ ajijñāsita tvāt jijñāsāyām adoṣaḥ jijñāsitam punar arthasya anyasya prasaṅga paraṃparayā yeṣa panna ādinā bahis prativādinaḥ prāśnikānām ca nyāya darśinām iti ebhiḥ kathā viccheda eva karaṇīyaḥ na hi kaścid arthaḥ kvacid kriyamāṇa prasaṅge na prayujyate nairātmya vādinaḥ tu tad sādhane nṛtya gīty ādeḥ api tatra prasaṅgāt yathā pratijñā abhidhāna pūrvakam kaścid kuryāt na asti ātmā iti vayam bauddhā brūmaḥ ke bauddhāḥ ye buddhasya bhagavataḥ śāsanam abhyupagatāḥ kaḥ buddhaḥ bhagavān yasya śāsane bhadanta aśva ghoṣaḥ pravrajitaḥ kaḥ punar bhadanta aśva ghoṣaḥ yasya rāṣṭra pālam nāma nāṭakam kīdṛśam rāṣṭra pālam nāma nāṭakam iti prasaṅgam kṛtvā nāndyante tatas praviśati sūtradhāra iti paṭhet nṛtyet gāyet ca prativādī tam ca sarva prasaṅgam na anukartum samartha iti parājitaḥ syāt iti sabhyaḥ sādhu sammatānām viduṣām tadtva cintā prakāraḥ na ca evam prastutasya paryavasānam sambhavati aniścaya phala tvāt anārambha eva vādasya katham ca evam jaya parājayau prativādinaḥ api ananubhāṣaṇasya evaṃprakārasya prasaṅgasya vistareṇa anubhāṣaṇa vyājena sambhavāt aniścita tvāt ca tasmāt pratijñā vacanam eva tāvan na nyāyyam kutas punar tatra ajijñāsita viśeṣa prasaṅga upanyāsas tad vyākhyā prasaṅga vitatha pralāpaḥ ca sarvaś ca ayam prakāraḥ durmatibhiḥ śaṭhaiḥ nyāya sāmarthyena artha pratipādane asamarthaiḥ pravartitaḥ yathā puruṣa atiśaya pūrvakāni tanu karaṇa bhuvana ādīni iti pratijñāya tanu karaṇa bhuvana vyākhyā vyājena sakala vaiśeṣika śāstra artha ghoṣaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ vā iti vāde dvādaśa lakṣaṇa prapañca prakāśana śāstra praṇetuḥ jaimini pratijñata tadtva nitya tā adhikaraṇa śabda ghaṭa anyatara sa dvitīyaḥ ghaṭa iti pratijñām uparacayya dvādaśa lakṣaṇa artha vyākhyānam sarvaḥ ayam durmatīnām asāmarthya pracchādana upāyaḥ na tu satyaiḥ asti upetaḥ tadtva parīkṣāyām phala ādi pratisaraṇa daṇḍa prayoga ādīnām ayukta tvāt bhavati eva nāṭaka ādi ghoṣaṇe artha antara gamanāt parājaya iti ced anyasya api ajijñāsitasya kim na bhavati na hi asya api kācid vivakṣita sādhya dharma siddhau na antarīyaka tā yathā hetu pratyaya pāratantrya lakṣaṇa saṃskāra duḥkha tā ādi siddhim antareṇa na anitya tā siddhiḥ tathāvidhas tu dharmaḥ pṛthak anuktaḥ api sādhya dharme antar bhāvāt pakṣīkṛta eva iti na pṛthak asya upanyāsaḥ vyākhyānam vā tasmāt evaṃvidhasya api tadānīm prativādinā ajijñāsitasya arthasya pratijñāyām anyatra vā upanyāsaḥ vyākhyānam vā artha antara gamanān nigraha sthānam eva tena jijñāsita dharma mātram eva sādhana aṅgam vācyam na prasaṅga upakṣeptavyaḥ tad upakṣepe atiprasaṅgāt evam asādhana aṅga vacanam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam prativādinā tathā abhāve pratipādite anyathā dvayoḥ ekasya api na jaya parājaya av iti adoṣa udbhāvanam prativādinaḥ nigraha sthānam vādinā sādhane prayukte abhyupagata uttara pakṣaḥ yatra viṣaye prativādī yadā na doṣam udbhāvayati tadā parājitaḥ vaktavyaḥ sādhana doṣāḥ punar nyūna tvam asiddhiḥ anaikāntika tā vādinaḥ sādhayitum iṣṭasya arthasya viparyaya sādhanam aṣṭādaśa dṛṣṭānta doṣaḥ ca teṣām anudbhāvanam apratyāyanam apratipādanam prativādinaḥ parājaya adhikaraṇam tad punar sādhanasya nirdoṣa tvāt sa doṣa tve api prativādinaḥ ajñānāt pratipādana asāmarthyāt vā na hi duṣṭa sādhana abhidhāne api vādinaḥ prativādinaḥ apratipādite doṣe parājaya vyavasthāpanā yuktā tayoḥ eva paraspara sāmarthya upaghāta apekṣayā jaya parājaya vyavasthāpanāt kevalam hetvābhāsāt bhūta pratipatteḥ abhāvāt apratipādakasya jayaḥ api na asti eva na hi tadtva cintāyām kaścid chala vyavahāraḥ yadi evam kim na parājayaḥ tadtva siddhi bhraṃśāt na anirākaraṇāt nirākaraṇam hi tasya anyena parājayaḥ na siddhy abhāvaḥ pratiyogi anapekṣaṇāt siddhy abhāvasya sādhana abhāve asati api pratiyogini bhāvāt pratiyoginaḥ ca tad nirākaraṇe asāmarthyāt parājayasya anutpatteḥ aparājayaḥ tasmāt ayam asamartha sādhana abhidhāyy api pareṇa tathā abhāve apratipādite aparājitaḥ vaktavyaḥ chala vyavahāre api vijigīṣūṇām vāda iti ced na durjana vipratipatty adhikāre satām śāstra pravṛtteḥ na hi para anugraha pravṛttā mithyā pralāpa ārambha ātma utkarṣa para paṃsana ādīn asad vyavahārān upadiśanti na ca para vipaṃsanena lābha satkāra śloke upārjanam satām ācāraḥ na api tathā pravṛttebhyaḥ sva hasta dānena prāṇinām upatāpanam sat sammatānām śāstra kāra sabhā sadām yuktam na ca nyāya śāstrāṇi sadbhiḥ lābha ādy upārjanāya praṇīyante tasmāt na yoga vihitaḥ kaścid vijigīṣu vādaḥ nāma para anugraha pravṛttā aḥ tu santaḥ vipratipannam pratipādayantaḥ nyāyam anusareyuḥ sat sādhana abhidhānena bhūta doṣa udbhāvanena vā sākṣi pratyakṣam tasya eva anuprabodhāya tad eva nyāya anusaraṇam satām vādaḥ ukta nyāye tadtva arthī ced pratipadyeta tad apratipattau api anyaḥ na pratipadyeta iti tadtva rakṣaṇa artham sadbhiḥ upahartavyam eva chala ādi vijigīṣubhiḥ iti ced na nakha capeṭa śastra prahāra ādīpana ādibhiḥ api iti vaktavyam tasmāt na jyāyān ayam tadtva rakṣaṇa upāyaḥ sādhana prakhyāpanam satām tadtva rakṣaṇa upāyaḥ sādhana ābhāsa dūṣaṇam ca tad abhāve mithyā pralāpāt atra para upatāpa vidhāne api tadtva apratiṣṭhāpanāt anyathā api nyāya upavarṇane vidvat pratiṣṭhānāt tasmāt para anugrahāya tadtva khyāpanam vādinaḥ vijayaḥ bhūta doṣa darśanena mithyā pratipatti nivartanam prativādinaḥ athavā yaḥ na doṣaḥ sādhanasya tad bhāve api vādinā sādhayitum iṣṭasya arthasya siddheḥ vighāta abhāvāt tasya udbhāvanam prativādinaḥ nigraha adhikaraṇam mithyā uttara abhidhānāt yathā sādhya tayā aniṣṭaḥ api vādinaḥ dharmaḥ śāstra upagamāt sādhya iti tad viparyāsena virodha udbhāvanam na asti ātmā iti tava pratijñā padayoḥ virodha iti pratijñā doṣa udbhāvanam prayatna anantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ prayatna anantarīyaka tvāt iti hetoḥ dharma viśeṣa tvāt pratijñā artha eka deśa iti asiddha udbhāvanam sarvāṇi sādharmya vaidharmya sama ādīni jāty uttarāṇi iti evam ādeḥ doṣasya udbhāvanam adoṣa udbhāvanam tasya vādinā doṣa ābhāsa tve prakhyāpite prativādī parājitaḥ vaktavyaḥ pūrva pakṣe sādhanasya nirdoṣa tvāt doṣavati punar sādhane na dvayoḥ ekasya api jaya parājayau tadtva aprakhyāpanāt adoṣa udbhāvanā t ca apratipakṣāyām ca pakṣa siddhau kṛtāyām jetā bhavati tasmāt jigīṣatā sva pakṣaḥ ca sthāpanīyaḥ para pakṣaḥ ca nirākartavyaḥ nirdoṣe sādhana abhidhāne api vādinaḥ prativādinā doṣa ābhāsa udbhāvite dūṣaṇa ābhāsatva khyāpana eva jaya parājayau na anyathā bhāvatas tadtva abhidhāne api pratipakṣa nirākaraṇena tattvasya prakhyāpana asāmarthyāt na prativādinaḥ api atra bhāvataḥ mithyā pratipatteḥ iti idam nyāyyam nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇam uktam asmābhiḥ anyat tu na yuktam iti na iṣyate yatra idam yathā uktam nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇam na asti tasya nigraha sthāna tvam ayuktam iti na uktam asmābhiḥ pratidṛṣṭānta dharma abhyanujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñā ahāniḥ nigraha sthānam iti atra bhāṣya kāra matam dūṣayitvā vārttikakāraḥ ayam sthita pakṣam āha tam eva brūmaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntasya yaḥ dharmas tam yadā sva dṛṣṭānte abhyanujānāti nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ tatra dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau ante ca vyavasthita iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ sva dṛṣṭāntaḥ sva pakṣaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ pratipakṣaḥ pratipakṣasya dharmam sva pakṣe abhyanujānan parājitaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt iti brūvan pratipakṣa vādini sāmānyena pratyavasthite āha yadi sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam śabdaḥ api evam astu iti eṣā pratijñāhāniḥ prāk pratijñātasya śabda anitya tvasya tyāgāt iti atra upagata pratijñā tyāgāt pratijñāhānau viśeṣa pratiniyamaḥ kim kṛtaḥ anena prakāreṇa pratijñām tyajataḥ pratijñā ahāniḥ iti sambhavati hi anyena api prakāreṇa hetu doṣa udbhāvana ādinā pratipakṣa sādhana abhidhānena ca sva pakṣa parityāgaḥ para pakṣa upagamaḥ ca idam eva ca pratijñā hāneḥ pradhānam nimittam evam pratipāditena pratijñā hātavyā hānau ca parājaya iti idam punar asambaddham eva sāmānyam nityam aindriyakam iti ukte śabdaḥ api evam astu iti kaḥ svastha ātmā svayam aindriyaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ ghaṭavat iti bruvan sāmānyena upadarśana mātreṇa nityam śabdam pratipadyate sāmānyasya api nityasya aindriyaka tve api anitye ghaṭe darśanāt saṃśayitaḥ syāt jāḍyāt pratipadyeta api iti ced tathā api kim sāmānyasya upadarśanena evam eva nityaḥ śabda iti vaktavyam jaḍasya pratipattau vicāra abhāvāt na ca nitya sāmānya upadarśanena tad dharmam śabde pratipadyamāne pratipakṣa dharma abhyanujñātaḥ bhavati anityaḥ śabda iti ca vadataḥ nityaḥ śabda iti āñjasaḥ pratipakṣaḥ syāt na nityam sāmānyam iti tasmāt aindriyaka tvasya nitya anitya pakṣa vṛtteḥ vyabhicārāt asādhana aṅgasya upādānān nigraha arhaḥ na pratipakṣa dharma anujñayā anena prakāreṇa pratijñā hāneḥ pratijñā artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñā antaram pratijñātaḥ arthaḥ anityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt iti eva tasya hetu vyabhicāra upadarśanena pratiṣedhe kṛte dharma bheda vikalpāt sāmānya ghaṭayoḥ sarva gatatva asarva gatatva dharma vikalpena pratijñā antaram karoti yathā ghaṭaḥ asarva gataḥ anitya eva śabdaḥ api asarva gataḥ anitya iti etad pratijñā antaram nāma nigraha sthānam sādhana sāmarthye api aparijñānāt sa hi pūrvasya anityaḥ śabda iti pratijñāyāḥ sādhanāya uttarām asarva gataḥ śabda iti pratijñām āha tad darśanāya tad artha nirdeśa iti āha tad arthaḥ pūrva ukta sādhya siddhy artha uttara pratijñā nirdeśa s tad artha nirdeśaḥ na ca pratijñā pratijñā antara sādhane samarthā iti nigraha sthānam atra api na evam bruvatā pratijñā antaram pūrva pratijñā sādhanāya uktam bhavati kim tarhi viśeṣaṇam aindriyaka tvasya hetoḥ sāmānye vṛttyā vyabhicāra udbhāvite asarva gata tve sati aindriyaka tvasya hetoḥ viśeṣaṇa upādāne vyabhicāram pariharati na punar pratijñā antaram āha asarva gata tvasya śabde siddha tvāt pratijñāya aś ca sādhya nirdeśa lakṣaṇa tvāt yad api uktam pūrva pratijñā sādhanāya uttarām pratijñām āha iti tad api ayuktam na hi pratijñā pratijñā sādhanāya ucyamānā pratijñā antaram bhavati kim tarhi hetv ādeḥ ananyatamaḥ sādhya sādhanāya upādānāt sādhana nirdeśaḥ sa syāt na sādhya nirdeśaḥ udāharaṇa sādharmya ādeś ca hetu lakṣaṇasya asarvaga tve bhāvāt pratijñā lakṣaṇasya ca abhāvāt hetu tvam asarvaga tve prayuktam na pratijñā antara tvam atyanta asambaddham ca idam pratijñām pratijñā sādhanāya āha iti yaḥ hi prāk pratijñām uktvā hetu udāharaṇa ādikam vaktum jānāti sa kiṃcid anukramam sādhanasya jānāti eva hi jānan katham avikala antaḥkaraṇaḥ pratijñām eva pratijñā sādhanāya upādadīta upādadatā ca anena pratijñā mātreṇa siddhiḥ iṣṭā bhavati tatas ca na prāk api hetum brūyāt evaṃprakāraṇām asambaddhānām parisaṃkhyātum aśakya tvāt lakṣaṇa niyamaḥ api asambaddha eva pratijñā antara abhidhāne pratijñā antaram nāma nigraha sthānam iti asambaddha abhidhānam nigraha sthānam iti evaṃprakārāṇām ekam eva lakṣaṇam vācyam syāt na ca evaṃvidhaḥ kaścid vivādeṣu dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ vyavahāraḥ yena tad artham yatnaḥ kriyate na ca bāla pralāpa anudiśya śāstram pravartate pravṛttau ca kā niṣṭhā teṣām aniṣṭānāt dṛśyate ca viduṣām api na ati nirūpaṇāt asiddha abhidhānam iti vyavahāra darśanāt tādṛśam parājaya adhikaraṇam vyavasthāpyate tasmāt iha api yadi nivṛtta ākāṅkṣe vādini paraḥ anaikāntika tām udbhāvayet asādhana aṅgasya anaikāntikasya abhidhānān nigraha sthānam vādinaḥ evam yadi prativādī sat sāmānyam aindriyakam nityam ca pramāṇena pratipādayitum śaknuyāt anudiśya apramāṇakam śāstra upagamam pramāṇena eṣām arthānām apratipādane na bhūta doṣa udbhāvanam iti na kaścid parājayaḥ abhyupagama mātreṇa vastu siddheḥ abhāvāt prativādinā doṣasya apratipādita tvāt pramāṇaiḥ asamarthita sādhana abhidhānāt tu jetā api na bhavati iti anitya ākāṅkṣe punar vādini na kaścid doṣaḥ viśeṣaṇa abhidhānena hetoḥ samarthana upakramāt pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pratijñā virodhaḥ yathā guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti pratijñā rūpa ādibhyaḥ artha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti hetuḥ saḥ ayam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ etena eva pratijñā virodhaḥ api uktaḥ yatra pratijñā sva vacanena virudhyate yathā śramaṇā garbhiṇī na asti ātmā iti vā hetu virodhaḥ api yatra pratijñayā hetuḥ virudhyate yathā sarvam pṛthak samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti etena pratijñayā dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ api vyākhyātaḥ hetoḥ ca dṛṣṭānta ādibhiḥ virodhaḥ pramāṇa virodhaḥ ca pratijñā hetvoḥ vaktavyaḥ para pakṣe sva siddhena gaḥtva ādinā anaikāntika codanād virodhaḥ yaḥ para pakṣam sva siddhena gaḥtva ādinā vyabhicārayati tad viruddham uttaram veditavyam sva pakṣa anapekṣam ca yaḥ ca sva pakṣa anapekṣam hetum prayuṅkte anityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt iti tasya sva siddhasya gaḥtva ādeḥ anityatva virodhāt viruddhaḥ ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannas tu anaikāntikaḥ yad ubhaya pakṣa pratipannam vastu tena anaikāntika codanā iti atra api pratijñāyāḥ sādhana vākye prayoga pratiṣedhāt tad āśrayas tad kṛtaḥ vā hetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ na virodha iti na pratijñā virodhaḥ nāma kiṃcid nigraha sthānam syāt etad asati api pratijñā prayoge gamyamānaḥ api pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ bhavati yathā rūpa ādibhyaḥ artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ tad guṇa vyatiriktam na upalabhyate ca rūpa ādibhyaḥ artha antaram dravyam iti ukte api gamyata eva sādhya sādhanayoḥ virodhaḥ katham tatas artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ tad vyatirekaḥ ca iti satyam syāt ayam virodhaḥ yadi hetuḥ sādhya dharma viparyayam sādhayet yadi hi upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvena upagatasya sataḥ dravyasya rūpa ādi pratibhāsa vivekena sva pratibhāsa anupalabdhiḥ tad tad vyatirekeṇa na asti iti iṣṭa vyatireka viparyaya sādhanāt viruddhaḥ hetuḥ asmābhiḥ ukta eva iti bhavati eva idam nigraha adhikaraṇam yadi evaṃvidhaḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ virodha iṣṭaḥ atha punar asya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ lupyate tadā na kaścid pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ vyatiriktānām api bhāvānām kutaścid viprakarṣiṇām tad vyatirekeṇa anupalabdhau api vyatirekasya bhāvāt yad uktam pratijñāyāḥ sva vacana virodhe pratijñā virodha iti tatra idam eva nigraha adhikaraṇam asādhana aṅga bhūtāyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ sādhana vākye prayogaḥ na virodhaḥ tad adhikaraṇa tvāt yadi pratijñā anapekṣaḥ virodhaḥ syāt syāt parājaya āśrayaḥ pratijñā adhikaraṇa tve punar tad prayoga kṛta eva parājayaḥ asya prastāva upasaṃhāra avasāna tvāt vyartham virodha udbhāvanam parājita parājaya abhāvāt bhasmīkṛta prajvalanavat ye tu kecid vicāra prasaṅgeṣu ekatra sādhye bahavaḥ hetava ucyante teṣām vikalpena tad sādhya sādhanāya vṛtteḥ sāmarthyam anyathā dvitīyasya vaiyarthyāt yadi hi tatra api eka prayogam antareṇa aparasya prayogaḥ na sambhavet na tadā dvitīyasya kaścid sādhana arthaḥ pratīta pratipādana abhāvāt tasmāt na pratijñāyāḥ sva vacana virodhaḥ nāma kiṃcid nigraha sthānam na ca na asti ātmā iti atra kaścid pratijñā virodhaḥ na asti ātma śabda arthasya bhāva upādānatva niṣedhāt śabda artha niṣedhe hi virodhaḥ syāt na ca sva lakṣaṇam śabda artha iti yaḥ punar pratijñayā bādhanāt hetu virodha uktaḥ yathā sarvam pṛthak samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti na atra pratijñāyāḥ prayogaḥ na api hetoḥ yena virodhaḥ syāt kim tarhi pratipādita artha upadarśanena upasaṃhāra vacanam etasmāt anyaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ śabdasya eka viśeṣa anabhidhānam aneka artha sāmānya abhidhānam ca pratipādya sarvasya śabda arthasya nānā artha rūpa tayā eka vastu viśeṣa svabhāva tā bhāvam upadarśayan śabda artham adhikṛtya sarvam pṛthak iti brūyāt etena tad virodhaḥ pratyuktaḥ dṛṣṭānta upadarśanam ca etad anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka anitya tvāt iti yathā kvacid arthe vipratipattau prasiddham aneka artha sāmānye śabda prayogam upadarśya pratipādita vipratipatti sthānaḥ sāmānyena upasaṃharati sarvam pṛthak iti yadi dṛṣṭānta prayogaḥ kim ṛjunā eva tad prayoga krameṇa na prayuktaḥ vipratipatti viṣaya ś ca kim na darśita iti ced na samāsa nirdeśāt evam api prayoga darśanāt asādhana vākya tvāt ca ata eva na pratijñayā hetoḥ bādhanam na ca ekam eva kiṃcid na asti iti bruvāṇaḥ kaścid tad samuccaya rūpam ekam samūham icchati yena virodhaḥ syāt yaḥ api yugapad ṣaṭkena yogāt iti ādinā paramāṇoḥ bhedam āha na tasya api ekaḥ samuccaya rūpaḥ sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ kim tarhi abhāva eva eka aneka pratiṣedhāt atas saḥ api na samūha s tasya iṣṭaḥ na tatra śabda iti na virodhaḥ na virodhaḥ ayam pūrvakāt pratijñā hetu virodhāt bhidyate yena pṛthak ucyeta tatra hetu pratijñāya ūr bādhanam iha pratijñayā hetoḥ iti asti bheda iti ced artha virodhe hi hetu pratijñayoḥ bādhya bādaka bhāvaḥ syāt sarvaḥ artha virodhaḥ dviṣv iti api parasparam bādhakam eka artha saṃnidhau apara arthā sambhavāt tatra hetu pratijñāyoḥ pṛthak bādha udāharaṇayoḥ na kaścid artha bhedaḥ api ca ayam viruddhaḥ aviruddhaḥ vā sati hetu prayoge vyadhikaraṇa tvāt asiddha iti asiddha tā hetoḥ nigraha sthānam sa khalu ucyamāna eva atad dharma tayā pratītaḥ vaktuḥ parājayam ānayati parājite tasmin tad artha virodha cintayā na kiṃcid api ca sarvatra ayam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ sambhavan na dvayīm hetu doṣa jātim atipatati viruddha tām asiddha tām ca iti viruddha tā siddhe hetoḥ dharmiṇi bhāve sādhya dharma viparyaya eva bhāvena pratijñā artha virodhāt asiddha tā punar dharmiṇi pratijñātā artha siddhau viruddhayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ ekatra asambhavāt na ca anyathā virodhaḥ asiddhe dharmi svabhāve abhihitayoḥ hetu pratijñā arthayoḥ virodhāt virodha sambhava iti ced apramāṇa yoge tu ubhayoḥ dharmiṇi saṃśayaḥ tathā sati hetoḥ dharmiṇi bhāva saṃśaye asiddha tā eva hetu doṣa iti asiddha viruddhābhyām anyaḥ na pratijñayā virodhaḥ nāma parājaya hetuḥ asiddha viruddhe ca hetv ābhāsa vacanāt eva ukta iti na pṛthak pratijñā virodhaḥ vaktavya iti ubhaya āśrita tvāt virodhasya vivakṣātaḥ anyatara nirdeśa iti ced syāt etad pratijñā hetvoḥ virodha iti pratijñā hetū āśritya ubhaya āśrayaḥ bhavati tatra yadā pratijñā virodhaḥ vivakṣita s tadā pratijñā virodha iti ucyate yadā pratijñāyā hetoḥ vā virodha s tadā viruddhaḥ hetuḥ iti atas pratijñā virodhaḥ hetu virodhaḥ vā iti adoṣaḥ tatra hetoḥ udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabda utpatti dharmaka tvāt iti pratijñā virodhasya na asti ātmā iti pratijñā hetvoḥ paraspara viruddha udāharaṇam guṇa vyatiriktam iti ādi pratijñayā hetu virodha udāharaṇam na asti ekaḥ bhāva iti ādikam iti na sarvatra hetv apekṣasya virodhasya hetv ābhāsa anatikramāt yathā uktam prāk anapekṣe ca kevale svatas pratijñā virodhe vivakṣite pratijñā hetvoḥ virodha iti hetu grahaṇam asambaddham na ca utpatti dharmaka tvān nityam iti atra api hetu virodhaḥ yuktaḥ pratijñayā hi hetoḥ bādhane hetu virodhaḥ iha tu hetunā pratijñā bādhyata iti pratijñā virodhaḥ yuktaḥ ubhaya āśraye api virodhe bādhyamāna vivakṣayā tad virodha vyavasthāpanāt yad api uktam etena pratijñayā dṛṣṭānta virodha ādayaḥ api vaktavyā bhaṇḍālekhya nyāyena iti tatra api pakṣīkṛta dharma viparyayavati dṛṣṭānte virodhaḥ syāt viruddhe ca dṛṣṭānte yadi pakṣa dharmasya vṛttiḥ ananya sādhāraṇā prasādhyate viruddha s tadā hetv ābhāsaḥ sādhāraṇāyām aprasādhite vā tad vṛtti niyame anaikāntikaḥ avṛttau vā asādhāraṇaḥ viruddha dṛṣṭāntā vṛttau viparyaya vṛttau ca hetoḥ na kaścid hetu doṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ ca pratijñayā iti ced na tad api saṃśaya hetutva anativṛtteḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ hi pratijñāyāḥ sādharmye doṣaḥ na vaidharmye abhimata tvāt sādharmya dṛṣṭānte ca viparīta dharmavati vastutas sādhyā avyabhicāre api hetoḥ na avyabhicāra dharmatā śakyā darśayitum iti na apradarśita avinā abhāva sambaddhāt hetoḥ niścayaḥ tad na pratijñayā dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ hetv ābhāsān ativartate ubhayathā api doṣaḥ astu iti ced na na hetu doṣasya prāk prasaṅgena parājitasya doṣa antara anapekṣaṇāt viśeṣeṇa sādhana avayava anukrama niyama vādina udāharaṇa sādharmyam hetu lakṣaṇam viruddhe dṛṣṭānte na sambhavati iti prāk prayuktasya hetoḥ doṣeṇa parājaya iti na uttara dṛṣṭānta apekṣayā virodhaḥ cintām arhati hetoḥ api dṛṣṭānta virodhe asādhāraṇa tvam viruddha tvam vā vaidharmye yadi vṛttiḥ syāt pramāṇa virodhe tu hetoḥ yathā na dahanaḥ agniḥ śaityāt iti ādi hi asiddhaḥ hetv ābhāsaḥ pratijñāyāḥ pramāṇa virodhaḥ sva vacana virodhena vyākhyāta iti sarva ete sādhana virodhā hetv ābhāseṣu eva antarbhavanti iti hetv ābhāsa vacanena eva uktāḥ yad tu viruddham uttaram para pakṣe sva siddhena gaḥtva ādinā anaikāntika codanā iti tad asambaddham eva yadi hi sva siddhena gaḥtva ādinā parasya vyabhicāra siddhim ākāṅkṣeta tasya tad sva pakṣa viruddham na abhimatam iti virodha yujyeta sa hi svayam pratipanne gaḥ tve hetu vṛtteḥ saṃśayānaḥ apratipattim ātmanaḥ tathā khyāpayati sa ca hetuḥ sati asati gaḥ tve aprasādhita sādhana sāmarthyaḥ saṃśaya hetu tvāt anaikāntika eva prasādhite tu sāmarthye gaḥ tve avṛttyā hetoḥ na saṃśaya eva sarva saṃśaya prakārāṇām parihāreṇa samarthanāt etena sva pakṣa anapekṣa hetu prayogasya anaikāntika tā vyākhyātā saḥ api sva abhimata nitya gaḥtva vṛttim hetum anitya tve bruvāṇaḥ asamarthita sādhana aṅgatayā saṃśaya hetum eva āha iti yad punar uktam ubhaya pakṣa sampratipannena vastunā anaikāntika codanā iti tatra api avaśyam saṃśaya hetutva mukhena eva anaikāntikaḥ vaktavyaḥ tad asamarthite anyatra api tulyam iti na ubhaya siddha itarayoḥ anaikāntika tvaiḥ viśeṣaḥ yad api uktam dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa hetv ābhāsa pūrvaka tvāt tad abhidhānena eva uktā iti na pṛthak nigraha sthāneṣu uktā iti tad api avayava antara vādinaḥ ayuktam yaḥ avayava antaram dṛṣṭāntam hetoḥ āha tasya na hetv ābhāsa uktyā dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa uktiḥ vyāpyā tad vacanena gamyamānasya tasmāt sādhana antara abhāva prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭānta ābhāsānām hetv ābhāseṣu antarbhāvāt dṛṣṭāntasya api hetau antarbhāva iṣṭaḥ bhavati tathā ca na dṛṣṭāntaḥ pṛthak sādhana avayavaḥ syāt apṛthak vṛtteḥ yaḥ dṛṣṭānta sādhyaḥ artha s tasya hetau antarbhāvāt hetunā eva sādhita iti na dṛṣṭāntasya pṛthak kiṃcid sāmarthyam api ca na kiṃcid pūrva pakṣa vādinaḥ hetv ābhāsa asaṃsparṣe nyāyyam nigraha sthānam asti iti tad sambandhīni sarvāṇi eva hetv ābhāsa vacanena eva uktāni iti na pṛthak vācyāni syuḥ artha antara gamana ādeḥ api hetoḥ asāmarthya eva sambhavāt na hi samarthe hetau sādhye ca siddhe artha antara gamanam kaścid ārabhate asamarthasya mithyā pravṛtteḥ iti pakṣa pratiṣedhe pratijñātā artha apanayanam pratijñā saṃnyāsaḥ yaḥ pratijñātam artham anityaḥ śabda aindriyaka tvāt iti sāmānya vṛttyā hetoḥ vyabhicāra pradarśanena pratiṣedhe kṛte ka evam āha anityaḥ śabda iti parityajati tasya pratijñā saṃnyāsaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam iti atra api yadi udbhāvite api hetoḥ vyabhicāre na sa pakṣam parityajati kim na gṛhyeta nigṛhīta eva hetv ābhāsa abhidhānāt iti ced kim idānīm uttara pratijñā sāṃnyāsa apekṣayā tasya tad eva adyam nigraha sthānam iti kim anyaiḥ aśakya paricchedaiḥ klība pralāpa ceṣṭitaiḥ upanyastaiḥ evam hi atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt pakṣa pratiṣedhe tūṣṇīṃbhavatas tūṣṇīṃbhāvaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam prapalāyamānasya prapalāyi tvam nāma nigraha sthānam iti evam ādy api vācyam syāt tasmāt etad api asambaddham iti aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam icchataḥ hetv antaram nidarśanam eka prakṛti idam vyaktam parimāṇāt mṛt pūrvakāṇām śarāva prabhṛtīnām dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti asya vyabhicāreṇa pratyavasthānam nānā prākṛtīnām eka prakṛtīnām ca dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti evam pratyavasthita āha eka prakṛti samanvaya vikārāṇām parimāṇa darśanāt sukha duḥkha moha samanvitam hi idam sarvam vyaktam parimitam gṛhyate tasya prakṛti antara rūpa samanvaya abhāve sati eka prakṛtika tvam iti tad idam aviśeṣa ukte hetau pratiṣiddhe viśeṣam bruvataḥ hetv antaram bhavati sati ca hetv antara bhāve pūrvasya hetoḥ asādhaka tvāt nigraha sthānam atra api pūrvasya eva hetoḥ anaikāntikasya abhidhānān nigṛhīte hetv antara cintā kva upayujyate yadi prāk sādhana vādī hetum anaikāntikam uktvā datta uttara avasaraḥ tena eva nigṛhyate adatta uttara avasaraḥ hetv antara abhidhāne api na nigraham arhati avirāmāt prakṛtāt arthāt apratibaddha artham artha antaram yathā ukta lakṣaṇe pakṣa pratipakṣa parigrahe hetutaḥ sādhya siddhau prakṛtyāyām kuryāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśa tvāt iti hetuḥ hetuḥ ca nāma hinoteḥ dhātoḥ tu śabde pratyaye kṛd antam padam padam ca nāma ākhyāta upasarga nipātā iti prastutya nāma ādīni vyācaṣṭe idam artha antaram nāma nigraha sthānam abhyupagata artha asaṃgata tvāt iti nyāyyam etad nigraha sthānam pūrva uttara pakṣa vādinoḥ pratipādite doṣe prakṛtam parityajyā sādhana aṅga vacanam adoṣa udbhāvanam ca sādhana vādinaḥ hi upanyasta sādhanasya samarthane kartavye tad akṛtvā aparasya prasaṅgena aprasaṅgena vā atan na antarīyakasya api abhidhānam parājaya sthānam uttara vādinaḥ api doṣa udbhāvana mātrād aparasya upakṣepa iti varṇa krama nirdeśavan nirarthakam yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ jabagaḍa daśa tvāt jhabhan ghaḍha dhaṣavat iti sādhana anupādānān nigṛhyata iti idam api asambaddham na hi varṇa krama nirdeśāt eva iṣṭa artha siddhau ānarthakyam yad eva kiṃcid asādhana aṅgasya vacanam tad eva anarthakam sādhya siddhy upayoginaḥ abhidheyasya abhāvāt niṣprayojana tvāt ca iti prakāra viśeṣa upādānam asambaddham vateḥ upādānāt adoṣa iti ced syāt etad varṇa krama nirdeśavat iti vatiḥ atra upāttar saḥ anyadā api ananurūpam gṛhnati iti adoṣa iti na artha antara ādeḥ nigraha sthānasya avacana prasaṅgāt evam hi tā na pṛthak vācyā nirarthakena eva abhidhānāt na sādhya siddhau anarthakam nirarthakam yasya na eva kaścid arthaḥ tad nirarthakam iṣṭam iti ced yasya kasyacid avādinaḥ api hi nirarthaka abhidhāne kim na nigrahaḥ nigraha nimitta aviśeṣāt na tasya iha aprastāvād iti ced āyātam iha yaḥ nirarthakam bravīti tasya tena eva nigraha iti tad tulyam sarvasya asādhana aṅga vādina iti sa sarvaḥ nirarthaka abhidhāyy anena eva nigraha sthānena nigraha arhaḥ na ca varṇa krama nirdeśaḥ sarvatra nirarthakaḥ kvacid prakaraṇe tasya api arthavat tvāt tasmāt atra eva asya ānarthakyāt nigraha sthāna tvam api ca ati alpam idam ucyate varṇa krama nirdeśaḥ nigraha sthānam iti kapola vādita kakṣa ghaṭṭitakam iti evam ādīnām api vācya tvāt parṣad prativādibhyām tris abhihitam api avijñātam avijñāta artham yad vākyam parṣadā prativādinā ca tris abhihitam na vijñāyate śliṣṭa śabdam apratīta prayogam atidruta uccāritam iti evam ādinā kāraṇena tad avijñāta artham asāmarthya saṃvaraṇāya prayuktam nigraha sthānam iti na idam nirarthakāt bhidyate sa yadi prakṛta artha sambaddham gamakam eva kuryāt na asya asāmarthyam tatra jāḍyāt parṣad ādayaḥ na pratipadyanta iti na vidvān nigraham arhati parṣad prajñām aparikalpya vacanān nigraha arha eva iti ced nyāya vādinaḥ jāḍyāt uktam ajānan kim na prativādī nigṛhyate jāḍyāt parṣad ādeḥ avijñāta pratipādana asāmarthya iti vijetā na syāt na nigraha arhaḥ asambaddha abhidhāne nirarthakam eva iti na pṛthak avijñāta artham nāma nigraha sthānam iti paurvāparya ayogāt apratibaddha artham apārthakam yatra anekasya padasya vākyasya vā paurvāparyeṇa yogaḥ na asti iti asambaddha artha tā gṛhyate tad samudāya arthasya apāyāt apārthakam daśa dāḍima ādi vākyavat idam kila padānām asambandhāt asambaddha varṇān nirarthakāt pṛthak uktam nanu evam asambaddha vākyam api pṛthak vācyam syāt na ubhaya saṃgrahāt apārthakam nirarthakasya api saṃgraha prasaṅgāt evaṃvidhāt ca viśeṣa samāśrayāt pṛthak nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇa pralapane atiprasaṅgaḥ api uktaḥ na ca saṃgraha nirdeśe kiṃcid doṣam paśyāmaḥ prabhede vā guṇa antaram iti yad kiṃcid etad avayava viparyāsa vacanam aprāpta kālam pratijñā ādīnām yathālakṣaṇam artha vaśāt kramaḥ tatra avayavānām viparyayeṇa abhidhānam nigraha sthānam na evam api siddheḥ iti ced na prayoga apeta śabda tulya tvāt yathā gauḥ iti asya padasya arthe goṇī iti prayujyamānam padam kakuda ādimantam artham pratipādyati iti na śabda anvākhyānam vyartham anena padena gaḥ śabdam eva pratipadyate gaḥ śabdāt kakuda ādimantam artham tathā pratijñā ādy avayava viparyayeṇa anupūrvīm pratipadyate ānupūrvyā ca artham iti tathā hi pūrvam karma upādīyate tatas karaṇam mṛt piṇḍa ādikam loka iti tad etad unmattasya unmatta saṃvarṇanam iva prayoga apeta śabdavat etad iti yadi goṇī śabdāt kakuda ādimatī arthe pratītiḥ śabda anvākhyāna prayatnena artham na paśyāmaḥ goṇī śabdasya artha pratipādane asāmarthyāt pratipādaka vyutpatty artham anvākhyānam iti ced nanu goṇī śabdāt api loke pratītiḥ dṛṣṭā satyam dṛṣṭā na tu sākṣāt iti uktam uktam etad na punar yuktam strī śūdrāṇām ubhaya pratīteḥ abhāvāt yaḥ khalu ubhayam vetti śabdam apaśabdam ca sa evam pratipadyate yaḥ tu nakka śabdam mukka śabdam eva vā vetti na nāsā śabdam sa katham apaśabdāt śabdam pratipadya tatas artham pratipadyeta dṛṣṭā ca anubhaya vedinaḥ api pratītiḥ iti na paraṃparayā pratītiḥ arthe asamarthasya śabde api prati iti janana asāmarthyāc ca na hi arthe api vācaka tvam nāma anyat eva tad viṣaya prati iti jananāt apaśabdaḥ ced śabde pratītim janayet artha eva kim na janayati na hi etasya arthāt kiṃcid bhayam paśyāmaḥ yena tam pariharet akṛta samayasya śabde api aprati iti jananāt ca na hi ayam apaśabdaḥ śabde api svabhāvataḥ pratītim janayati adarśanāt samayata eva tu janayet samaya vaśād vartamānaḥ artha eva kim na pravartate evam hi pratipatti paraṃparā pariśramaḥ parihṛtaḥ bhavati viparyaya darśana āt ca śabdāt artham apratipadyamānāḥ apaśabdaiḥ eva bahulam vyutpadyamānā loke dṛśyante iti vyartham śabda anuśāsanam na vyartham saṃskṛta śabda vyutpatty artha tvāt iti ced kaḥ ayam śabdānām saṃskāraḥ na hi eṣām prajñā bāhu śruty ādikam saṃskāram paśyāmaḥ na api eṣām ekāntena śravya tā na api artha pratyāyane kaścid atiśayaḥ na dharma sādhana tā mithyā vṛtti codanebhyaḥ saṃskṛtebhyaḥ api adharma utpatteḥ anyebhyaḥ api viparyaye dharma utpatteḥ śabdasya su prayogāt eva svarga modana ghoṣaṇā vacana mātram na ca evaṃvidhān āgamān ādriyante yukti jñāḥ na ca dāna ādi dharma sādhana codanā śūnya kevala śabda su prayogān naraka pātam iti bruvāṇasya kasyacid mukham vakrībhavati tasmāt na saṃskṛtaḥ nāma kaścid śabdaḥ śiṣṭa prayogaḥ saṃskāra iti ced ke śiṣṭāḥ ye vidita vedya tā ādi guṇa yuktāḥ kaḥ punar eṣām guṇa utkarṣa anapekṣaḥ alīka nirbandhaḥ yad te amūn eva śabdān prayuñjate na aparān na ca atra kaścid śabde parokṣaḥ sākṣī yata idam evam niścinumaḥ prayuñjate nāma śiṣṭāḥ nanu evam vayam guṇa atiśayam apaśyantaḥ saṃskāram keṣāṃcid śabdānām anumanyāmahe tad anvākhyāna yatnam vā guṇa atiśaya abhāvāt veda rakṣa ādikam ca aprayojanam eva atat samaya sthāyinaḥ sati api guṇa atiśaye na karaṇīya eva anvākhyāne yatnaḥ tad svabhāvasya anyatas api siddheḥ prākṛta apabhraṃśa dramiḍa andhra ādi bhāṣāvat na hi pratideśam bhāṣāṇām kiṃcid lakṣaṇam asti atha ca sampradāya vaśāt tā loka s tathā eva pratipadyate tāsām ca prayoga bhraṃśam tathā saṃskṛtānām śabdānām pratītiḥ bhaviṣyati iti jaḍa pravṛttiḥ eva eṣā yā śabdānām lakṣaṇe pravṛttiḥ avayava viparyaye api yadi teṣām vacanānām sambandha pratītiḥ na viparyayaḥ na api artha apratītiḥ sāmarthyāt na hi atra kaścid samayaḥ pratyāyana aviśeṣe api evam eva avayavāḥ prayoktavyā iti sa eva teṣām kramaḥ yathā avasthitebhyaḥ artha pratītiḥ bhavati iti na viparyayāt pratītiḥ tatas ānupūrvī pratipattyā pratītiḥ iti ced na apratīyamāna sambandhebhya ānupūrvī pratipattiḥ yeṣām śabdānām kaścid sambandhaḥ jāyate idam iha sambadhyata iti teṣu vidita sambandheṣu kaḥ kasya pūrvaḥ aparaḥ vā kramaḥ yena krameṇa vyavasthāpyeran sambandha pratipattau sa eva teṣām kramaḥ yaḥ yathā avasthitānām sambandhaḥ pratīyate na hi vākyeṣu padānām krama niyamaḥ kaścid yathā rājñaḥ puruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ rajña iti yāvadbhiḥ padaiḥ artha parisamāptiḥ tadā ekam vākyam yathā devadatta gām ānaya kṛṣṇām iti atra padānām yathākāmam prayoge api na artha pratītau viśeṣa iti kaścid krama abhiniveśaḥ pratipāditam ca pratijñā vacana antareṇa api yathārtham pratītiḥ bhaviṣyati iti pratīyamāna arthasya ca śabdasya prayoge atiprasaṅgaḥ pariśiṣṭeṣu ca sambandham pradarśya dharmiṇi bhāvaḥ pradarśyeta dharmiṇi bhāvam pradarśya sambandhaḥ pradarśyeta iti na niyamaḥ kaścid ubhayathā api prati ity utpatteḥ iti uktam apratīyamāna sambandheṣu ca padeṣu na tebhya ānupūrvyā api pratītiḥ iti na idam apārthakāt bhidyata iti na aprāpta kālam pṛthak vācyam syāt iti hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūnam yasmin vākye pratijñā ādīnām anyatamaḥ avayavaḥ na bhavati tad vākyam hīnam sādhana abhāve sādhyā siddheḥ na pratijñā nyūnam hīnam tad abhāve prati iti bhāvāt iti pratipāditam hīnam eva tad nyūna tāyām api nigrahāt iti aparaḥ yaḥ pratīyamāna artham anarthakam śabdam prayuṅkte sa nigraham arhet na artha upasaṃhitasya abhidhātā iti asamīkṣita abhidhānam etad ata eva ca pratijñāyā na sādhana aṅga bhāva iti hetu udāharaṇa adhikam adhikam ekena kṛta tvāt anyatarasya ānarthakyam iti tad etad niyama abhyupagame veditavyam yatra eka sādhana vākya prayoga pūrva kaḥ vicāraḥ tatra adhika abhidhānam anarthakam iti nigraha sthānam prapañca kathāyām tu na kaścid doṣaḥ niyama abhāvāt iti śabda arthayoḥ punarvacanam punaruktam anyatra anuvādāt śabda punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabda iti artha punaruktam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nirodha dharmakaḥ dhvāna iti atra na śabda punaruktam pṛthak vācyam artha punarukta vacanena eva gata tvāt na hi artha bhede śabda sāmye api kaścid doṣaḥ yathā hasati hasati svāminy uccai rudati atiroditi kṛta parikaram sveda udgāram pradhāvati dhāvati guṇa samuditam doṣa apetam praṇindati nindati dhana lava parikrītam yantram pranṛtyati nṛtyati yathā vā yad yasmin bhavati bhavati na bhavati na bhavati tad tasya kāryam itarat kāraṇam iti gamyamāna artham punarvacanam api punaruktam niyata pada prayoge sādhana vākye yathā pratijñā vacanam iti artha punaruktena eva gata artha tvāt na pṛthak vācyam ayam api niyata sādhana vākya eva doṣaḥ vaktavyaḥ na vistara kathāyām vyācakṣāṇaḥ hi kadācid asamyak śravaṇa pratipatti śaṅkayā sākṣi prabhṛtīnām punar punar brūyāt api na tatra kiṃcid chalam na aviṣaya tvāt iti ced na ayam guruḥ na śiṣya iti na yatnatas pratipāda niyaḥ yena punar punar ucyata iti punarvacane nigraha eva iti ced na sākṣiṇām yatnena pratipādya tvāt tad apratipādane doṣa abhidhānāt pratipādyasya śiṣya tvāt vijigīṣu vāda pratiṣedha tvāt tris abhidhāna vacanāt punarvacana prasaṅge samaya niyama abhāvāt ca na ca idam adhikāt bhidyata iti na pṛthak vācyam viniyata pada prayoge hi sādhana vākye ādhikya doṣa iti punarvacane api gata arthasya ādhikyam eva padasya iti prapañca kathāyām api akathita eka artha sādhana adhikaraṇāyām nānā artha sādhana īpsāyām nānā sādhana īpsāyām vā śrotuḥ hetv ādi bāhulasya punarvacanasya adoṣa tvāt pratīta pratyaya abhāvāt hetv ādi bāhulyam vacana bāhulyam ca sādhana doṣa iti ādhikya punarvacanayoḥ tulya doṣa iti saṃgraha vacanam nyāyyam doṣa abhāvāt eva guṇa abhāvāt evaṃprakārānām bhedānām vacane ca atiprasaṅgāt iti uktam paryāya śabda kalpaḥ hi aparaḥ hetuḥ eka hetu pratipādite viṣaye vartamānaḥ pratipādyasya viśeṣa abhāvāt arthaḥ punar pratipādanān na bhidyate yad punar uktam anuvāde tu apunaruktam śabda abhyāsāt artha viśeṣa upapatteḥ yathā hetv apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam nigamanam iti pratijñāyā eva gamyamāna arthāyāḥ vacanam punarvacanam kim punar asyāḥ punarvacanam iti ayuktam nigamanam vijñātasya parṣadā tris abhihitasya apratyuccāraṇam ananubhāṣaṇam vijñāta vākya arthasya parṣadā prativādinā tris abhihitasya yad apratyuccāraṇam tad ananubhāṣaṇam nāma nigraha sthānam apratyuccārayan kim āśrayam para pakṣa pratiṣedham kuryāt iti uttareṇa avasānān na idam nigraha sthānam iti ced syāt etad uttareṇa guṇa doṣavatā mūḍha amūḍha tvam gamyata iti kim punar uccāritena asti hi kaścid uttare samarthaḥ na pratyuccāraṇe na asau tāvatā nigraham arhet iti na uttara viṣaya aparijñānāt yadi ayam na pratyuccārayati nirviṣayam uttaram prasajyeta atha uttaram bravīti katham na uccārayati tad idam vyāhatam ucyate na uccārayati uttaram ca bravīti iti apratijñāna āt ca na ca idam pratijñāyate pūrvam sarvam uccārayitavyam paścāt uttaram abhidhātavyam iti api tu yathā kathaṃcid uttaram vācyam uttaram ca āśraya abhāve ayuktam iti yuktam apratyuccāraṇam nigraha sthānam iti yadi nāma vādī sva sādhana artha vivaraṇa vyājena prasaṅgāt apara aparam ghoṣayet vivāda āspadam ca jijñāsitam artha mātram uktvā pratijñā ādiṣu artha viśeṣa paraṃparayā aparān arthān upakṣipya kathām vistārayet tad ca sarvam yadā na anuvaktum śaknuyāt kas tasya vivāda āśraya artha mātra uttara vacane sāmarthya vighātaḥ yena vādi vacana ananubhāṣaṇam nigraha sthānam ucyate tasmāt sarvām vādi kathām ananubhāṣamāṇaḥ na uttare asamarthaḥ yad vacana na antarīyakā jijñāsita artha siddhiḥ yathā pakṣa dharma tā vyāpti prasādhana mātram na tatra api prasaṅga antara upakṣepaḥ tad avaśyam sādhana aṅga viṣaya tvāt dūṣaṇena upadarśyata eva tatra api na sarvam prāk anukrameṇa uccāritavyam paścāt dūṣaṇam vācyam dvis uccāraṇa prasaṅgāt dūṣaṇa viṣaya upadarśana arthe anubhāṣaṇe vādi vacana anukrama ghoṣaṇam vyartham iti na kāryam eva dūṣayatā asya ayam doṣa iti na antarīya tvāt pratidoṣa vacanam viṣaya upadarśanam kriyata eva na hi sarva viṣaya upadarśanam kṛtvā yugapad doṣaḥ śakyate abhidhātum pratyartham doṣa bhedāt tasmāt yam padārtham dūṣayati sa eva tad dūṣaṇa viṣaya s tadā pradarśanīyaḥ na aparaḥ tad dūṣaṇe apara upadarśanasya asambhavāt tasmin dūṣite punar anyaḥ arthaḥ apara doṣa viṣaya iti ayam anubhāṣaṇe dūṣaṇe ca nyāyaḥ sakṛt sarva anubhāṣaṇe api doṣa vacana kāle punar viṣayaḥ pradarśanīya eva apradarśite doṣasya vaktum aśakya tvāt tathā ca dvis anubhāṣaṇam kṛtam syāt tatra prathamam sarva anukrama anubhāṣaṇam niṣprayojanam dūṣaṇa vādinā dūṣaṇe vaktavye yad na tatra upayujyate tasya abhidhānam adoṣa udbhāvanam dvis uktiḥ ca iti sakṛt sarva anubhāṣaṇam parājaya adhikaraṇam vācyam tathā astu iti ced syāt etad uktam etad artha antaram nigraha sthānam iti tatra sādhane yatas kutaścid prasaṅga ādinā anāntarīyakā abhidhānam vādinaḥ artha antara gamanam eva iti sa nigrahā arhaḥ na kaścid tad kathita kriyamāṇa prasaṅgaḥ na prasajyate na api tad tasya anubhāṣaṇīyam na ca idam api asmābhiḥ anujñāyate sarvam prāk sakṛt vaktavyam paścāt dūṣaṇam iti kim tu dūṣayatā avaśyam viṣayaḥ darśanīyaḥ anyathā dūṣaṇā vṛtteḥ iti evam tarhi na ananubhāṣaṇam pṛthak nigraha sthānam vācyam apratibhayā gata tvāt uttarasya hi apratipattiḥ apratibhā na ca uttara viṣayam apradarśayan uttaram pratipattum samarthaḥ na hi anākṣipta anuttara pratipattikam ananubhāṣaṇam tena ananubhāṣaṇasya vyāpikāyām apratibhāyām vihitam nigraha sthāna tvam ananubhāṣaṇe labdham eva gavi vihitam iva sāsnā ādimat tvam bāhuleye api tasmāt apratibhā eva nigraha adhikaraṇa tvena vācyā na ananubhāṣaṇam kaś ca ayam samaya niyamas tris abhihitasya ananubhāṣaṇam iti yadi tāvat para pratipādana arthā pravṛttiḥ kim tris abhidhīyeta tathā tathā sa grāhaṇīyaḥ yathā asya pratipattiḥ bhavati atha para upatāpana arthā tadā api kim tris abhidhīyate sākṣiṇām karṇe nivedya prativādī kaṣṭa pratīta druta saṃkṣipta ādibhiḥ upadrotavyaḥ yathā uttara pratipatti vimūḍha s tūṣṇīṃbhavati na hi para upatāpana krame kaścid nyāyaḥ yena kaṣṭa pratīta prayoga druta uccāritāni nivāryante tris abhidhānam vā vidhīyate na ca para upatāpāya santaḥ pravartante śāstrāṇi vā praṇīyante iti adaḥ vaktavyam tasmāt tāvat vaktavyam yāvat anena na gṛhītam na tris eva agrahaṇa sāmarthye prāk eva paricchinna sāmarthyena parihartavyaḥ parān anupratibodhya iti avijñātam ca ajñānam vijñātam parṣadā prativādinā yad avijñātam tad ajñānam nāma nigraha sthānam arthe khalu avijñāte na tasya pratiṣedham brūyāt iti etad api ananubhāṣaṇavat apratibhayā eva gamya tvāt avācyam yathā ananubhāṣaṇe apradarśita viṣaya tvāt uttara pratipattiḥ aśakyā iti anuttara pratipattyā eva nigraha sthāna tvam uttara viṣaya pradarśana prasaṅgam antareṇa anubhāṣaṇasya vaiyarthyāt tathā jñāne api uttara apratipattyā eva nigraha sthāna tvam ajānānaḥ katham uttaram uttara viṣayam ca uttaram brūyāt iti viṣaya ajñānam uttara jñānam ca nigraha sthānam anyathā pratibhāyā nirviṣaya tvāt anavadhārita arthaḥ hi na anubhāṣet ananubhāṣamāṇaḥ viṣayam apradarśya uttaram pratipattum na śaknuyād iti uttaram na pratipadyeta jñāta uttara tad viṣayasya uttara apratipatteḥ asambhavāt ubhayam etad uttara apratipatteḥ kāraṇam iti tad abhāve pratipattiḥ bhavati eva iti tayoḥ pṛthak vacane apratibhāyāḥ kaḥ viṣaya iti vaktavyam nirviṣaya tvāt avācyā eva syāt na uttara ajñānam ajñānam kim tarhi viṣaya ajñānam ajñāte hi viṣaye uttara ajñānāt tad na pratipadyeta iti asti viṣayaḥ apratibhāyā iti ced evam tarhi ananubhāṣaṇam nirviṣayam ajñānena ākṣepāt na hi viṣayam samyak pratipadyamānaḥ kaścid na anubhāṣeta iti na ananubhāṣaṇam pṛthak vācyam uttara ajñānasya ca ākṣepāt viṣaya ajñānena uttara ajñānam api ākṣiptam eva na hi viṣayam ajānan uttaram jānāti iti na eva apratibhāyā viṣayaḥ asti jñāte api viṣaye punar uttara ajñānam apratibhāyā viṣaya iti ced evam tarhi viṣaya uttara ajñānayoḥ api prabhedān nigraha sthāna antarāṇi vācyāni yathā ajñānasya viṣaya ajñānam uttara ajñānam iti prabhedāt asati api guṇa atiśaye nigraha sthāna antara vyavasthā kriyate tathā ajñānayoḥ api sarvā jñāna ardha ajñānam iti ādi prabhedān nigraha sthāna antarāṇi kim na ucyante na ca ubhayasya api ajñānasya saṃgraha vacane kaścid doṣaḥ guṇa s tu syāt iti saṃgraha vacanam nyāyyam tasmāt ananubhāṣaṇa jñānayoḥ apratibhā viṣaya tvān na pṛthak vacanam api ca na pūrva uttara vādinaḥ hetv ābhāsā pratibhābhyām anyan nigraha sthānam nyāyyam asti tad ubhaya vacanena eva sarvam uktam iti tad ubhaya ākṣipteṣu prabhedeṣu guṇa atiśayam antareṇa vacana ādeḥ atiprasaṅgāt vyarthaḥ prapañca iti uttarasya apratipattiḥ apratibhā para pakṣa pratiṣedha uttaram yadā na pratipadyate tadā nigṛhītaḥ vaktavyaḥ sādhana vacana anantaram prativiṣayam uttare vyartham tad ajñāna krama ghoṣaṇa śloke pāṭha ādinā kālam gamayan kartavya apratipattyā nigraha arha iti nyāyyam nigraha sthānam iti kārya vyāsaṅgāt kathā vicchedaḥ vikṣepaḥ yad kiṃcid kartavyam vyāsajya kathām vicchinatti idam me karaṇīyam parihīyate asmin avasite paścāt kariṣyāmi pratiśyāya kalā me kaṇṭham kṣiṇoti evam ādinā kathām vicchinatti sa vikṣepaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam ekatara nigraha antāyām kathāyām svayam eva kathā antam pratipadyata iti idam api yadi pūrva pakṣa vādī kuryāt vyāja upakṣepa mātreṇa na punar bhūtasya tathāvidha kathā uparodhinaḥ kāryasya bhāve tasya sva sādhana asāmarthya paricchedāt eva vikṣepaḥ syāt tathā ca idam artha antara gamana eva antar bhavet asamartha sādhana abhidhānāt hetv ābhāseṣu vā prakṛta sādhana asambaddha pratipatteḥ ca nirarthaka apārthakābhyām na bhidyate atiprasaṅgaḥ ca evaṃprakārāṇām asambaddha sādhana vākya pratipatti bhedānām pṛthak nigraha sthāna vyavasthāpane proktaḥ atha uttara pakṣa vādy evam vikṣipet tasya api sādhana anantaram uttare pratipattavye tad apratipattyā vikṣepa pratipattiḥ apratibhāyām artha antare vā antarbhavati nanu na avaśyam sādhana dūṣaṇābhyām eva sarvasya pratipattiḥ yena sarvā vādi prativādinoḥ na asamyak pratipattiḥ hetv ābhāseṣu apratibhāyām vā antar bhavet bhavati hi anibaddhena api kathā prapañcena vivāda iti na asambhavāt ekatra adhikaraṇe viruddha abhyupagamaya ūḥ vivādaḥ syāt aviruddha abhyupagamaya ūḥ anabhyupagamayoḥ vā vivādā abhāvāt tatra avaśyam ekasya prāk vacana pravṛttiḥ yugapad pravṛttau paraspara vacana śravaṇa avadhāraṇa uttarāṇām asambhavena pravṛtti vaiphalyāt svastha ātmanām apravṛtteḥ tena ca sva upagama upanyāse avaśyam sādhanam vaktavyam anyathā pareṣām apratipatteḥ apareṇa ca tad sambandhi dūṣaṇam ubhayoḥ asamyak pratipattau hetv ābhāsa apratibhayoḥ prasaṅga iti sarvaḥ nyāya pravṛttaḥ pūrva uttara pakṣa upanyāsaḥ dvayam na atipatati etena eva vitaṇḍā pratyukta abhyupagama abhāve vivāda abhāvāt yadā tarhi abhyupagamya vādam viphala tayā na kiṃcid vakti anyat vā yad kiṃcid pralapati tadā katham hetv ābhāsa antarbhāvaḥ asamarthita sādhana abhidhāna evam uktam anabhidhāna anya abhidhānayoḥ api parājaya eva iti uktam abhyupagamya vādam asādhana aṅga vacanāt etena adhikasya punaruktasya ca pratijñā ādeḥ vacanasya ca nigraha sthāna tvam vyākhyātam tad api hi pratipādita artha viparyaya tvāt sādhana sāmarthya anabhidhānam apratīta pratyaya tayā lakṣaṇāt sādhanasya asādhana aṅga vacanam iti nigraha sthānam iti sva pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā yaḥ pareṇa coditam doṣam anuddhṛtya bhavataḥ api ayam doṣa iti bravīti yathā bhavān cauraḥ puruṣa tvāt iti ukte sa tam pratibrūyāt bhavān api iti sa sva pakṣe doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣe tam doṣam prasañjayan para matam anujānāti iti mata anujñā nigraha sthānam iti atra api yadi puruṣa tvāt cauraḥ bhavān api syāt na ca bhavatā ātmā evam iṣṭaḥ tasmāt na ayam caurya hetuḥ iti yadi ayam abhiprāyaḥ tadā na kaścid doṣaḥ anabhimate tad ātmani caura tvena hetu darśanena dūṣaṇāt prasaṅgam antareṇa āñjasena eva kim na vyabhicārita iti ced yad kiṃcid etad santi hi evaṃprakārā api vyavahārā loka iti atha tad upakṣepam abhyupagacchati eva tadā api asau uttara apratipattyā eva tad sādhane nigraha arhaḥ na aparatra sva doṣa upakṣepāt tad sādhana nirdoṣa tāyām hi tad abhyupagama eva uttara apratipattiḥ iti tāvatā eva pūrvam āpanna nigrahasya para doṣa upakṣepasya anapekṣaṇīya tvāt iti nigraha prāptasya anigrahaḥ paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam paryanuyojyaḥ nāma nigraha upapattyā codanīyaḥ tasya upekṣaṇam nigraha prāptaḥ asi iti ananuyogaḥ etad ca kasya parājaya iti anuyuktayā parṣadā vaktavyam na khalu nigraha prāptaḥ sva kaupīnam vivṛṇuyāt iti atra api yadi sādhana vādinam nigraha prāptam uttara vādī na paryanuyuṅkte apratibhā eva asya uttara apratipatteḥ iti na paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam pṛthak nigraha sthānam nyāya cintāyām punar na dvayoḥ ekasya api atra jaya parājayau sādhana ābhāsena artha apratipādanāt bhūta doṣa anabhidhānāt ca atha kaṃcid doṣam udbhāvayati kaṃcid na na tadā nigraham arhati uttara pratipatteḥ arhati eva sarvasya sataḥ doṣasya anudbhāvanād iti ced na santa iti kṛtvā sarve doṣā avaśyam vaktavyā avacane vā nigrahaḥ ekena api tad sādhana vighātāt eka sādhana vacanavat yathā ekasya artha asya aneka sādhana sadbhāve api ekena eva tad siddheḥ na sarva upādānam iti na doṣam udbhāvayan eva aparasya anudbhāvanān nigraha arhaḥ atha pūrva pakṣa vādī uttara pakṣa vādinam nigraha prāptam na nigṛhṇāti tadā tayoḥ nyāyena na ekasya api pūrvavaj jaya parājayau doṣa ābhāsam brūvānam uttara vādinam sva sādhanāt anutsārayataḥ asamarthita sādhana aṅga tvān na jayaḥ vādinaḥ sarva doṣa asambhava pradarśanena sādhana aṅga samarthanāt na api uttara vādinaḥ bhūta doṣa apratipādanāt tasmāt evam api na paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam nāma parājaya adhikaraṇam iti asthāne nigraha sthāna anuyogaḥ niranuyojya anuyogaḥ nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya mithyā avasāyāt anigraha sthāne nigṛhītaḥ asi iti bruvan niranuyojya anuyogān nigṛhītaḥ vaktavyaḥ atra api yadi tad sādhana vādinam abhūtaiḥ doṣaiḥ uttara vādy abhiyuñjīta saḥ asthāne nirdoṣe nigraha sthānasya abhiyokta udbhāvayitā na bhavati tathā ca bhūta doṣa udbhāvana lakṣaṇasya uttarasya apratipatteḥ itareṇa uttara ābhāsa tve pratipādite apratibhayā eva nigṛhīta iti na idam atas nigraha sthāna antaram atha uttara vādinam bhūtam sādhana doṣam udbhāvayantam aparaḥ doṣa ābhāsa vacanena abhiyuñjīta tasya tena bhūta doṣa tve pratipādite sādhana ābhāsa vacanena eva nigṛhīta iti evam api na idam hetv ābhāsebhyaḥ bhidyate avaśyam hi viṣaya antara vyāpti artham hetv ābhāsā nigraha sthāna tvena vaktavyāḥ tad uktau apara uktiḥ anarthakā iti siddhāntam abhyupetyā niyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ kasyacid arthasya tathā abhāvam pratijñāya pratijñātā artha viparyayāt kathā prasaṅgam kurvataḥ apasiddhāntaḥ vijñeyaḥ yathā na sataḥ vināśaḥ na asad utpadyata iti siddhāntam abhyupetya pakṣam avasthāpayati ekā prakṛtiḥ vyaktasya vikārāṇām anvaya darśanāt mṛd anvayānām śarāva ādīnām dṛṣṭam eka prakṛtika tvam tathā ca ayam vyakta bhedas sukha duḥkha moha samanvitaḥ gṛhyate tad sukha ādibhiḥ eka prakṛtiḥ iti sa evam uktavān paryanuyujyate atha prakṛtiḥ vikāra iti katham lakṣayitavyam iti yasya avasthitasya dharma antara nivṛttau dharma antaram pravartate sā prakṛtiḥ yad tad dharma antaram sa vikāra iti saḥ ayam prakṛta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt kathām prasañjayati pratijñātam khalu anena na asad āvirbhavati na sat tirobhavati iti sat asatā uḥ ca tirobhāva āvirbhāvau antareṇa na kasyacid pravṛtty uparamaḥ pravṛttiḥ vā iti evam pratyavasthitaḥ yadi sata ātma hānam asataḥ ca ātma lābham abhyupaiti apasiddhāntaḥ bhavati atha na abhyupaiti pakṣaḥ asya na sidhyati iti iha api na kaścid aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ yad tena upagatan na asad utpadyate na sat vinaśyati iti tasya samarthanāya idam uktam eka prakṛtikam idam vyaktam anvaya darśanāt iti tatra ekā prakṛtiḥ sukha duḥkha mohaḥ tad avibhakta yonikam idam vyaktam tad anvaya darśanāt vyaktasya tad svabhāva tā bheda upalabdheḥ iti sukha ādīnām utpatti vināśa abhyupagama abhāvāt sarvasya tad ātmakasya na utpatti vināśau iti siddham bhavati atra tad uktasya hetoḥ doṣam anudbhāvya vikāra prakṛti lakṣaṇam pṛcchan svayam ayam prakṛta asambandhena aniyamāt kathām pravartayati tatra idam syāt vācyam vyaktam nāma pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmakam na tathā sukha ādayaḥ vyaktasya sukha ādy anvaye sukha ādi svabhāvatāyām pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmatā lakṣaṇam avahīyata iti na tad rahita sukha ādi svabhāva tā vyakta lakṣaṇa virodhāt iti sukha ādy anvaya darśanāt iti asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti evam hi tasya sādhana doṣa udbhāvanena pakṣaḥ dūṣitaḥ bhavati saḥ anupasaṃhṛtya sādhana doṣam kathām pratānayan sva doṣam paratra upakṣipati ayam eva doṣaḥ anena prakaraṇena ucyata iti ced eṣa naimittikāṇām viṣayaḥ na lokaḥ śabdaiḥ apratipāditam artham pratipattum samartha iti sa eva ayam bhaṇḍālekhya nyāyaḥ atra api yathā uktena nyāyena pūrvakasya asādhana aṅgasya asiddhasya hetoḥ abhidhānāt eva nigrahaḥ na api aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgāt iti idam api hetv ābhāseṣu antar bhāvān na pṛthak vācyam hetv ābhāsāḥ ca yathā uktāḥ hetv ābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānāni kim punar lakṣaṇa antara yogāt hetv ābhāsā nigraha sthāna bhāvam āpadyante yathā pramāṇāni prameya tvam iti ata āha yathā ukta hetv ābhāsa lakṣaṇena eva nigraha sthāna bhāva iti atra api yathā uktam kṛtvā cintyam eva kim te yathālakṣita prabhedāḥ tathā eva āhosvit anyathā iti tad tu cintyamānam iha atiprasajyata iti na pratanyate hetv ābhāsāḥ ca yathānyāyam nigraha sthānam iti etāvat mātram iṣṭam iti loke avidyā timira paṭala ullekhanaḥ tadtva dṛṣṭeḥ vāda nyāyaḥ para hita rataiḥ eṣa sadbhiḥ praṇītaḥ tadtva ālokam timirayati tam durvidagdhaḥ janaḥ ayam tasmāt yatnaḥ kṛta iha mayā tad samujjvālanāya vāda nyāyaḥ nāma prakaraṇam samāptam
